لِي مِنْهَا مَخْرَجًا. وَقَالَ هِلَالُ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، إِنِّي قَدْ أَرَى مَا اشْتَدَّ عَلَيْكَ مِمَّا جِئْتُ بِهِ، وَاللَّهُ يَعْلَمُ إِنِّي لَصَادِقٌ. فَوَاللَّهِ إِنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ يُرِيدُ أَنْ يَأْمُرَ بِضَرْبِهِ، إِذْ أَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ عَلَى رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ الْوَحْيَ -وَكَانَ إِذَا نَزَلَ عَلَيْهِ الْوَحْيُ عَرَفُوا ذَلِكَ، فِي تَرَبُّد وَجْهِهِ . يَعْنِي: فَأَمْسَكُوا عَنْهُ حَتَّى فَرَغَ مِنَ الْوَحْيِ -فَنَزَلَتْ: ﴿وَالَّذِينَ يَرْمُونَ أَزْوَاجَهُمْ وَلَمْ يَكُنْ لَهُمْ شُهَدَاءُ إِلا أَنْفُسُهُمْ فَشَهَادَةُ أَحَدِهِمْ﴾ الْآيَةَ، فَسُرّي عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ، فَقَالَ: "أَبْشِرْ يَا هِلَالُ، قَدْ جَعَلَ اللَّهُ لَكَ فَرَجًا وَمَخْرَجًا". فَقَالَ هِلَالٌ: قَدْ كُنْتُ أَرْجُو ذَلِكَ مِنْ رَبِّي، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ. فَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "أرسلوا إليها".

فَأَرْسَلُوا إِلَيْهَا، فَجَاءَتْ، فَتَلَاهَا رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ عَلَيْهِمَا، وَذَكَّرَهُمَا وَأَخْبَرَهُمَا أَنَّ عذابَ الْآخِرَةِ أَشَدُّ مِنْ عَذَابِ الدُّنْيَا. فَقَالَ هِلَالٌ: وَاللَّهِ -يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ -لَقَدْ صَدَقتُ عَلَيْهَا. فَقَالَتْ: كَذَبَ. فَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "لَاعِنُوا بَيْنَهُمَا". فَقِيلَ لِهِلَالٍ: اشْهَدْ. فَشَهِدَ أَرْبَعَ شَهَادَاتٍ بِاللَّهِ إِنَّهُ لِمَنَ الصَّادِقِينَ، فَلَمَّا كَانَ فِي الْخَامِسَةِ قِيلَ لَهُ: يَا هِلَالُ، اتَّقِ اللَّهَ، فَإِنَّ عَذَابَ الدُّنْيَا أهونُ مِنْ عَذَابِ الْآخِرَةِ، وَإِنَّ هَذِهِ الموجبةُ الَّتِي تُوجِبُ عَلَيْكَ الْعَذَابَ. فَقَالَ: وَاللَّهِ لَا يُعَذِّبُنِي اللَّهُ عَلَيْهَا، كَمَا لَمْ يَجْلِدْنِي عَلَيْهَا. فَشَهِدَ فِي الْخَامِسَةِ أَنَّ لَعْنَةَ اللَّهِ عَلَيْهِ إِنْ كَانَ مِنَ الْكَاذِبِينَ. ثُمَّ قِيلَ [لَهَا: اشْهَدِي أَرْبَعَ شَهَادَاتٍ بِاللَّهِ إِنَّهُ لِمَنَ الْكَاذِبِينَ، فَلَمَّا كَانَتِ الْخَامِسَةُ قِيلَ] لَهَا: اتَّقِي اللَّهَ، فَإِنَّ عَذَابَ الدُّنْيَا أَهْوَنُ مِنْ عَذَابِ الْآخِرَةِ، وإن هذه الموجبةُ التي توجب عليك العذاب. فَتَلَكَّأَتْ سَاعَةً، ثُمَّ قَالَتْ: وَاللَّهِ لَا أَفْضَحُ قَوْمِي فَشَهِدَتْ فِي الْخَامِسَةِ أَنَّ غَضَبَ اللَّهِ عَلَيْهَا إِنْ كَانَ مِنَ الصَّادِقِينَ. فَفَرَّقَ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ بَيْنَهُمَا، وَقَضَى أَلَّا يُدْعَى وَلَدُهَا لِأَبٍ وَلَا يُرْمَى وَلَدُهَا، وَمَنْ رَمَاهَا أَوْ رَمَى وَلَدَهَا فَعَلَيْهِ الْحَدُّ، وَقَضَى أَلَّا [بَيْتَ لَهَا عَلَيْهِ وَلَا] قُوتَ لَهَا، مِنْ أَجْلِ أَنَّهُمَا يَتَفَرَّقَانِ مِنْ غَيْرِ طَلَاقٍ، وَلَا مُتَوَفى عَنْهَا. وَقَالَ: "إِنْ جَاءَتْ بِهِ أصَيْهِب أرَيسح حَمْش السَّاقِينَ فَهُوَ لِهِلَالٍ، وَإِنْ جَاءَتْ بِهِ أَوْرَقَ جَعدًا جَمَاليًّا خَدلَّج السَّاقَيْنِ سَابِغَ الْأَلْيَتَيْنِ، فَهُوَ الَّذِي رُمِيَتْ بِهِ" فَجَاءَتْ بِهِ أَوْرَقَ جَعْدًا جَمَالِيًّا خَدَلَّجَ السَّاقَيْنِ سَابِغَ الْأَلْيَتَيْنِ، فَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "لَوْلَا الْأَيْمَانُ لَكَانَ لِي وَلَهَا شَأْنٌ".

قَالَ عِكْرِمَةُ: فَكَانَ بَعْدَ ذَلِكَ أَمِيرًا عَلَى مِصْرَ، وَكَانَ يُدْعَى لِأُمِّهِ وَلَا يُدْعَى لِأَبٍ.

وَرَوَاهُ أَبُو دَاوُدَ عَنِ الْحَسَنِ بْنِ عَلِيٍّ، عَنْ يَزِيدَ بْنِ هَارُونَ، بِهِ نَحْوَهُ مُخْتَصَرًا .

وَلِهَذَا الْحَدِيثِ شَوَاهِدُ كَثِيرَةٌ فِي الصِّحَاحِ وَغَيْرِهَا مِنْ وُجُوهٍ كَثِيرَةٍ. فَمِنْهَا مَا قَالَ الْبُخَارِيُّ: حَدَّثَنِي مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ بَشَّار، حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ أَبِي عَدِيّ، عَنْ هِشَامِ بْنِ حَسَّانَ، حَدَّثَنِي عِكْرِمَة، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ؛ أَنَّ هِلَالَ بْنَ أُمَيَّةَ قَذَفَ امْرَأَتَهُ عِنْدَ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ بشَرِيك بْنِ سَحْماء، فَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: " الْبَيِّنَةَ أَوْ حَدُّ فِي ظَهْرِكَ" فَقَالَ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، إذا أري أَحَدُنَا عَلَى امْرَأَتِهِ رَجُلًا ينطلقُ يَلْتَمِسُ الْبَيِّنَةَ؟ فَجَعَلَ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ يَقُولُ: "الْبَيِّنَةُ وَإِلَّا حَدٌّ فِي ظَهْرِكَ". فَقَالَ هِلَالٌ: وَالَّذِي بَعَثَكَ بِالْحَقِّ إِنِّي لِصَادِقٌ، وَلَيُنْزِلَنَّ اللَّهُ مَا يُبرئ ظَهْرِي مِنَ الْحَدِّ. فَنَزَلَ جِبْرِيلُ، وَأَنْزَلَ عَلَيْهِ: ﴿وَالَّذِينَ يَرْمُونَ أَزْوَاجَهُمْ﴾ ، فَقَرَأَ حَتَّى بَلَغَ: ﴿إِنْ كَانَ مِنَ الصَّادِقِينَ﴾ فَانْصَرَفَ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ فَأَرْسَلَ إِلَيْهِمَا، فَجَاءَ هِلَالٌ فَشَهِدَ، وَالنَّبِيُّ ﷺ يَقُولُ: "اللَّهُ يَشْهَدُ أَنَّ أَحَدَكُمَا كَاذِبٌ، فَهَلْ مِنْكُمَا تَائِبٌ"؟ ثُمَّ قَامَتْ فَشَهِدَتْ، فَلَمَّا كَانَتْ عِنْدَ الْخَامِسَةِ وَقَّفُوها وَقَالُوا: إِنَّهَا مُوجبة. قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: فَتَلَكَّأَتْ وَنَكَصَتْ حَتَّى ظَنَنَّا أَنَّهَا تَرْجِعُ، ثُمَّ قَالَتْ: لَا أَفْضَحُ قَوْمِي سَائِرَ الْيَوْمِ. فَمَضَتْ، فَقَالَ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ: "أبْصِرُوها، فَإِنْ جَاءَتْ بِهِ أكحلَ الْعَيْنَيْنِ، سَابِغَ الْأَلْيَتَيْنِ، خَدَلَّج السَّاقَيْنِ، فَهُوَ لشَرِيك بْنِ سَحْمَاءَ". فَجَاءَتْ بِهِ كَذَلِكَ، فَقَالَ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ: "لَوْلَا مَا مَضَى مِنْ كتاب الله، لكان لي ولها شأن".

انْفَرَدَ بِهِ الْبُخَارِيُّ مِنْ هَذَا الْوَجْهِ وَقَدْ رَوَاهُ مِنْ غَيْرِ وَجْهٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ وَغَيْرِهِ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَحْمَدُ بْنُ مَنْصُورٍ الزِّيَادَيُّ حَدَّثَنَا يُونُسُ بْنُ مُحَمَّدٍ، حَدَّثَنَا صَالِحٌ -وَهُوَ ابْنُ عُمَرَ -حَدَّثَنَا عَاصِمٌ -يَعْنِي: ابْنَ كُلَيْب -، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، حَدَّثَنِي ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: جَاءَ رَجُلٌ إِلَى رَسُولِ اللَّهِ، فَرَمَى امْرَأَتَهُ بِرَجُلٍ، فَكَرِهَ ذَلِكَ رسولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ، فَلَمْ يَزَلْ يُرَدّده حَتَّى أَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ: ﴿وَالَّذِينَ يَرْمُونَ أَزْوَاجَهُمْ وَلَمْ يَكُنْ لَهُمْ شُهَدَاءُ [إِلا أَنْفُسُهُمْ] ﴾ [فَقَرَأَ] حَتَّى فَرَغَ مِنَ الْآيَتَيْنِ، فَأَرْسَلَ إِلَيْهِمَا فَدَعَاهُمَا، فَقَالَ: "إِنَّ اللَّهَ، عَزّ وَجَلَّ، قَدْ أَنْزَلَ فِيكُمَا". فَدَعَا الرَّجُلَ فَقَرَأَ عَلَيْهِ، فَشَهِدَ أَرْبَعَ شَهَادَاتٍ بِاللَّهِ إِنَّهُ لِمَنَ الصَّادِقِينَ. ثُمَّ أَمَرَ بِهِ فَأُمْسِكَ عَلَى فِيهِ فَوَعْظَهُ، فَقَالَ لَهُ:"كُلُّ شَيْءٍ أَهْوَنُ عَلَيْهِ مِنْ لَعْنَةِ اللَّهِ". ثُمَّ أَرْسَلَهُ فَقَالَ: ﴿لَعْنتَ اللَّهِ عَلَيْهِ إِنْ كَانَ مِنَ الْكَاذِبِينَ﴾ ثُمَّ دَعَاهَا بِهَا، فَقَرَأَ عَلَيْهَا، فَشَهِدَتْ أَرْبَعَ شَهَادَاتٍ بِاللَّهِ إِنَّهُ لِمَنَ الْكَاذِبِينَ، ثُمَّ أَمَرَ بِهَا فَأُمْسِكَ عَلَى فِيهَا فَوَعَظَهَا، وَقَالَ: "وَيْحَكِ. كُلُّ شَيْءٍ أَهْوَنُ مِنْ غَضَبِ اللَّهِ". ثُمَّ أَرْسَلَهَا، فَقَالَتْ: ﴿غَضَبَ اللَّهِ عَلَيْهَا إِنْ كَانَ مِنَ الصَّادِقِينَ﴾ فَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "أَمَا وَاللَّهِ لَأَقْضِيَنَّ بَيْنَكُمَا قَضَاءً فَصْلًا". قَالَ: فَوَلَدَتْ، فَمَا رَأَيْتُ مَوْلُودًا بِالْمَدِينَةِ أَكْثَرَ غَاشِيَةً مِنْهُ، فَقَالَ: "إِنْ جَاءَتْ بِهِ لِكَذَا وَكَذَا فَهُوَ كَذَا، وَإِنْ جَاءَتْ بِهِ لِكَذَا وَكَذَا فَهُوَ لِكَذَا". فَجَاءَتْ بِهِ يُشَبِهُ الَّذِي قُذفت بِهِ.

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا يَحْيَى بْنُ سَعِيدٍ، حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الْمَلِكِ بْنُ أَبِي سُلَيْمَانَ قَالَ: سَمِعْتُ سَعِيدَ بْنَ جُبَير قَالَ: سُئلْتُ عَنِ الْمُتَلَاعِنَيْنِ أَيُفَرَّقُ بَيْنَهُمَا -فِي إِمَارَةِ ابْنِ الزُّبَيْرِ؟ فَمَا دَرَيتُ مَا أَقُولُ، فَقُمْتُ مِنْ مَكَانِي إِلَى مَنْزِلِ ابْنِ عُمَرَ فقلتُ: أَبَا عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ، الْمُتَلَاعِنَانِ أَيُفَرَّقُ بَيْنَهُمَا؟ فَقَالَ: سُبْحَانَ اللَّهِ، إِنَّ أَوَّلَ مَنْ سَأَلَ عَنْ ذَلِكَ فَلَانُ بْنُ فُلَانٍ فَقَالَ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، أَرَأَيْتَ الرَّجُلَ يَرَى امْرَأَتَهُ عَلَى فَاحِشَةٍ فَإِنْ تَكَلَّم تَكَلَّمَ بِأَمْرٍ عَظِيمٍ، وَإِنْ سَكَتَ سَكَتَ عَلَى مِثْلِ ذَلِكَ. فَسَكَتَ فَلَمْ يُجِبْهُ، فَلَمَّا كَانَ بَعْدَ ذَلِكَ أَتَاهُ فَقَالَ: الَّذِي سَأَلْتُكَ عَنْهُ قَدِ ابتُليت بِهِ. فَأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ هَذِهِ الْآيَاتِ فِي سُورَةِ النُّورِ: ﴿وَالَّذِينَ يَرْمُونَ أَزْوَاجَهُمْ﴾ حَتَّى بَلَغَ: ﴿أَنَّ غَضَبَ اللَّهِ عَلَيْهَا إِنْ كَانَ مِنَ الصَّادِقِينَ﴾ . فَبَدَأَ بِالرَّجُلِ فَوَعَظَهُ وذكَّره، وَأَخْبَرَهُ إن عذاب الدنيا أهونُ من عذاب الآخرة، فَقَالَ: وَالَّذِي بَعَثَكَ بِالْحَقِّ مَا كَذَبْتُك. ثُمَّ ثَنَّى بِالْمَرْأَةِ فَوَعَظَهَا وذَكَّرها، وَأَخْبَرَهَا أَنَّ عَذَابَ الدُّنْيَا أَهْوَنُ مِنْ عَذَابِ الْآخِرَةِ، فَقَالَتْ: وَالَّذِي بَعَثَكَ بِالْحَقِّ إِنَّهُ لَكَاذِبٌ. قَالَ: فَبَدَأَ بِالرَّجُلِ، فَشَهِدَ أَرْبَعَ شَهَادَاتٍ بِاللَّهِ إِنَّهُ لِمَنَ الصَّادِقِينَ، وَالْخَامِسَةُ أَنَّ لَعْنَةَ اللَّهِ عَلَيْهِ إِنْ كَانَ مِنَ الْكَاذِبِينَ. ثُمَّ ثَنَّى بِالْمَرْأَةِ فَشَهِدَتْ أَرْبَعَ شهادات بالله إنه لمن الكاذبين، والخامسة أن غَضَبَ اللَّهِ عَلَيْهَا إِنْ كَانَ مِنَ الصَّادِقِينَ، ثُمَّ فَرَّقَ بَيْنَهُمَا.

رَوَاهُ النَّسَائِيُّ فِي التَّفْسِيرِ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ عَبْدِ الْمَلِكِ بْنِ أَبِي سُلَيْمَانَ، بِهِ وَأَخْرَجَاهُ فِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ مِنْ حَدِيثِ سَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْرٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ .

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا يَحْيَى بْنُ حَمَّادٍ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو عَوَانة، عن الأعمش، عن إبراهيم، عن عَلْقَمَةَ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ قَالَ: كنَّا جُلُوسًا عَشِيَّةَ الْجُمُعَةِ فِي الْمَسْجِدِ، فَقَالَ رَجُلٌ مِنَ الْأَنْصَارِ: أَحَدُنَا إِذَا رَأَى مَعَ امْرَأَتِهِ رَجُلًا فَقَتَلَهُ قَتَلْتُمُوهُ، وَإِنْ تَكَلَّمَ جَلَدْتُمُوهُ، وَإِنْ سَكَتَ سَكَتَ عَنْ غَيْظٍ؟ وَاللَّهِ لَئن أَصْبَحْتُ صَالِحًا لَأَسْأَلَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ. قَالَ: فَسَأَلَهُ. فَقَالَ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، إِنَّ أحدنا إذا رأى مع امرأته رجلا فقتله قَتَلْتُمُوهُ، وَإِنْ تَكَلَّمَ جَلَدْتُمُوهُ، وَإِنْ سَكَتَ سَكَتَ عَلَى غَيْظٍ؟ اللَّهُمَّ احْكُمْ. قَالَ: فَأُنْزِلَ آيَةُ اللِّعَانِ، فَكَانَ ذَلِكَ الرَّجُلُ أَوَّلَ مَنِ ابْتُلِيَ بِهِ.

انْفَرَدَ بِإِخْرَاجِهِ مُسْلِمٌ، فَرَوَاهُ مِنْ طُرُق، عَنْ سُلَيْمَانَ بْنِ مِهْران الْأَعْمَشِ، بِهِ .

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ أَيْضًا: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو كَامِلٍ: حَدَّثَنَا إِبْرَاهِيمُ بْنُ سَعْدٍ، حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ شِهَابٍ، عَنْ سَهْلِ بْنِ سَعْدٍ، قَالَ: جَاءَ عُوَيْمر إِلَى عَاصِمِ بْنِ عَدِيّ فَقَالَ: سَلْ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ: أَرَأَيْتَ رَجُلًا وَجَدَ رَجُلًا مَعَ امْرَأَتِهِ فَقَتَلَهُ، أَيُقَتَلُ بِهِ أَمْ كَيْفَ يَصْنَعُ؟ فَسَأَلَ عَاصِمٌ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ، فعابَ رسولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ الْمَسَائِلَ. قَالَ: فَلَقِيَهُ عُوَيمر فَقَالَ: مَا صنعْتَ؟ قَالَ: مَا صَنَعْتُ! إِنَّكَ لَمْ تَأْتِنِي بِخَيْرٍ؛ سَأَلْتُ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ فَعَابَ الْمَسَائِلَ فَقَالَ عُوَيمر: وَاللَّهِ لَآتِيَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ فَلأسألنه. فَأَتَاهُ فَوَجَدَهُ قَدْ أُنْزِلَ عَلَيْهِ فِيهِمَا. قَالَ: فَدَعَا بِهِمَا فَلاعَن بَيْنَهُمَا. قَالَ عُوَيمر: لَئِنِ انطلقتُ بِهَا يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ لَقَدْ كَذَبْتُ عَلَيْهَا. قَالَ: فَفَارَقَهَا قَبْلَ أَنْ يَأْمُرَهُ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ فَصَارَتْ سُنَّةَ الْمُتَلَاعِنِينَ، فَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "أبصروها، فإن جاءت به أَسْحَمَ أَدْعَجَ الْعَيْنَيْنِ عَظِيمَ الْأَلْيَتَيْنِ، فَلَا أَرَاهُ إِلَّا قَدْ صَدَقَ، وَإِنْ جَاءَتْ بِهِ أُحَيْمِرَ كَأَنَّهُ وَحَرَة فَلَا أَرَاهُ إِلَّا كَاذِبًا". فَجَاءَتْ بِهِ عَلَى النَّعْتِ الْمَكْرُوهِ.

أَخْرَجَاهُ فِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ وَبَقِيَّةُ الْجَمَاعَةِ إِلَّا التِّرْمِذِيَّ، مِنْ طُرُقٍ، عَنِ الزُّهْرِيِّ، بِهِ .

وَقَالَ الْحَافِظُ أَبُو بَكْرٍ الْبَزَّارُ: حَدَّثَنَا إِسْحَاقُ بْنُ الضَّيْفِ، حَدَّثَنَا النَّضْرُ بْنُ شُمَيْل، حَدَّثَنَا يُونُسُ بْنُ أَبِي إِسْحَاقَ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنْ زَيْدِ بْنِ يُثَيْع، عَنْ حُذَيْفَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ لِأَبِي بَكْرٍ: "لَوْ رَأَيْتَ مَعَ أُمِّ رُومَانَ رَجُلًا مَا كُنْتَ فَاعِلًا بِهِ؟ قَالَ: كُنْتُ وَاللَّهِ فَاعِلًا بِهِ شرًّا. قَالَ:"فأنتَ يَا عُمَرُ؟ ". قَالَ: كنتُ وَاللَّهِ فَاعِلًا كُنْتُ أَقُولُ: لَعَنَ اللَّهُ الْأَعْجَزَ، وَإِنَّهُ خَبِيثٌ. قَالَ: فَنَزَلَتْ: ﴿وَالَّذِينَ يَرْمُونَ أَزْوَاجَهُمْ وَلَمْ يَكُنْ لَهُمْ شُهَدَاءُ إِلا أَنْفُسُهُمْ﴾

ثُمَّ قَالَ: لَا نَعْلَمُ أَحَدًا أَسْنَدَهُ إِلَّا النَّضر بْنُ شُميْل، عَنْ يُونُسَ بْنِ أَبِي إِسْحَاقَ، ثُمَّ رَوَاهُ مِنْ حَدِيثِ الثَّوْرِيِّ عَنْ [أَبِي] أَبِي إِسْحَاقَ، عَنْ زَيْدِ بْنِ يُثَيْع مُرْسَلًا فَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ .

وَقَالَ الْحَافِظُ أَبُو يَعْلَى: حَدَّثَنَا مُسْلِمُ بْنُ أَبِي مُسْلِمٌ الجَرْمي، حَدَّثَنَا مُخَلَّدُ بْنُ الْحُسَيْنِ، عَنْ هِشَامٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ سِيرِينَ، عَنْ أَنَسِ بْنِ مَالِكٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: لَأَوَّلُ لِعَانٍ كَانَ فِي الْإِسْلَامِ أَنَّ شَرِيكَ بْنَ سَحْمَاء قذَفه هِلَالُ بْنُ أُمَيَّةَ بِامْرَأَتِهِ، فَرَفَعَهُ إِلَى رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ، فَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ:"أَرْبَعَةَ شُهُودٍ وَإِلَّا فَحَدٌّ فِي ظَهْرِكَ"، فَقَالَ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، إِنَّ اللَّهَ يَعْلَمُ إِنِّي لَصَادِقٌ، وَلَيُنْزِلَنَّ اللَّهُ عَلَيْكَ مَا يُبَرِّئُ بِهِ ظَهْرِي مِنَ الْجَلْدِ. فَأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ آيَةَ اللِّعَانِ: ﴿وَالَّذِينَ يَرْمُونَ أَزْوَاجَهُمْ وَلَمْ يَكُنْ لَهُمْ شُهَدَاءُ إِلا أَنْفُسُهُمْ﴾ إِلَى آخَرِ الْآيَةِ. قَالَ: فَدَعَاهُ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ فَقَالَ: "اشْهَدْ بِاللَّهِ إِنَّكَ لَمِنَ الصَّادِقِينَ فِيمَا رَمَيْتَهَا بِهِ مِنَ الزِّنَى" فَشَهِدَ بِذَلِكَ أَرْبَعَ شَهَادَاتٍ، ثُمَّ قَالَ لَهُ فِي الْخَامِسَةِ: "وَلَعْنَةُ اللَّهِ عَلَيْكَ إِنْ كنتَ مِنَ الْكَاذِبِينَ فِيمَا رَمَيْتَهَا بِهِ مِنَ الزِّنَى"، فَفَعَلَ. ثُمَّ دَعَاهَا رسول الله صلى الله عليه وسلم فقال: "قُومِي فَاشْهَدِي بِاللَّهِ إِنَّهُ لَمِنَ الْكَاذِبِينَ فِيمَا رَمَاكِ بِهِ مِنَ الزِّنَى". فَشَهِدَتْ بِذَلِكَ أَرْبَعَ شَهَادَاتٍ، ثُمَّ قَالَ لَهَا فِي الْخَامِسَةِ: "وغَضب اللَّهِ عَلَيْكِ إِنْ كَانَ مِنَ الصَّادِقِينَ فِيمَا رَمَاكِ بِهِ مِنَ الزِّنَى"، فَقَالَتْ: فَلَمَّا كَانَتِ الرَّابِعَةُ أَوِ الْخَامِسَةُ سَكَتَتْ سَكْتَةً، حَتَّى ظَنُّوا أَنَّهَا سَتَعْتَرِفُ، ثُمَّ قَالَتْ: لَا أَفْضَحُ قَوْمِي سَائِرَ الْيَوْمِ. فَمَضَتْ عَلَى الْقَوْلِ، ففرَّق رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ بَيْنَهُمَا، وَقَالَ: "انْظُرُوهُ، فَإِنْ جَاءَتْ بِهِ جَعْدًا حَمْشَ السَّاقِينَ، فَهُوَ لشَرِيك بْنِ سَحْماء، وَإِنْ جَاءَتْ بِهِ أبيض سبطا فَضيء الْعَيْنَيْنِ فَهُوَ لِهِلَالِ بْنِ أُمَيَّةَ". فَجَاءَتْ بِهِ آدَمَ جَعَدًا حَمْش السَّاقَيْنِ، فَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "لَوْلَا مَا نَزَلَ فِيهِمَا مِنْ كِتَابِ اللَّهِ، لَكَانَ لِي وَلَهَا شأن" .

---

## 24:11 — verse 11

### Translation

These ten verses were all revealed concerning the matter of A'isha, Mother of the Believers, may Allah be pleased with her, when the people of the falsehood and slander among the hypocrites accused her with what they said, which was sheer lying and fabrication. Allah, exalted is He, felt jealous protectiveness on her behalf and on behalf of His Prophet, blessings and peace of Allah be upon him, so He sent down [Allah, mighty and majestic] her declaration of innocence to safeguard the honor of the Messenger, upon him be the most excellent blessings and peace. He said: {Indeed, those who came with the falsehood are a band} that is, a group among you, meaning it was not one person or two but a group. The one who took the lead in this slander was Abdullah ibn Ubayy ibn Salul, the head of the hypocrites, for he was the one who gathered it and stirred it up, until it entered into the minds of some of the Muslims, and they spoke of it, while others among them allowed themselves to repeat it. The matter remained thus for nearly a month, until the Qur'an was revealed. The account of that is found in the authentic hadiths.

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Abd al-Razzaq told us, Ma'mar told us, from al-Zuhri, who said: Sa'id ibn al-Musayyab, Urwa ibn al-Zubayr, Alqama ibn Waqqas, and Ubaydullah ibn Abdullah ibn Utba ibn Mas'ud informed me, concerning the account of A'isha, the wife of the Prophet ﷺ, of when the people of the falsehood said about her what they said, and Allah declared her innocent. Each of them related to me a portion of her account, and some of them retained her account more thoroughly and gave a more precise narration than others, and I have retained from each one of them the account he related to me, and some of their accounts confirm others. They mentioned that A'isha, the wife of the Prophet ﷺ, said:

Whenever the Messenger of Allah ﷺ wished to set out on a journey, he would draw lots among his wives, and whichever of them the lot fell upon, the Messenger of Allah ﷺ would take her with him. A'isha said: He drew lots among us for a campaign he undertook, and the lot fell upon me, so I went out with the Messenger of Allah ﷺ. This was after the verse of the veil had been revealed, so I would be carried in my howdah and set down in it during our journeys. When the Messenger of Allah ﷺ had finished his campaign and was returning, and we drew near to Medina, he gave notice one night that we would depart. I got up when they announced the departure and walked until I had passed beyond the army. When I had finished my business, I came back toward the mount and felt my chest, and found that a necklace of Zafar onyx beads had broken and fallen. So I went back and searched for my necklace, and my search for it delayed me.

The group of men who used to load my howdah came and picked it up and placed it on my camel that I used to ride, thinking that I was inside it. She said: Women in those days were light, not overburdened with flesh or heavily built, for they ate only a little food. So the men did not find the howdah's weight unusual when they lifted and loaded it, and I was a young girl. So they drove on the camel and set off. I found my necklace after the army had already moved on, so I came to their camping place, but there was no one there to call out or answer. So I made my way to the spot where I had been, thinking that the people would miss me and come back for me.

While I was sitting in my place, drowsiness overcame me and I fell asleep. Safwan ibn al-Mu'attal al-Sulami, then al-Dhakwani, had stayed behind the army for the night and had traveled through the early morning, and by morning he was at my resting place. He saw the dark shape of a sleeping person and came to me, and he recognized me when he saw me, for he had seen me before the command of veiling was given. I woke up at his exclamation of "inna lillahi wa inna ilayhi raji'un" when he recognized me, and I covered my face with my outer garment. By Allah, he did not speak a single word to me, nor did I hear a word from him besides his exclamation, until he made his camel kneel down, and he stepped on its foreleg and I mounted it. Then he set off leading me on the camel, until we caught up with the army after they had halted in the intense heat of midday.

Then those who perished did perish concerning my affair, and the one who took the greatest part in it was Abdullah ibn Ubayy ibn Salul. We arrived in Medina, and I fell ill for a month after we arrived, while the people were busy spreading the talk of the people of falsehood, and I was unaware of any of it. What made me suspicious during my illness was that I no longer sensed from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ the same gentleness I used to see from him when I was ill. The Messenger of Allah ﷺ would only come in, greet me, and then say, "How is she?" That made me suspicious, but I did not perceive the evil of it.

Until I went out after I had recovered somewhat, and Umm Mistah went out with me toward al-Manasi, which was our place for relieving ourselves, and we would only go out at night, one night to another, and that was before we had latrines built near our houses. Our custom was like that of the early Arabs in seeking privacy, and we found it distasteful to have latrines built in our houses. So I set out, I and Umm Mistah, who was the daughter of Abu Ruhm ibn al-Muttalib ibn Abd Manaf, whose mother was the daughter of Sakhr ibn Amir, the maternal aunt of Abu Bakr al-Siddiq, and whose son was Mistah ibn Uthatha ibn Abbad ibn al-Muttalib.

I and the daughter of Abu Ruhm were heading back toward my house when we had finished our business, and Umm Mistah stumbled over her cloak and said, "May Mistah perish!" I said to her, "What a bad thing you have said, cursing a man who fought at Badr!" She said, "O you simple one, have you not heard what he said?" I said, "And what did he say?" So she told me what the people of falsehood had said, and my illness increased upon my illness.

When I returned home, the Messenger of Allah ﷺ came in to me, greeted me, and then said, "How is she?" I said, "Will you permit me to go to my parents?" She said: At that time I wanted to verify the news from them. So the Messenger of Allah ﷺ gave me permission, and I came to my parents and said to my mother, "O my mother, what are the people saying?" She said, "O my daughter, take it lightly, for by Allah, rarely is there a beautiful woman married to a man who loves her, and who has co-wives, but that they speak much against her." I said, "Glory be to Allah! Are the people really talking about this?" She said: I wept that night until morning, my tears never ceasing, nor did sleep touch my eyes, and I continued weeping into the morning.

Then the Messenger of Allah ﷺ summoned Ali and Usama ibn Zayd, when the revelation was delayed, to consult them about separating from his wife. As for Usama ibn Zayd, he advised the Messenger of Allah ﷺ according to what he knew of the innocence of his family and according to the affection he held for him in his heart, saying, "O Messenger of Allah, they are your family, and we know nothing but good." As for Ali ibn Abi Talib, he said, "Allah has not placed you in difficulty, and there are many women besides her, but ask the servant girl, and she will tell you the truth."

She said: So the Messenger of Allah ﷺ called Barira and said, "O Barira, have you seen anything that makes you suspicious of A'isha?" Barira said to him, "By Him who sent you with the truth, I have never seen anything about her that I would find fault with, except that she is a young girl who sometimes falls asleep while tending her family's dough, and the household animal comes and eats it."

Then the Messenger of Allah ﷺ stood up and sought redress against Abdullah ibn Ubayy ibn Salul. She said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said, while on the pulpit, "O company of Muslims, who will help me against a man whose harm against my family has reached me? By Allah, I know nothing but good of my family, and they have mentioned a man of whom I know nothing but good, and he never entered my house except with me."

Then Sa'd ibn Mu'adh al-Ansari stood up and said, "I will help you against him, O Messenger of Allah. If he is from the Aws, we will strike off his neck, and if he is from our brothers of the Khazraj, command us, and we will carry out your command." She said: Then Sa'd ibn Ubada stood up, who was the chief of the Khazraj, and he was a righteous man, but zealous partisanship overcame him, and he said to Sa'd ibn Mu'adh, "By the life of Allah, you shall not kill him, and you are not able to kill him." Then Usayd ibn Hudayr stood up, who was the cousin of Sa'd ibn Mu'adh, and said to Sa'd ibn Ubada, "You have lied! By the life of Allah, we will surely kill him, for you are a hypocrite arguing on behalf of the hypocrites."

Then the two tribes, the Aws and the Khazraj, became agitated against each other until they nearly fought, while the Messenger of Allah ﷺ was standing on the pulpit. The Messenger of Allah ﷺ continued to calm them down until they fell silent, and the Messenger of Allah ﷺ fell silent.

She said: I wept that whole day, my tears never ceasing, nor did sleep touch my eyes, and my parents thought that the weeping would split my liver. She said: While the two of them were sitting with me and I was weeping, a woman of the Ansar asked permission to come in to me, and I gave her permission, and she sat weeping with me. While we were in that state, the Messenger of Allah ﷺ came in to us, greeted us, and then sat down. She said: He had not sat with me since what had been said about me was said, and a month had passed without any revelation coming to him concerning my affair.

She said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ recited the testimony of faith when he sat down, then said, "Now then, O A'isha, it has reached me about you such and such. If you are innocent, Allah will declare your innocence, but if you have committed a sin, then seek Allah's forgiveness and turn to Him in repentance, for when a servant confesses a sin and then repents, Allah accepts his repentance."

She said: When the Messenger of Allah ﷺ finished his speech, my tears dried up until I did not feel a single drop of them. I said to my father: Answer the Messenger of Allah ﷺ on my behalf. He said: By Allah, I do not know what to say to the Messenger. So I said to my mother: Answer the Messenger of Allah on my behalf. She said: By Allah, I do not know what to say to the Messenger of Allah. She said: So I said, while I was a young girl who did not memorize much of the Qur'an: By Allah, I know indeed that you have heard this until it settled in your minds and you believed it. If I tell you that I am innocent, and Allah knows that I am innocent, you will not believe me in that. And if I confess to you something, while Allah, mighty and majestic is He, knows that I am innocent, you will believe me. By Allah, I find no example for myself and for you except what the father of Yusuf said: {So patience is beautiful, and Allah is the one sought for help against what you describe} [Yusuf: 18]. She said: Then I turned and lay down on my bed. She said: And I, by Allah, at that time knew that I was innocent, and that Allah would declare my innocence through my innocence itself, but by Allah I never thought that revelation would be sent down concerning my affair to be recited, for my affair was too insignificant in my own eyes for Allah to speak about me with a matter that would be recited. But I hoped that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ might see in his sleep a dream through which Allah would declare my innocence. She said: By Allah, the Messenger of Allah ﷺ did not move from his seat, and no one of the household went out, until Allah sent down revelation upon His Prophet. He was seized by what used to seize him at the time of revelation, until beads of sweat like pearls poured down from him even on a cold winter day, from the heaviness of the words revealed to him.

She said: When the state was lifted from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, he was laughing, and the first word he spoke was: "Rejoice, O Aisha, for Allah has indeed declared you innocent." My mother said to me: Get up to him. I said: By Allah, I will not get up to him, and I will not praise anyone but Allah, mighty and majestic is He. He is the One who sent down my innocence.

[The narration continues with material that appears somewhat disordered in the text, concerning a beautiful woman with a husband who loves her and co-wives who envy her, and the recognition that what befell her was greater than what befell others, and her asking whether her father knew of it, and being told yes, and whether the Messenger of Allah ﷺ knew of it, and being told yes, he too.]

Then I wept and cried, and Abu Bakr heard my voice while he was above the house reciting. He came down and said to my mother: What is the matter with her? She said: What has been said concerning her affair has reached her. His eyes overflowed with tears and he said: I adjure you, my daughter, to go back to your house. So I went back.

And the Messenger of Allah ﷺ had come to my house and asked my servant girl about me. She said: No, by Allah, I know no fault in her except that she used to sleep until the sheep would come in and eat her dough, or her kneaded flour. Some of his companions rebuked her and said: Tell the Messenger of Allah ﷺ the truth, until they pressed her hard about it. She said: Glory be to Allah. By Allah, I know nothing about her except what a goldsmith knows about a lump of red gold.

The matter reached the man who had been spoken of, and he said: Glory be to Allah. By Allah, I have never uncovered the private area of any woman. Aisha said: He was later killed as a martyr in the way of Allah.

She said: My parents spent the morning with me, and they did not leave until the Messenger of Allah ﷺ came in to me, having prayed the afternoon prayer. He entered while my parents were beside me, one on my right and one on my left. He praised Allah and extolled Him, then said: "Now then, O Aisha, if you have committed a wrong or done injustice, then repent to Allah, for Allah accepts repentance from His servants."

She said: A woman from the Ansar had come and was sitting at the door. I said: Are you not ashamed before this woman, that you should mention such a thing? The Messenger of Allah ﷺ admonished me, so I turned to my father and said to him: Answer him. He said: What should I say? I turned to my mother and said: Answer him. She said: What should I say?

When neither of them answered him, I bore witness to the faith, praised Allah and extolled Him as He deserves, then said: Now then, by Allah, if I tell you that I did not do it, and Allah, mighty and majestic is He, is witness that I am truthful, that will not benefit me with you, for you have spoken of it and your hearts have drunk it in. And if I say that I did do it, while Allah knows that I did not do it, you will surely say she has admitted it against herself. By Allah, I find no example for myself and for you, and I sought the name of Yaqub but could not recall it, except the father of Yusuf when he said: {So patience is beautiful, and Allah is the one sought for help against what you describe} [Yusuf: 18].

Then Allah sent down revelation upon His Messenger ﷺ at that very moment, so we fell silent. When the state was lifted from him, I could clearly see joy on his face as he wiped his forehead and said: "Rejoice, O Aisha, for Allah has sent down your innocence." She said: I was at the height of anger I had ever felt. My parents said to me: Get up to him. I said: No, by Allah, I will not get up to him, nor will I praise him, nor will I praise you two, but I will praise Allah who sent down my innocence. You had heard of it and yet did not deny it nor change it.

Aisha used to say: As for Zaynab bint Jahsh, Allah protected her through her religion, so she said nothing but good. But her sister Hamnah bint Jahsh perished among those who perished. The ones who spread the talk were Mistah and Hassan ibn Thabit. As for the hypocrite Abdullah ibn Ubayy ibn Salul, he was the one who used to draw it out and gather it together, and he was the one who bore the greatest burden of it among them, he and Hamnah.

She said: Abu Bakr swore that he would never again benefit Mistah in any way. Then Allah sent down: {And let not those of you who possess dignity and ample means} to the end of the verse, meaning Abu Bakr, {refrain from giving to their relatives and the needy}, meaning Mistah, up to His saying: {Do you not love that Allah should forgive you? And Allah is Forgiving, Merciful} [al-Nur: 22]. Abu Bakr said: Yes indeed, by Allah, O our Lord, we do love that You forgive us, and he resumed what he had been doing for him.

Thus al-Bukhari related it by this route, in suspended form with a definite attribution, from Abu Usamah Hammad ibn Usamah, one of the trustworthy leading scholars. Ibn Jarir also related it in his tafsir, from Sufyan ibn Waki', from Abu Usamah, in a similarly lengthy form or close to it. Ibn Abi Hatim related it from Abu Sa'id al-Ashajj, from Abu Usamah, with part of it.

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] ... Hushaym told us, Umar ibn Abi Salamah informed us, from his father, from Aisha, may Allah be pleased with her, who said: When my exoneration came down from heaven, the Prophet ﷺ came to me and informed me of that, so I said: We praise Allah, not you.

Imam Ahmad also said: [chain] ... Ibn Abi Adi told me, from Muhammad ibn Ishaq, from Abdullah ibn Abi Bakr, from Amrah, from Aisha, who said: When my exoneration came down, the Messenger of Allah ﷺ stood up and mentioned that, and recited the Qur'an. When it came down, he ordered that two men and a woman be given their prescribed punishment.

This was also recorded by the compilers of the four Sunan collections, and al-Tirmidhi said: This is a hasan (sound) hadith. In the version of Abu Dawud their names are given: Hassan ibn Thabit, Mistah ibn Uthathah, and Hamnah bint Jahsh.

These are numerous routes, from the Mother of the Believers, Aisha, may Allah be pleased with her, found in the Masanid, the authentic collections, the Sunan, and elsewhere.

It has also been related from the hadith of her mother, Umm Ruman, may Allah be pleased with her. Imam Ahmad said:

[chain] ... Ali ibn Asim told us, Husayn informed us, from Abu Wa'il, from Masruq, from Umm Ruman, who said: While I was with Aisha, a woman from the Ansar came in to her and said: May Allah do such and such to her son. Aisha said: Why? She said: He was among those who spread the talk. Aisha said: What talk? She said: Such and such. Aisha said: Has that reached the Messenger of Allah ﷺ? She said: Yes. And has it reached Abu Bakr? She said: Yes.

Then Aisha, may Allah be pleased with her, fell down unconscious, and when she recovered she had a shivering fever. Umm Ruman said: I got up and covered her. Then the Prophet ﷺ came and said: "What is the matter with her?" I said: O Messenger of Allah, a shivering fever has seized her. He said: "Perhaps it is because of a story that has been spread about her."

Umm Ruman said: Then Aisha sat herself up and said: By Allah, if I swear to you, you will not believe me, and if I offer you an excuse, you will not excuse me. My example and yours is like the example of Yaqub and his sons: {And Allah is the one sought for help against what you describe} [Yusuf: 18].

She said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ then went out, and Allah sent down her exoneration. The Messenger of Allah ﷺ returned, and Abu Bakr with him. He entered and said: "O Aisha, Allah, exalted is He, has indeed sent down your exoneration." She said: By the praise of Allah, not by your praise. Abu Bakr said to her: Do you say this to the Messenger of Allah ﷺ? She said: Yes.

She said: among those who narrated this hadith was a man whom Abu Bakr used to support financially. Abu Bakr swore that he would not maintain ties with him. So Allah revealed: {And let not those of you who possess affluence and ample means swear off} to the end of the verse [al-Nur: 22]. Abu Bakr said: "Yes indeed," and he resumed supporting him.

Only al-Bukhari related this, not Muslim, through the route of Husayn. Al-Bukhari related it from Musa ibn Isma'il, from Abu 'Awana, and also from Muhammad ibn Salam, from Muhammad ibn Fudayl, both of them from Husayn, with this content. In Abu 'Awana's wording it says: "Umm Ruman narrated to me." This is explicit that Masruq heard directly from her, but a number of the hadith scholars have denied this, among them al-Khatib al-Baghdadi, because the historians have recorded that she died during the lifetime of the Prophet ﷺ. Al-Khatib said: "Masruq used to relate it in a disconnected form (mursal), saying: 'Umm Ruman was asked,' and then he would narrate it. Perhaps someone wrote 'she was asked' (su'ilat) with an alif, and the transmitter took it to mean 'she asked' (sa'alat), thinking it thereby connected." Al-Khatib said: "Al-Bukhari related it in this way, and its defect was not apparent to him." This is what he said, and Allah knows best.

As for His saying, {Indeed, those who brought forth the lie}, that is, the falsehood, the slander, and the fabrication, {are a band}, that is, a group from among you, {do not think it evil for you}, that is, O family of Abu Bakr, {rather it is good for you}, that is, in this world and the next: a truthful reputation in this world and elevated ranks in the hereafter, and a manifestation of honor for them through Allah's attention to 'A'isha, Mother of the Believers, in that Allah Most High revealed her innocence in the mighty Qur'an, that {falsehood does not approach it from before it or from behind it, a revelation from the Wise, the Praised} [Fussilat: 42]. For this reason, when Ibn 'Abbas, may Allah be pleased with him, came to her while she was in the throes of death, he said to her: "Rejoice, for you are the wife of the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, and he loved you, and he married no other virgin besides you, and your innocence was sent down from heaven."

Ibn Jarir said in his tafsir: [chain] Muhammad ibn 'Abdullah ibn Jahsh said: 'A'isha and Zaynab, may Allah be pleased with both of them, were boasting to one another. Zaynab said: "I am the one whose marriage was sent down [from heaven]." He said: And 'A'isha said: "I am the one whose exoneration was sent down in His Book, when Ibn al-Mu'attal carried me on the mount." Zaynab said to her: "O 'A'isha, what did you say when you mounted it?" She said: "I said, 'Allah is sufficient for me, and He is the best guardian.'" Zaynab said: "You spoke the word of the believers."

As for His saying, {For every person among them is what he has earned of sin}, that is, for everyone who spoke in this affair and cast at the Mother of the Believers, 'A'isha, may Allah be pleased with her, any accusation of indecency, there is a mighty portion of punishment.

{And the one who took upon himself the greater part of it}: it is said that this means he initiated it. It is also said that it refers to the one who used to gather it, provoke it, spread it, and circulate it. {For him is a great punishment}, that is, for that.

The majority hold that what is meant by this is 'Abdullah ibn Ubayy ibn Salul, may Allah disfigure him and curse him, who is the one previously named explicitly in the hadith. This was said by Mujahid and others.

It is also said that what is meant is Hassan ibn Thabit, but this is a strange (gharib) view, and were it not that something appearing to support it occurs in Sahih al-Bukhari, there would be little benefit in mentioning it, for he was among the Companions who had virtues, noble deeds, and merits, and the best of his fine qualities was that he used to defend the Messenger of Allah ﷺ [with his poetry]. He is the one to whom the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Satirize them, and Gabriel is with you."

Al-A'mash said, from Abu al-Duha, from Masruq, who said: I was with 'A'isha, may Allah be pleased with her, when Hassan ibn Thabit came in. She ordered that a cushion be laid out for him. When he left, I said to 'A'isha: "What are you doing with this man?" meaning, letting him come in to see you. And in another version it was said to her: "Do you permit this man to visit you, when Allah has said, {And the one among them who took upon himself the greater part of it, for him is a great punishment}?" She said: "What punishment is more severe than blindness?" for he had lost his sight. "Perhaps Allah has made that the great punishment." Then she said: "He used to defend the Messenger of Allah ﷺ vigorously."

In another version, it is reported that he recited to her, when he came in to see her, poetry in her praise, saying:

"A chaste and dignified woman, never suspected of any impropriety, who rises hungry, never feasting on the flesh of the heedless (that is, never slandering anyone)..."

She said: "As for you, you are not like that." And in another version: "But you are not like that."

Ibn Jarir said: [chain] from 'Amir, from 'A'isha, that she said: "I have never heard anything finer than Hassan's poetry, and I never recited it without hoping Paradise for him," referring to his saying to Abu Sufyan, that is, the son of [al-Harith] ibn 'Abd al-Muttalib:

"You satirized Muhammad, and I answered on his behalf, and with Allah lies the reward for that.

For my father and his father and my honor are, against your honor, a shield for Muhammad's honor.

Do you revile him, when you are no match for him? Then let the worse of you two be ransomed for the better.

My tongue is a sharp sword, free of any flaw, and my sea is one whose waters the buckets cannot muddy."

It was said: "O Mother of the Believers, is this not idle talk (laghw)?" She said: "No, idle talk is only what is said in the presence of women." It was said: "Does not Allah say, {And the one among them who took upon himself the greater part of it, for him is a great punishment}?" She said: "Did not a great punishment befall him? Did he not lose his sight and become crippled (kunni'a) by the sword?" meaning the blow that Safwan ibn al-Mu'attal [al-Sulami] struck him with, when it reached him that Hassan had spoken about that matter, so he attacked him with the sword and nearly killed him.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

هَذِهِ الْعَشْرُ الْآيَاتِ كُلُّهَا نَزَلَتْ فِي شَأْنِ عَائِشَةَ أُمِّ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهَا، حِينَ رَمَاهَا أَهْلُ الْإِفْكِ وَالْبُهْتَانِ مِنَ الْمُنَافِقِينَ بِمَا قَالُوهُ مِنَ الْكَذِبِ الْبَحْتِ وَالْفِرْيَةِ الَّتِي غَارَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى لَهَا وَلِنَبِيِّهِ، صَلَوَاتُ اللَّهِ وَسَلَامُهُ عَلَيْهِ، فَأَنْزَلَ [اللَّهُ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ] بَرَاءَتَهَا صِيَانَةً لِعِرْضِ الرَّسُولِ، عَلَيْهِ أَفْضَلُ الصَّلَاةِ وَالسَّلَامِ فَقَالَ: ﴿إِنَّ الَّذِينَ جَاءُوا بِالإفْكِ عُصْبَةٌ﴾ أَيْ: جَمَاعَةٌ مِنْكُمْ، يَعْنِي: مَا هُوَ وَاحِدٌ وَلَا اثْنَانِ بَلْ جَمَاعَةٌ، فَكَانَ المقدَّم فِي هَذِهِ اللَّعْنَةِ عبد الله بن أبي بن سلول رأس الْمُنَافِقِينَ، فَإِنَّهُ كَانَ يَجْمَعُهُ وَيَسْتَوْشِيهِ، حَتَّى دَخَلَ ذَلِكَ فِي أَذْهَانِ بَعْضِ الْمُسْلِمِينَ، فَتَكَلَّمُوا بِهِ، وَجوّزه آخَرُونَ مِنْهُمْ، وَبَقِيَ الْأَمْرُ كَذَلِكَ قَرِيبًا مِنْ شَهْرٍ، حَتَّى نَزَلَ الْقُرْآنُ، وَسِيَاقُ ذَلِكَ فِي الْأَحَادِيثِ الصَّحِيحَةِ.

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الرَّزَّاقِ، حَدَّثَنَا مَعْمَر، عنِ الزُّهْرِيِّ قَالَ: أَخْبَرَنِي سَعِيدُ بْنُ المسَيَّب، وعُرْوَة بْنُ الزُّبَيْرِ، وَعَلْقَمَةُ بْنُ وَقَّاصٍ، وعُبَيد اللَّهِ بْنِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عُتْبَةَ بْنِ مَسْعُودٍ، عَنْ حَدِيثِ عائشة زوج النبي صلى الله عليه وسلم، حِينَ قَالَ لَهَا أَهْلُ الْإِفْكِ مَا قَالُوا، فَبَرَّأَهَا اللَّهُ، وَكُلُّهُمْ قَدْ حَدَّثَنِي بِطَائِفَةٍ مِنْ حَدِيثِهَا، وَبَعْضُهُمْ كَانَ أَوَعَى لِحَدِيثِهَا مِنْ بَعْضٍ وَأَثْبَتَ اقْتِصَاصًا، وَقَدْ وَعَيْتُ عَنْ كُلِّ وَاحِدٍ مِنْهُمُ الْحَدِيثَ الَّذِي حَدَّثَنِي، وَبَعْضُ حَدِيثِهِمْ يُصَدِّقُ بَعْضًا: ذَكَرُوا أَنَّ عَائِشَةَ زَوْجَ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ قَالَتْ: كَانَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ إِذَا أَرَادَ أَنْ يَخْرُجَ سَفَرًا أَقْرَعَ بَيْنَ نِسَائِهِ، فَأَيَّتُهُنَّ خَرَجَ سَهْمُهَا خَرَجَ بِهَا رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ مَعَهُ، قَالَتْ عَائِشَةُ: فَأَقْرَعَ بَيْنَنَا فِي غَزْوَةٍ غَزَاهَا، فَخَرَجَ فِيهَا سَهْمِي، وَخَرَجْتُ مَعَ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ، وَذَلِكَ بَعْدَمَا أُنْزِلَ الحجابُ، فَأَنَا أحْمَل فِي هَودَجي وَأُنْزَلُ فِيهِ مَسِيرَنَا، حَتَّى إِذَا فَرَغَ رسول الله صلى الله عليه وسلم من غَزْوه وَقَفَلَ وَدَنَوْنَا مِنَ الْمَدِينَةِ، آذَنَ لَيْلَةً بِالرَّحِيلِ، فَقُمْتُ حِينَ آذَنُوا بِالرَّحِيلِ، فَمَشَيْتُ حَتَّى جَاوَزْتُ الْجَيْشَ، فَلَمَّا قَضَيْتُ شَأْنِي أَقْبَلْتُ إِلَى الرَّحْلِ فَلَمَسْتُ صَدْرِي، فَإِذَا عقْد مِنْ جَزْع ظَفار قَدِ انْقَطَعَ، فَرَجَعْتُ فَالْتَمَسْتُ عِقْدِي، فحَبَسني ابْتِغَاؤُهُ. وَأَقْبَلَ الرَّهْطُ الَّذِينَ كَانُوا يَرْحَلُونَ بِي فَحَمَلُوا هَوْدَجِي فَرَحَلُوهُ عَلَى بَعِيرِي الَّذِي كُنْتُ أَرْكَبُ -وَهُمْ يَحْسَبُونَ أَنِّي فِيهِ -قَالَتْ: وَكَانَ النساء إذ ذاك خفافا لم يُهَلَبْهُنَّ وَلَمْ يَغْشَهُنَّ اللحمُ، إِنَّمَا يَأْكُلْنَ العُلقْة مِنَ الطَّعَامِ. فَلَمْ يَسْتَنْكِرِ الْقَوْمُ ثِقَلَ الْهَوْدَجِ حِينَ رَحَّلُوهُ وَرَفَعُوهُ، وَكُنْتُ جَارِيَةً حَدِيثَةَ السِّنِّ، فَبَعَثُوا الجمل وساروا، وَوَجَدْتُ عِقْدِي بَعْدَمَا اسْتَمَرَّ الْجَيْشُ، فَجِئْتُ مَنَازِلَهُمْ وَلَيْسَ بِهَا دَاعٍ وَلَا مُجِيبٌ، فَتَيَمَّمْتُ مَنْزِلِي الَّذِي كُنْتُ فِيهِ، وَظَنَنْتُ أَنَّ الْقَوْمَ سَيَفْقِدُونِي فَيَرْجِعُونَ إِلَيَّ. فَبَيْنَا أَنَا جَالِسَةٌ فِي مَنْزِلِي، غَلَبَتْنِي عَيْنِي فَنِمْتُ -وَكَانَ صَفْوَانُ بْنُ الْمُعَطَّلِ السُّلَمِيُّ ثُمَّ الذّكْوَانَي قَدْ عَرَس مِنْ وَرَاءِ الْجَيْشِ -فَادَّلَجَ فَأَصْبَحَ عِنْدَ مَنْزِلِي، فَرَأَى سَوَادَ إِنْسَانٍ نَائِمٍ، فَأَتَانِي فَعَرَفَنِي حِينَ رَآنِي. وَقَدْ كَانَ يَرَانِي قَبْلَ أَنْ يُضْرَب عَلَيَّ الْحِجَابُ، فَاسْتَيْقَظْتُ بِاسْتِرْجَاعِهِ حِينَ عَرَفَنِي، فخَمَّرت وَجْهِي بِجِلْبَابِي، وَاللَّهِ مَا كَلَّمَنِي كَلِمَةً، وَلَا سَمِعْتُ مِنْهُ كَلِمَةً غيرَ اسْتِرْجَاعِهِ، حَتَّى أَنَاخَ رَاحِلَتَهُ، فَوْطئ عَلَى يَدها فركبتُها، فَانْطَلَقَ يَقُودُ بِي الرَّاحِلَةَ حَتَّى أَتَيْنَا الْجَيْشَ بَعْدَمَا نَزَلُوا مُوغرين فِي نَحْرِ الظَّهِيرَةِ. فَهَلَكَ مَنْ هَلَكَ فِي شَأْنِي، وَكَانَ الَّذِي تَوَلَّى كِبْره عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ أُبَيِّ بْنِ سَلُولٍ. فَقَدمتُ الْمَدِينَةَ فَاشْتَكَيْتُ حِينَ قَدِمْنَا شَهْرًا، وَالنَّاسُ يُفيضُون فِي قَوْلِ أَهِلِ الْإِفْكِ، وَلَا أَشْعُرُ بِشَيْءٍ مِنْ ذَلِكَ، وَهُوَ يَريبني فِي وَجَعِي أَنِّي لَا أَعْرِفُ مِنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ اللُّطْف الَّذِي كُنْتُ أَرَى مِنْهُ حِينَ أَشْتَكِي، إِنَّمَا يَدْخُلُ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ فَيُسَلِّمُ، ثُمَّ يَقُولُ: " كَيْفَ تِيكُم؟ " فَذَلِكَ يَرِيبني وَلَا أَشْعُرُ بِالشَّرِّ، حَتَّى خَرَجْتُ بَعْدَمَا نَقِهْت وخَرَجَت مَعِي أُمُّ مِسطْح قِبَلَ الْمَنَاصِعِ -وَهُوَ مُتَبَرَّزُنا -وَلَا نَخْرُجُ إِلَّا لَيْلًا إِلَى لَيْلٍ، وَذَلِكَ قَبْلَ أَنْ نَتَّخذَ الكُنُف قَرِيبًا مِنْ بُيُوتِنَا، وَأَمْرُنَا أَمْرُ الْعَرَبِ الْأُوَلِ فِي التَّنَزُّهِ، وَكُنَّا نَتَأَذَّى بالكُنُف أَنْ نَتَّخِذَهَا فِي بُيُوتِنَا. فَانْطَلَقْتُ أَنَا وَأُمُّ مسْطَح -وَهِيَ ابْنَةُ أَبِي رُهْم بْنِ الْمُطَّلِبِ بْنِ عَبْدِ مَنَافٍ، وَأُمُّهَا ابنة صخر بن عامر، خالة أبي بكر الصديق، وَابْنُهَا مسْطَح بْنُ أُثَاثَةَ بْنِ عَبَّاد بْنِ الْمُطَّلِبِ -فَأَقْبَلْتُ أَنَا وَابْنَةُ أَبِي رُهْمٍ قِبَلَ بَيْتِي حِينَ فَرَغْنَا مِنْ شَأْنِنَا، فَعَثَرَتْ أُمُّ مسْطح فِي مِرْطها فَقَالَتْ: "تَعس مسْطح". فَقُلْتُ لَهَا: بِئْسَمَا قُلْتِ، تَسُبِّينَ رَجُلًا [قَدْ «١» ] شَهِدَ «٢» بَدْرًا؟ قَالَتْ: أَيْ هَنْتاه، أَلَمْ «٣» تَسْمَعِي مَا قَالَ؟ قُلْتُ: وَمَاذَا قَالَ؟ فَأَخْبَرَتْنِي «٤» بِقَوْلِ أَهْلِ الْإِفْكِ، فازددتُ مَرَضًا إِلَى «٥» مَرَضِي. فَلَمَّا رجعتُ إِلَى بَيْتِي دَخَلَ عَلَيَّ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ فَسَلَّمَ، ثُمَّ قَالَ: "كَيْفَ تِيكُم؟ " قُلْتُ: أَتَأْذَنُ لِي أَنْ آتِيَ أَبَوَيَّ؟ -قَالَتْ: وَأَنَا حِينَئِذٍ أُرِيدُ أَنْ أَتَيَقَّنَ الْخَبَرَ مِنْ قبَلهما -فأذنَ لِي رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ، فَجِئْتُ أَبَوَيَّ فَقُلْتُ لِأُمِّي: يَا أمَّتاه، مَا يَتَحَدَّثُ النَّاسُ؟ فَقَالَتْ: أيْ بُنَية «٦» هَوِّني عَلَيْكِ، فَوَاللَّهِ لَقَلَّمَا كَانَتِ «٧» امْرَأَةٌ قَطّ وَضِيئَةٌ، عِنْدَ رَجُلٍ يُحِبُّهَا، وَلَهَا ضَرَائِرُ إِلَّا أَكْثَرْنَ عَلَيْهَا. قَالَتْ: فقلتُ: سُبْحَانَ اللَّهِ أَوَقَدَ تَحَدَّثَ النَّاسُ بِهَذَا؟ قَالَتْ: فَبَكَيْتُ تِلْكَ اللَّيْلَةَ حَتَّى أَصْبَحْتُ، لَا يَرْقَأُ لِي دَمْعٌ وَلَا أَكْتَحِلُ بِنَوْمٍ، ثُمَّ أَصْبَحْتُ أَبْكِي. فَدَعَا رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ عَلِيّا «٨» وَأُسَامَةَ بْنَ زَيْدٍ حِينَ اسْتَلْبَثَ الوحيُ، يَسْتَشِيرُهُمَا فِي فِرَاقِ أَهْلِهِ، قَالَتْ: فَأَمَّا أُسَامَةُ بْنُ زَيْدٍ فَأَشَارَ عَلَى رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ بِالَّذِي يَعْلَمُ مِنْ بَرَاءَةِ أَهْلِهِ، وَبِالَّذِي يَعْلَمُ فِي نَفْسِهِ لَهُ مِنَ الْوُدِّ، فَقَالَ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، هُمْ أَهْلُكَ، وَلَا نَعْلَمُ إِلَّا خَيْرًا. وَأَمَّا عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَالِبٍ فَقَالَ: لَمْ يُضيق اللَّهُ عَلَيْكَ، وَالنِّسَاءُ سِوَاهَا كَثِيرٌ، وَإِنْ تَسْأَلِ الْجَارِيَةَ تصدُقك الْخَبَرَ. قَالَتْ «٩» : فَدَعَا رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ بَريرة، فَقَالَ: "أيْ بَرِيرة، هَلْ رَأَيْتِ مِنْ شَيْءٍ يَريبك مِنْ عَائِشَةَ؟ " فَقَالَتْ لَهُ بِرَيْرَةُ: وَالَّذِي بَعَثَكَ بِالْحَقِّ إنْ رَأَيْتُ عَلَيْهَا أَمَرًا قَطّ أغمصُه عَلَيْهَا، أَكْثَرَ مِنْ أَنَّهَا جَارِيَةٌ حَدِيثَةُ السِّنِّ، تَنَامُ عَنْ عَجِينِ أَهْلِهَا، فَتَأْتِي الدَّاجِنَ فَتَأْكُلُهُ، فَقَامَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ فَاسْتَعْذَرَ مِنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ أُبَيِّ بْنِ سَلُول. قَالَتْ: فَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ وَهُوَ عَلَى الْمِنْبَرِ: "يَا مَعْشَرَ الْمُسْلِمِينَ مَنْ يَعْذِرُنِي مِنْ رَجُلٍ قَدْ بَلَغَنِي أَذَاهُ فِي أَهْلِ بَيْتِي، فَوَاللَّهِ مَا عَلِمْتُ عَلَى أَهْلِي إِلَّا خَيْرًا، وَلَقَدْ ذَكَرُوا رَجُلًا مَا عَلِمْتُ عَلَيْهِ إِلَّا خَيْرًا، وَمَا كَانَ يَدْخُلُ عَلَى أَهْلِي إِلَّا مَعِي". فَقَامَ سَعْدُ بْنُ مُعَاذٍ الْأَنْصَارِيُّ فَقَالَ: أَنَا أَعْذِرُكَ مِنْهُ يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، إِنْ كَانَ مِنَ الْأَوْسِ ضَرَبْنَا عُنُقَهُ، وَإِنْ كَانَ مِنْ إِخْوَانِنَا مِنَ الْخَزْرَجِ، أَمَرْتَنَا فَفَعَلْنَا أَمْرَكَ. قَالَتْ: فَقَامَ سَعْدُ بْنُ عُبَادَةَ -وَهُوَ سَيِّدُ الْخَزْرَجِ، وَكَانَ رَجُلًا صَالِحًا، وَلَكِنِ احْتَمَلَتْهُ الْحَمِيَّةُ -فقال لسعد ابن مُعَاذٍ: لَعَمْرُ اللَّهِ لَا تَقْتُلُهُ «١٠» وَلَا تَقْدِرُ عَلَى قَتْلِهِ. فَقَامَ أُسَيد بْنُ حُضير _ وَهُوَ ابْنُ عَمِّ سَعْدِ بْنِ مُعَاذٍ -فَقَالَ لِسَعْدِ بْنِ عُبَادَةَ: كَذَبْتَ! لَعَمْرُ اللَّهِ «١١» لَنَقْتُلَنَّهُ، فَإِنَّكَ مُنَافِقٌ تُجَادِلُ عَنِ الْمُنَافِقِينَ. فَتَثَاوَرَ الْحَيَّانِ الْأَوْسُ وَالْخَزْرَجُ حَتَّى هَمّوا أَنْ يَقْتَتِلُوا، وَرَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ [قَائِمٌ عَلَى الْمِنْبَرِ. فَلَمْ يَزَلْ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ] «١٢» يُخَفّضهم حَتَّى سَكَتُوا وَسَكَتَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ، قَالَتِ: وَبَكَيْتُ يَوْمِي ذَلِكَ، لَا يَرْقَأُ لِي دَمْعٌ، وَلَا أَكْتَحِلُ بِنَوْمٍ، وَأَبَوَايَ يَظُنَّانِ أَنَّ الْبُكَاءَ فَالِقُ كَبِدِي. قَالَتْ: فَبَيْنَمَا هُمَا جَالِسَانِ عِنْدِي وَأَنَا أَبْكِي، استأذَنَت عليَّ امْرَأَةٌ مِنَ الْأَنْصَارِ، فأذنتُ لَهَا، فَجَلَسَتْ تَبْكِي مَعِي، فَبَيْنَا نَحْنُ عَلَى ذَلِكَ «١٣» إِذْ دَخَلَ عَلَيْنَا رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ فَسَلَّمَ ثُمَّ جَلَسَ -قَالَتْ: وَلَمْ يَجْلِسْ عِنْدِي مُنْذُ قِيلَ [لِي] «١٤» مَا قِيلَ، وَقَدْ لَبِثَ شَهْرًا لَا يُوحَى إِلَيْهِ فِي شَأْنِي شَيْءٌ -قَالَتْ: فَتَشْهَّدَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ حِينَ جَلَسَ، ثُمَّ قَالَ: أَمَّا بَعْدُ يَا عَائِشَةُ، فَإِنَّهُ قَدْ بَلَغَنِي عَنْكِ كَذَا وَكَذَا، فَإِنْ كُنْتِ بَرِيئَةً فَسَيُبَرِّئُكِ اللَّهُ، وَإِنْ كُنْتِ ألْمَمْت بِذَنْبٍ فَاسْتَغْفِرِي اللَّهَ ثُمَّ تُوبِي إِلَيْهِ، فَإِنَّ الْعَبْدَ إِذَا اعْتَرَفَ بِذَنْبٍ ثُمَّ تَابَ، تَابَ اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ. قَالَتْ: فَلَمَّا قَضَى رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ مَقَالَتَهُ قَلَص دَمْعِي حَتَّى مَا أُحِسُّ مِنْهُ قَطْرَةً، فَقُلْتُ «١٥» لِأَبِي: أَجِبْ عَنِّي رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ. فَقَالَ: وَاللَّهِ مَا أَدْرِي مَا أَقُولُ لِلرَّسُولِ. فَقُلْتُ لِأُمِّي: أَجِيبِي عَنِّي رَسُولَ اللَّهِ. فَقَالَتْ: وَاللَّهِ مَا أَدْرِي مَا أَقُولُ لِرَسُولِ اللَّهِ. قَالَتْ: فَقُلْتُ -وَأَنَا جَارِيَةٌ حَدِيثَةُ السِّنِّ، لَا أَحْفَظُ «١٦» كَثِيرًا مِنَ الْقُرْآنِ -: [إِنِّي] «١٧» وَاللَّهِ لَقَدْ عَرَفْتُ أَنَّكُمْ قَدْ سَمِعْتُمْ بِهَذَا، حَتَّى اسْتَقَرَّ «١٨» فِي أَنْفُسِكُمْ وَصَدَّقْتُمْ بِهِ، ولَئَن «١٩» قُلْتُ لَكُمْ إِنِّي بَرِيئَةٌ -وَاللَّهُ يَعْلَمُ أَنِّي بَرِيئَةٌ -لَا تُصَدِّقُونِي [بِذَلِكَ. وَلَئِنِ اعْتَرَفْتُ لَكُمْ بِأَمْرٍ وَاللَّهُ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ يَعْلَمُ أَنِّي بَرِيئَةٌ تُصَدِّقُونِي] «٢٠» ، وَإِنِّي وَاللَّهِ مَا أَجِدُ لِي «٢١» وَلَكُمْ مَثَلًا إِلَّا كَمَا قَالَ أَبُو يُوسُفَ: ﴿فَصَبْرٌ جَمِيلٌ وَاللَّهُ الْمُسْتَعَانُ عَلَى مَا تَصِفُونَ﴾ [يُوسُفَ: ١٨] . قَالَتْ: ثُمَّ تَحَوَّلْتُ فَاضْطَجَعْتُ عَلَى فِرَاشِي، قَالَتْ: وَأَنَا وَاللَّهِ حِينَئِذٍ أَعْلَمُ أَنِّي بَرِيئَةٌ، وَأَنَّ اللَّهَ مُبَرِّئي بِبَرَاءَتِي، وَلَكِنْ وَاللَّهِ مَا كُنْتُ أَظُنُّ أَنْ يُنْزَلَ فِي شَأْنَيْ وَحَيٌّ يُتْلَى، وَلَشَأْنِي كَانَ أحقرَ فِي نَفْسِي مِنْ أَنْ يَتَكَلَّمَ اللَّهُ فِيَّ بِأَمْرٍ يُتلى. وَلَكِنْ كُنْتُ أَرْجُو أَنْ يَرَى رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ فِي النَّوْمِ رؤْيا يُبَرِّئُنِي اللَّهُ بِهَا. قَالَتْ: فَوَاللَّهِ مَا رَامَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ مِنْ مَجْلِسِهِ، وَلَا خَرَجَ مِنْ أَهْلِ الْبَيْتِ أَحَدٌ، حَتَّى أَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ عَلَى نَبِيِّهِ، فَأَخَذَهُ مَا كَانَ يَأْخُذُهُ مِنَ الْبُرَحَاءِ عِنْدَ الْوَحْيِ، حَتَّى إِنَّهُ لَيَنْحَدِرُ مِنْهُ مِثْلُ الجُمَان مِنَ العرق في اليوم الشاتي، مِنْ ثِقَل الْقَوْلِ الَّذِي أُنْزِلَ عَلَيْهِ. قَالَتْ «٢٢» : فَلَمَّا سُرّيَ عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ وَهُوَ يَضْحَكُ، كَانَ أَوَّلَ كَلِمَةٍ تَكَلَّمَ بِهَا أَنْ قَالَ: "أَبْشِرِي يَا عَائِشَةُ، أَمَّا اللَّهُ «٢٣» فَقَدْ بَرّأك «٢٤» . فَقَالَتْ لِي أُمِّي: قُومِي إِلَيْهِ. فَقُلْتُ: وَاللَّهِ لَا أَقُومُ إِلَيْهِ وَلَا أَحْمَدُ إِلَّا اللَّهَ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، هُوَ الَّذِي أَنْزَلَ بَرَاءَتِي «٢٥» وَأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ عَزَّ وَج حَسْنَاءُ، عِنْدَ رَجُلٍ يُحِبُّهَا، لَهَا ضَرَائِرُ إِلَّا حَسَدنها، وَقِيلَ فِيهَا وَإِذَا هُوَ لَمْ يَبْلُغْ مِنْهَا مَا بَلَغَ مِنِّي، فَقُلْتُ: وَقَدْ عَلِم بِهِ أَبِي؟ قَالَتْ: نَعَمْ. قُلْتُ: ورسولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ؟ قَالَتْ: نَعَمْ، وَرَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ] .فاستَعْبَرْتُ وَبَكَيْتُ، فسمعَ أَبُو بَكْرٍ صَوْتِي، وَهُوَ فَوْقُ الْبَيْتِ يَقْرَأُ، فَنَزَلَ فَقَالَ لِأُمِّي: مَا شَأْنُهَا؟ قَالَتْ: بَلَغَهَا الَّذِي ذُكر مِنْ شَأْنِهَا. فَفَاضَتْ عَيْنَاهُ وَقَالَ : أَقْسَمْتُ عَلَيْكِ -أيْ بُنَيّة -إِلَّا رَجَعْتِ إِلَى بَيْتِكِ فَرَجعتُ، وَلَقَدْ جَاءَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ بَيْتِي، فَسَأَلَ عَنِّي خَادِمِي فَقَالَتْ: لَا وَاللَّهِ مَا عَلِمْتُ عَلَيْهَا عَيْبًا، إِلَّا أَنَّهَا كَانَتْ تَرْقُدُ حَتَّى تَدْخُلَ الشَّاةُ فَتَأْكُلَ خَميرها -أَوْ: عَجِينَهَا -وَانْتَهَرَهَا بَعْضُ أَصْحَابِهِ فَقَالَ: اصدُقي رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ حَتَّى أَسْقَطُوا لَهَا بِهِ، فَقَالَتْ: سُبْحَانَ اللَّهِ. وَاللَّهِ مَا عَلِمْتُ عَلَيْهَا إِلَّا مَا يَعْلَمُ الصَّائِغُ عَلَى تبْر الذَّهَبِ الْأَحْمَرِ. وَبَلَغَ الْأَمْرُ ذَلِكَ الرجلَ الَّذِي قِيلَ لَهُ، فَقَالَ: سُبْحَانَ اللَّهِ. وَاللَّهِ مَا كَشَفت كَنَف أُنْثَى قَطُّ -قَالَتْ عَائِشَةُ: فَقُتِلَ شَهِيدًا فِي سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ -قَالَتْ: وَأَصْبَحَ أَبَوَايَ عِنْدِي، فَلَمْ يَزَالَا حَتَّى دَخَلَ عَلَيَّ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ وَقَدْ صَلّى الْعَصْرَ، ثُمَّ دَخَلَ وَقَدِ اكتنفَني أَبَوَايَ، عَنْ يَمِينِي وَعَنْ شِمَالِي، فَحَمِدَ اللَّهَ وَأَثْنَى عَلَيْهِ، ثُمَّ قَالَ: "أَمَّا بَعْدُ يَا عَائِشَةُ، إِنْ كُنْتِ قَارَفْتِ سُوءًا أَوْ ظَلَمت فَتُوبِي إِلَى اللَّهِ، فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ يَقْبَلُ التَّوْبَةَ عَنْ عِبَادِهِ". قَالَتْ: وَقَدْ جَاءَتِ امْرَأَةٌ مِنَ الْأَنْصَارِ، فَهِيَ جَالِسَةٌ بِالْبَابِ، فَقُلْتُ: أَلَا تَسْتَحِي مِنْ هَذِهِ الْمَرْأَةِ أَنْ تَذْكُرَ شَيْئًا؟ فَوَعَظَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ، فَالْتَفَتُّ إِلَى أَبِي، فَقُلْتُ لَهُ: أجبْه. قَالَ: فَمَاذَا أَقُولُ؟ فالتفتُ إِلَى أُمِّي فَقُلْتُ: أَجِيبِيهِ. قَالَتْ: أَقُولُ مَاذَا؟ فَلَمَّا لَمْ يُجِيبَاهُ، تَشَّهدتُ فحمدتُ اللَّهَ وَأَثْنَيْتُ عَلَيْهِ بِمَا هُوَ أَهْلُهُ، ثُمَّ قُلْتُ: أَمَّا بَعْدُ، فَوَالله لَئن قُلْتُ لَكُمْ إِنِّي لَمْ أَفْعَلْ -وَاللَّهُ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ يَشْهَدُ إِنِّي لَصَادِقَةٌ -مَا ذَاكَ بِنَافِعِي عِنْدَكُمْ، لَقَدْ تَكَلَّمْتُمْ بِهِ، وأشْربته قُلُوبُكُمْ، وَإِنْ قُلْتُ: إِنِّي قَدْ فَعَلْتُ -وَاللَّهُ يَعْلَمُ أَنِّي لَمْ أَفْعَلْ -لتقولُنَ: قَدْ بَاءَتْ بِهِ عَلَى نَفْسِهَا، وَإِنِّي -وَاللَّهِ -مَا أَجِدُ لِي وَلَكُمْ مَثَلًا -والتمستُ اسْمَ يَعْقُوبَ فَلَمْ أَقْدِرْ عَلَيْهِ -إِلَّا أَبَا يُوسُفَ حِينَ قَالَ: ﴿فَصَبْرٌ جَمِيلٌ وَاللَّهُ الْمُسْتَعَانُ عَلَى مَا تَصِفُونَ﴾ [يُوسُفَ: ١٨] ، وَأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ عَلَى رَسُولِهِ ﷺ مِنْ سَاعَتِهِ، فَسَكَتْنَا، فَرُفع عَنْهُ وَإِنِّي لَأَتَبَيَّنُ السُّرُورَ فِي وَجْهِهِ، وَهُوَ يَمْسَحُ جَبِينَهُ وَيَقُولُ: "أَبْشِرِي يَا عَائِشَةُ، فَقَدْ أَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ بَرَاءَتَكِ" قَالَتْ: وَكُنْتُ أَشَدَّ مَا كنتُ غَضَبًا، فَقَالَ لِي أَبَوَايَ: قُومِي [إِلَيْهِ] فَقُلْتُ: لَا وَاللَّهِ لَا أَقُومُ إِلَيْهِ وَلَا أَحْمَدُهُ وَلَا أَحْمَدُكُمَا، وَلَكِنْ أَحْمَدُ اللَّهَ الَّذِي أَنْزَلَ بَرَاءَتِي، لَقَدْ سَمِعْتُمُوهُ فَمَا أَنْكَرْتُمُوهُ وَلَا غَيَّرتموه، وَكَانَتْ عَائِشَةُ تَقُولُ: أَمَّا زَيْنَبُ بِنْتُ جَحْشٍ فَقَدْ عَصَمَهَا اللَّهُ بِدِينِهَا، فَلَمْ تَقُلْ إِلَّا خَيْرًا. وَأَمَّا أُخْتُهَا حَمنة بِنْتُ جَحْشٍ، فَهَلَكَتْ فِيمَنْ هَلَكَ. وَكَانَ الَّذِي يَتَكَلَّمُ بِهِ مِسْطَحٌ وَحَسَّانُ بْنُ ثَابِتٍ. وَأَمَّا الْمُنَافِقُ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ أُبَيِّ بْنِ سَلُولٍ فَهُوَ الَّذِي [كَانَ] يَسْتَوْشِيهِ وَيَجْمَعُهُ، وَهُوَ الَّذِي تَوَلَّى كِبْرَه مِنْهُمْ هُوَ وَحَمْنَةُ. قَالَتْ: وَحَلَفَ أَبُو بَكْرٍ أَلَّا يَنْفَعَ مِسْطَحًا بِنَافِعَةٍ أَبَدًا، فَأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ: ﴿وَلا يَأْتَلِ أُولُو الْفَضْلِ مِنْكُمْ وَالسَّعَةِ﴾ إِلَى آخِرِ الْآيَةِ، يَعْنِي: أَبَا بَكْرٍ، ﴿وَالسَّعَةِ أَنْ يُؤْتُوا أُولِي الْقُرْبَى وَالْمَسَاكِينَ﴾ يَعْنِي: مِسْطَحًا، إِلَى قَوْلِهِ: ﴿أَلا تُحِبُّونَ أَنْ يَغْفِرَ اللَّهُ لَكُمْ وَاللَّهُ غَفُورٌ رَحِيمٌ﴾ [النُّورِ: ٢٢] . فَقَالَ أَبُو بَكْرٍ: بَلَى وَاللَّهِ يَا رَبّنا، إِنَّا لنُحِبّ أَنْ تَغْفِرَ لَنَا وَعَادَ لَهُ بِمَا كَانَ يَصْنَعُ.

هَكَذَا رَوَاهُ الْبُخَارِيُّ مِنْ هَذَا الْوَجْهِ مُعَلَّقا بِصِيغَةِ الْجَزْمِ عَنْ أَبِي أُسَامَةَ حَمَّادِ بْنِ أُسَامَةَ [أَحَدِ الْأَئِمَّةِ الثِّقَاتِ. وَقَدْ رَوَاهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ فِي تَفْسِيرِهِ، عَنْ سُفْيَانَ بْنِ وَكيع، عَنْ أَبِي أُسَامَةَ] بِهِ مُطَوَّلًا مِثْلَهُ أَوْ نَحْوَهُ. وَرَوَاهُ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ عَنْ أَبِي سَعِيدٍ الْأَشَجِّ، عَنْ أَبِي أُسَامَةَ، بِبَعْضِهِ.

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَثنا هُشَيْم، أَخْبَرَنَا عُمَرَ بْنِ أَبِي سَلَمَةَ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنْ عَائِشَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهَا، قَالَتْ: لَمَّا نَزَلَ عُذْري مِنَ السَّمَاءِ، جَاءَنِي النَّبِيُّ ﷺ فَأَخْبَرَنِي بِذَلِكَ، فَقُلْتُ: نَحمدُ اللَّهَ لَا نَحمدك .

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنِي ابْنُ أَبِي عَدِيّ، عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ إِسْحَاقَ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ أَبِي بَكْرٍ، عَنْ عَمْرَةَ، عَنْ عَائِشَةَ قَالَتْ: لَمَّا نَزَلَ عُذْري قَامَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ فَذَكَرَ ذَلِكَ، وَتَلَا الْقُرْآنَ، فَلَمَّا نَزَلَ أَمَر بِرَجُلَيْنِ وَامْرَأَةٍ فَضُربوا حَدَّهُمْ .

وَأَخْرَجَهُ أَهْلُ السُّنَنِ الْأَرْبَعَةِ، وَقَالَ التِّرْمِذِيُّ: هَذَا حَدِيثٌ حَسَنٌ. وَوَقَعَ عِنْدَ أَبِي دَاوُدَ تَسْمِيَتُهُمْ: حَسَّانُ بْنُ ثَابِتٍ، ومِسْطح بْنُ أُثَاثَةَ، وحَمْنة بِنْتُ جَحْشٍ.

فَهَذِهِ طُرُقٌ مُتَعَدِّدَةٌ، عَنْ أُمِّ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ عَائِشَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهَا، فِي الْمَسَانِيدِ وَالصِّحَاحِ وَالسُّنَنِ وَغَيْرِهَا .

وَقَدْ رُوي مِنْ حَدِيثِ أُمِّهَا أُمِّ رُومَانَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهَا، فَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ:

حَدَّثَنَا عَلِيُّ بْنُ عَاصِمٍ، أَخْبَرَنَا حُصَين، عَنْ أَبِي وَائِلٍ، عَنْ مَسْرُوقٍ، عَنْ أُمِّ رُومَانَ قَالَتْ: بَيْنَا أَنَا عِنْدَ عَائِشَةَ، إِذْ دَخَلَتْ عَلَيْهَا امْرَأَةٌ مِنَ الْأَنْصَارِ فَقَالَتْ: فَعَلَ اللَّهُ -بِابْنِهَا -وَفَعَلَ. فَقَالَتْ عَائِشَةُ: وَلِمَ؟ قَالَتْ: إِنَّهُ كَانَ فِيمَنْ حَدَّث الْحَدِيثَ. قَالَتْ عَائِشَةُ: وَأَيُّ حَدِيثٍ؟ قَالَتْ: كَذَا وَكَذَا. قَالَتْ: وَقَدْ بَلَغَ ذَلِكَ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ؟ قَالَتْ: نَعَمْ، وَبَلَغَ أَبَا بَكْرٍ؟ قَالَتْ: نَعَمْ، فَخَرَّتْ عَائِشَةُ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهَا، مَغْشِيًّا عَلَيْهَا، فَمَا أَفَاقَتْ إِلَّا وَعَلَيْهَا حُمَّى بِنَافِضٍ. قَالَتْ: فَقُمْتُ فَدَثَّرْتُهَا، قَالَتْ: وَجَاءَ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ فَقَالَ: "مَا شَأْنُ هَذِهِ؟ " قُلْتُ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، أَخَذَتْهَا حُمَّى بِنَافِضٍ. قَالَ: فَلَعَلَّهُ فِي حَدِيثٍ تُحُدِّث بِهِ". قَالَتْ: فَاسْتَوَتْ لَهُ عَائِشَةُ قَاعِدَةً فَقَالَتْ: وَاللَّهِ لَئِنْ حَلَفْتُ لَكُمْ لَا تُصَدِّقُونِي، وَلَئِنِ اعْتَذَرْتُ إِلَيْكُمْ لَا تُعذرُوني، فَمَثَلِي وَمَثَلُكُمْ كَمَثَلِ يَعْقُوبَ وَبَنِيهِ ﴿وَاللَّهُ الْمُسْتَعَانُ عَلَى مَا تَصِفُونَ﴾ [يُوسُفَ: ١٨] قَالَتْ: وَخَرَجَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ، فَأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ عُذْرَهَا، فَرَجَعَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ مَعَهُ أَبُو بَكْرٍ، [فَدَخَلَ فَقَالَ: "يَا عَائِشَةُ، إِنَّ اللَّهَ تَعَالَى قَدْ أَنْزَلَ عُذْرَكِ". فَقَالَتْ: بِحَمْدِ اللَّهِ لَا بِحَمْدِكَ. فَقَالَ لَهَا أَبُو بَكْرٍ: تَقُولِينَ هَذَا لِرَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ؟ قَالَتْ: نَعَمْ. قَالَتْ: فَكَانَ فِيمَنْ حَدَّثَ هَذَا الْحَدِيثَ رَجُلٌ كَانَ يَعُولُهُ أَبُو بَكْرٍ] فَحَلَفَ أَبُو بَكْرٍ أَلَّا يَصِلَهُ، فَأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ: ﴿وَلا يَأْتَلِ أُولُو الْفَضْلِ مِنْكُمْ وَالسَّعَةِ﴾ إِلَى آخِرِ الْآيَةِ [النُّورِ: ٢٢] ، قال أبو بكر: بلى، فوصله.

تَفَرَّدَ بِهِ الْبُخَارِيُّ دُونَ مُسْلِمٍ، مِنْ طَرِيقِ حُصَين وَقَدْ رَوَاهُ الْبُخَارِيُّ، عَنْ مُوسَى بْنِ إِسْمَاعِيلَ، عَنْ أَبِي عَوَانة -وَعَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ سَلَامٍ -، عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ فُضَيْلٍ، كِلَاهُمَا عَنْ حُصَيْنٍ، بِهِ وَفِي لَفْظِ أَبِي عَوَانَةَ: حَدَّثَتْنِي أُمُّ رُومَانَ. وَهَذَا صَرِيحٌ فِي سَمَاعِ مَسْرُوقٍ مِنْهَا، وَقَدْ أَنْكَرَ ذَلِكَ جَمَاعَةٌ مِنَ الْحُفَّاظِ، مِنْهُمُ الْخَطِيبُ الْبَغْدَادِيُّ، وَذَلِكَ لِمَا ذَكَرَهُ أَهْلُ التَّارِيخِ أَنَّهَا مَاتَتْ فِي زَمَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ، قَالَ الْخَطِيبُ: وَقَدْ كَانَ مَسْرُوقٌ يُرْسِلُهُ فَيَقُولُ: "سُئِلَتْ أُمُّ رُومَانَ"، وَيَسُوقُهُ، فَلَعَلَّ بَعْضَهُمْ كَتَبَ "سُئلت" بِأَلِفٍ، فَاعْتَقَدَ الرَّاوِي أَنَّهَا "سَألت"، فَظَنَّهُ مُتَّصِلًا. قَالَ الْخَطِيبُ: "وَقَدْ رَوَاهُ الْبُخَارِيُّ كَذَلِكَ، وَلَمْ تَظْهَرْ لَهُ عِلَّتُهُ". كَذَا قَالَ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

فَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿إِنَّ الَّذِينَ جَاءُوا بِالإفْكِ﴾ أَيْ: بِالْكَذِبِ وَالْبَهْتِ وَالِافْتِرَاءِ، ﴿عُصْبَةٌ﴾ أَيْ: جَمَاعَةٌ مِنْكُمْ، ﴿لَا تَحْسَبُوهُ شَرًّا لَكُمْ﴾ أَيْ: يَا آلَ أَبِي بَكْرٍ ﴿بَلْ هُوَ خَيْرٌ لَكُمْ﴾ أَيْ: فِي الدُّنْيَا وَالْآخِرَةِ، لِسَانُ صِدْقٍ فِي الدُّنْيَا وَرِفْعَةُ مَنَازِلَ فِي الْآخِرَةِ، وَإِظْهَارُ شَرَفٍ لَهُمْ بِاعْتِنَاءِ اللَّهِ بِعَائِشَةَ أُمِّ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ، حَيْثُ أَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى بَرَاءَتَهَا فِي الْقُرْآنُ الْعَظِيمُ الذِي ﴿لَا يَأْتِيهِ الْبَاطِلُ مِنْ بَيْنِ يَدَيْهِ وَلا مِنْ خَلْفِهِ تَنزيلٌ مِنْ حَكِيمٍ حَمِيدٍ﴾ [فُصِّلَتْ: ٤٢] وَلِهَذَا لَمَّا دَخَلَ عَلَيْهَا ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ وَهِيَ فِي سِيَاقِ الْمَوْتِ، قَالَ لَهَا: أَبْشِرِي فَإِنَّكِ زَوْجَةُ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ، وَكَانَ يُحِبُّكِ، وَلَمْ يَتَزَوَّجْ بِكْرًا غَيْرَكِ، وَأُنْزِلَ بَرَاءَتُكِ مِنَ السَّمَاءِ .

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ فِي تَفْسِيرِهِ: حَدَّثَنِي مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ عُثْمَانَ الْوَاسِطِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا جَعْفَرُ بْنُ عَوْنٍ، عَنِ الْمُعَلَّى بْنِ عُرْفَانَ، عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ جَحْش قَالَ: تفاخَرَت عائشةُ وزينبُ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمَا، فَقَالَتْ زينب: أنا التي نزل تزوُّجي [مِنَ السَّمَاءِ] قَالَ: وَقَالَتْ عَائِشَةُ: أَنَا الَّتِي نَزَلَ عُذري فِي كِتَابِهِ، حِينَ حَمَلَنِي ابْنُ الْمُعَطَّلِ عَلَى الرَّاحِلَةِ. فَقَالَتْ لَهَا زَيْنَبُ: يَا عَائِشَةُ، مَا قُلْتِ حِينَ رَكَبْتِيهَا؟ قَالَتْ: قُلْتُ: حَسْبِيَ اللَّهُ وَنِعْمَ الْوَكِيلُ. قَالَتْ: قُلْتِ كَلِمَةَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿لِكُلِّ امْرِئٍ مِنْهُمْ مَا اكْتَسَبَ مِنَ الإثْمِ﴾ أَيْ: لِكُلِّ مَنْ تَكَلَّمَ فِي هَذِهِ الْقَضِيَّةِ ورَمَى أُمَّ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ عَائِشَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهَا، بِشَيْءٍ مِنَ الْفَاحِشَةِ، نَصِيبٌ عَظِيمٌ مِنَ الْعَذَابِ.

﴿وَالَّذِي تَوَلَّى كِبْرَهُ﴾ قِيلَ: ابْتَدَأَ بِهِ. وَقِيلَ: الَّذِي كَانَ يَجْمَعُهُ وَيَسْتَوْشِيهِ وَيُذِيعُهُ وَيُشِيعُهُ، ﴿لَهُ عَذَابٌ عَظِيمٌ﴾ أَيْ: عَلَى ذَلِكَ.

ثُمَّ الْأَكْثَرُونَ عَلَى أَنَّ الْمُرَادَ بِذَلِكَ إِنَّمَا هُوَ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ أُبَيِّ بْنِ سَلُول -قَبَّحَهُ اللَّهُ وَلَعْنَهُ -وَهُوَ الَّذِي تَقَدَّمَ النَّصُّ عَلَيْهِ فِي الْحَدِيثِ، وَقَالَ ذَلِكَ مُجَاهِدٌ وَغَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ.

وَقِيلَ: بَلِ الْمُرَادُ بِهِ حَسَّانُ بْنُ ثَابِتٍ، وَهُوَ قَوْلٌ غَرِيبٌ، وَلَوْلَا أَنَّهُ وَقَعَ في صحيح البخاري ما قَدْ يَدُلُّ عَلَى ذَلِكَ لَمَا كَانَ لِإِيرَادِهِ كَبِيرُ فَائِدَةٍ، فَإِنَّهُ مِنَ الصَّحَابَةِ الَّذِينَ كَانَ لَهُمْ فَضَائِلُ وَمَنَاقِبُ وَمَآثِرُ، وَأَحْسَنُ مَحَاسِنِهِ أَنَّهُ كَانَ يَذُب عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ [بِشِعْرِهِ] ، وَهُوَ الَّذِي قَالَ لَهُ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "هَاجِهِمْ وَجِبْرِيلُ مَعَكَ"

وَقَالَ الْأَعْمَشُ، عَنْ أَبِي الضُّحَى، عَنْ مَسْرُوقٍ قَالَ: كنتُ عندَ عَائِشَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهَا، فَدَخَلَ حَسَّانُ بْنُ ثَابِتٍ، فَأَمَرَتْ فَأُلْقِيَ لَهُ وِسَادَةٌ، فَلَمَّا خَرَجَ قُلْتُ لِعَائِشَةَ: مَا تَصْنَعِينَ بِهَذَا؟ يَعْنِي: يَدْخُلُ عَلَيْكِ -وَفِي رِوَايَةٍ قِيلَ لَهَا: أَتَأْذَنِينَ لِهَذَا يَدْخُلُ عَلَيْكِ، وَقَدْ قَالَ اللَّهُ: ﴿وَالَّذِي تَوَلَّى كِبْرَهُ مِنْهُمْ لَهُ عَذَابٌ عَظِيمٌ﴾ ؟ قَالَتْ: وأيُّ عَذَابٍ أَشَدُّ مِنَ الْعَمَى -وَكَانَ قَدْ ذَهَبَ بَصَرُهُ -لَعَلَّ اللَّهَ أَنْ يَجْعَلَ ذَلِكَ هُوَ الْعَذَابَ الْعَظِيمَ. ثُمَّ قَالَتْ: إِنَّهُ كَانَ يُنافحُ عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ.

وَفِي رِوَايَةٍ أَنَّهُ أَنْشَدَهَا عِنْدَمَا دَخَلَ عَلَيْهَا [شِعْرًا] يَمْتَدِحُهَا بِهِ، فَقَالَ:

حَصَان رَزَانٌ مَا تُزَنّ بِرِيبَةٍ ... وتُصْبح غَرْثَى مِنْ لُحوم الغَوَافل ...

فَقَالَتْ: أَمَّا أَنْتَ فَلَسْتَ كَذَلِكَ. وَفِي رِوَايَةٍ: لَكِنَّكَ لَسْتَ كَذَلِكَ .

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنَا الْحَسَنُ بْنُ قَزْعَة، حَدَّثَنَا سَلَمَةُ بْنُ عَلْقَمَةَ، حَدَّثَنَا دَاوُدُ، عَنْ عَامِرٍ، عَنْ عَائِشَةَ أَنَّهَا قَالَتْ: مَا سَمِعْتُ بِشَيْءٍ أَحْسَنَ مِنْ شِعْرِ حِسَّانَ، وَلَا تَمَثَّلْتُ بِهِ إِلَّا رَجَوْتُ لَهُ الْجَنَّةَ، قَوْلُهُ لِأَبِي سُفْيَانَ -يَعْنِي ابْنَ [الْحَارِثِ] بْنِ عَبْدِ الْمُطَّلِبِ -:

هَجَوتَ مُحَمَّدا فَأجبتُ عَنْهُ ... وَعندَ اللَّهِ فِي ذَاكَ الجزاءُ ...

فَإنَ أَبِي وَوَالده وعِرْضي ... لعرْضِ مُحَمَّد مِنْكُمْ وقاءُ ...

أَتَشْتُمُه، ولستَ لَه بكُفءٍ؟ ... فَشَرُّكُمَا لخَيْركُمَا الفدَاءُ ...

لِسَانِي صَارمٌ لَا عَيْبَ فِيه ... وَبَحْرِي لَا تُكَدِّرُه الدِّلاءُ ...

فَقِيلَ: يَا أُمَّ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ، أَلَيْسَ هَذَا لَغْوًا؟ قَالَتْ: لَا إِنَّمَا اللَّغْوُ مَا قِيلَ عِنْدَ النِّسَاءِ. قِيلَ: أَلَيْسَ اللَّهُ يَقُولُ ﴿وَالَّذِي تَوَلَّى كِبْرَهُ مِنْهُمْ لَهُ عَذَابٌ عَظِيمٌ﴾ ، قَالَتْ: أَلَيْسَ قَدْ أَصَابَهُ [عَذَابٌ] عَظِيمٌ؟ [أَلَيْسَ] قَدْ ذَهَبَ بَصَرُهُ وكُنِّع بِالسَّيْفِ؟ تَعْنِي: الضَّرْبَةَ الَّتِي ضَرَبَهُ إِيَّاهَا صَفْوَانُ بْنُ الْمُعَطَّلِ [السُّلَمِيُّ] ، حِينَ بَلَغَهُ عَنْهُ أَنَّهُ يَتَكَلَّمُ فِي ذَلِكَ، فَعَلَاهُ بِالسَّيْفِ، وَكَادَ أَنْ يَقْتُلَهُ .

---

## 24:12-13 — verses 12-13 (shared commentary)

### Translation

This is discipline from Allah directed to the believers concerning the case of Aisha, may Allah be pleased with her, when some of them indulged in that evil talk and what was mentioned regarding the affair of the slander (ifk). He said: {Lawla} meaning: why not, {when you heard it} that is, that speech, meaning what the Mother of the Believers was accused of, {did the believing men and believing women think good of themselves} that is, they should have measured that speech against themselves. For if it would not befit them, then the Mother of the Believers is more deserving of being cleared of it, by an even greater and more fitting reasoning.

It has been said that it was revealed concerning Abu Ayyub Khalid ibn Zayd al-Ansari and his wife, may Allah be pleased with both of them, as the imam Muhammad ibn Ishaq ibn Yasar said, from his father, from one of the men of Banu al-Najjar: that Abu Ayyub Khalid ibn Zayd's wife, Umm Ayyub, said to him: "O Abu Ayyub, do you not hear what the people are saying about Aisha, may Allah be pleased with her?" He said: "Yes, and that is a lie. Would you have done that, O Umm Ayyub?" She said: "No, by Allah, I would never have done it." He said: "Then Aisha, by Allah, is better than you." He said: When the Qur'an was revealed, Allah, Mighty and Majestic, mentioned those among the people of the slander who said what they said about the immoral act: {Indeed, those who came with the slander are a group among you} [al-Nur: 11], and that was Hassan and his companions who said what they said. Then He said: {Why did not, when you heard it, the believers think...} the verse, that is, as Abu Ayyub and his wife had said.

Muhammad ibn Umar al-Waqidi said: Ibn Abi Habiba narrated to me, from Dawud ibn al-Husayn, from Abu Sufyan, from Aflah the freedman of Abu Ayyub, that Umm Ayyub said to Abu Ayyub: "Do you not hear what the people are saying about Aisha?" He said: "Yes indeed, and that is a lie. Would you, O Umm Ayyub, have done that?" She said: "No, by Allah." He said: "Then Aisha, by Allah, is better than you." When the Qur'an was revealed and mentioned the people of the slander, Allah, Mighty and Majestic, said: {Why did not, when you heard it, the believing men and believing women think good of themselves and say, 'This is a clear falsehood'} meaning Abu Ayyub, when he said to Umm Ayyub what he said.

And it is also said that it was Ubayy ibn Ka'b who said it.

Concerning His saying: {did the believing men and believing women think good of themselves}, meaning: why did they not think well, for the Mother of the Believers is deserving and most worthy of that. This pertains to what is inward. {and say} that is, with their tongues, {this is a clear falsehood (ifk mubin)} meaning an open lie against the Mother of the Believers. For what occurred was not a matter of suspicion. This is because the Mother of the Believers' arrival, riding openly upon the mount of Safwan ibn al-Mu'attal at midday, with the entire army witnessing it, and the Messenger of Allah ﷺ present among them, had there been any suspicion in this matter, it would not have happened so openly, nor would the two of them have proceeded with such a thing in front of witnesses. Rather, had it been possible, it would have been done secretly and concealed. So it is established that what the people of the slander brought forth, that with which they accused the Mother of the Believers, is sheer falsehood, false speech, foul and immoral recklessness, and a losing bargain.

Allah, the Exalted, said: {Lawla} meaning: why did they not, {bring for it} that is, for what they claimed, {four witnesses} to testify to the truth of what they brought. {And since they did not bring the witnesses, then it is those, in the sight of Allah, who are the liars}, meaning: in Allah's judgment they are liars, sinners.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

هَذَا تَأْدِيبٌ مِنَ اللَّهِ لِلْمُؤْمِنِينَ فِي قَضِيَّةِ عَائِشَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهَا، حِينَ أَفَاضَ بَعْضُهُمْ في ذَلِكَ الْكَلَامِ السَّيِّئِ، وَمَا ذُكِرَ مِنْ شَأْنِ الْإِفْكِ، فَقَالَ: ﴿لَوْلا﴾ بِمَعْنَى: هَلَّا ﴿إِذْ سَمِعْتُمُوهُ﴾ أَيْ: ذَلِكَ الْكَلَامَ، أَيْ: الَّذِي رُمِيَتْ بِهِ أُمُّ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ ﴿ظَنَّ الْمُؤْمِنُونَ وَالْمُؤْمِنَاتُ بِأَنْفُسِهِمْ خَيْرًا﴾ أَيْ: قَاسُوا ذَلِكَ الْكَلَامَ عَلَى أَنْفُسِهِمْ، فَإِنْ كَانَ لَا يَلِيقُ بِهِمْ فَأُمُّ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ أَوْلَى بِالْبَرَاءَةِ مِنْهُ بِطَرِيقِ الْأَوْلَى وَالْأَحْرَى.

وَقَدْ قِيلَ: إِنَّهَا نَزَلَتْ فِي أَبِي أَيُّوبَ خَالِدِ بْنِ زَيْدٍ الْأَنْصَارِيِّ وَامْرَأَتِهِ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمَا، كَمَا قَالَ الْإِمَامُ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ بْنِ يَسَار، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنْ بَعْضِ رِجَالِ بَنِي النَّجَّارِ؛ أَنَّ أَبَا أَيُّوبَ خالدَ بْنَ زَيْدٍ قَالَتْ لَهُ امْرَأَتُهُ أُمُّ أَيُّوبَ: يَا أَبَا أَيُّوبَ، أَمَا تَسْمَعُ مَا يَقُولُ النَّاسُ فِي عَائِشَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهَا؟ قَالَ: نَعَمْ، وَذَلِكَ الْكَذِبُ. أكنتِ فَاعِلَةً ذَلِكَ يَا أُمَّ أَيُّوبَ؟ قَالَتْ: لَا وَاللَّهِ مَا كنتُ لِأَفْعَلَهُ. قَالَ: فَعَائِشَةُ وَاللَّهِ خَيْرٌ مِنْكِ. قَالَ: فَلَمَّا نَزَلَ الْقُرْآنُ ذَكَرَ اللَّهُ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، مَنْ قَالَ فِي الْفَاحِشَةِ مَا قَالَ مِنْ أَهْلِ الْإِفْكِ: ﴿إِنَّ الَّذِينَ جَاءُوا بِالإفْكِ عُصْبَةٌ مِنْكُمْ﴾ [النُّورِ: ١١] وَذَلِكَ حَسَّانُ وَأَصْحَابُهُ، الَّذِينَ قَالُوا مَا قَالُوا، ثُمَّ قَالَ: ﴿لَوْلا إِذْ سَمِعْتُمُوهُ ظَنَّ الْمُؤْمِنُونَ﴾ الْآيَةَ، أَيْ: كَمَا قَالَ أَبُو أَيُّوبَ وَصَاحِبَتُهُ .

وَقَالَ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ عُمَرَ الْوَاقِدَيُّ: حَدَّثَنِي ابْنُ أَبِي حَبِيبَةَ عَنْ دَاوُدَ بْنِ الْحُصَيْنِ، عَنْ أَبِي سُفْيَانَ، عَنْ أَفْلَحَ مَوْلَى أَبِي أَيُّوبَ، أَنَّ أُمَّ أَيُّوبَ قَالَتْ لِأَبِي أَيُّوبَ: أَلَا تَسْمَعُ مَا يَقُولُ النَّاسُ فِي عَائِشَةَ؟ قَالَ: بَلَى، وَذَلِكَ الْكَذِبُ، أَفَكُنْتِ يَا أُمَّ أَيُّوبَ [فَاعِلَةً ذَلِكَ] ؟ قَالَتْ: لَا وَاللَّهِ. قَالَ: فَعَائِشَةُ وَاللَّهِ خَيْرٌ مِنْكِ. فَلَمَّا نَزَلَ الْقُرْآنُ، وَذَكَرَ أَهْلَ الْإِفْكِ، قَالَ اللَّهُ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ: ﴿لَوْلا إِذْ سَمِعْتُمُوهُ ظَنَّ الْمُؤْمِنُونَ وَالْمُؤْمِنَاتُ بِأَنْفُسِهِمْ خَيْرًا وَقَالُوا هَذَا إِفْكٌ مُبِينٌ﴾ يَعْنِي: أَبَا أَيُّوبَ حِينَ قَالَ لِأُمِّ أَيُّوبَ مَا قَالَ.

وَيُقَالُ: إِنَّمَا قَالَهَا أُبَيُّ بْنُ كَعْبٍ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿ظَنَّ الْمُؤْمِنُونَ وَالْمُؤْمِنَاتُ بِأَنْفُسِهِمْ خَيْرًا﴾ أَيْ: هَلا ظَنُّوا الْخَيْرَ، فَإِنَّ أُمَّ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ أَهْلُهُ وَأَوْلَى بِهِ، هَذَا مَا يَتَعَلَّقُ بِالْبَاطِنِ، ﴿وَقَالُوا﴾ أَيْ: بِأَلْسِنَتِهِمْ ﴿هَذَا إِفْكٌ مُبِينٌ﴾ أَيْ: كَذِبٌ ظَاهِرٌ عَلَى أُمِّ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ، فَإِنَّ الَّذِي وَقَعَ لَمْ يَكُنْ رِيبَةً، وَذَلِكَ أَنَّ مَجِيءَ أُمِّ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ رَاكِبَةً جَهْرَة عَلَى رَاحِلَةِ صَفْوَانَ بْنِ الْمُعَطَّلِ فِي وَقْتِ الظَّهِيرَةِ، وَالْجَيْشُ بِكَمَالِهِ يُشَاهِدُونَ ذَلِكَ، وَرَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ بَيْنَ أَظْهُرِهُمْ، لَوْ كَانَ هَذَا الْأَمْرُ فِيهِ رِيبَةٌ لَمْ يَكُنْ هَكَذَا جَهْرَة، وَلَا كَانَا يُقدمان عَلَى مِثْلِ ذلك على رؤوس الْأَشْهَادِ، بَلْ كَانَ يَكُونُ هَذَا -لَوْ قُدر -خُفْيَةً مَسْتُورًا، فتعيَّن أَنَّ مَا جَاءَ بِهِ أَهْلُ الْإِفْكِ مِمَّا رَمَوا بِهِ أُمَّ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ هُوَ الْكَذِبُ الْبَحْتُ، وَالْقَوْلُ الزُّورُ، والرّعُونة الْفَاحِشَةُ [الْفَاجِرَةُ] وَالصَّفْقَةُ الْخَاسِرَةُ.

قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿لَوْلا﴾ أَيْ: هَلَّا ﴿جَاءُوا عَلَيْهِ﴾ أَيْ: عَلَى مَا قَالُوهُ ﴿بِأَرْبَعَةِ شُهَدَاءَ﴾ يَشْهَدُونَ عَلَى صِحَّةِ مَا جَاءُوا بِهِ ﴿فَإِذْ لَمْ يَأْتُوا بِالشُّهَدَاءِ فَأُولَئِكَ عِنْدَ اللَّهِ هُمُ الْكَاذِبُونَ﴾ أَيْ: فِي حُكْمِ الله كَذَبَةٌ فاجرون .

---

## 24:14-15 — verses 14-15 (shared commentary)

### Translation

[Allah] says: {And were it not for the favor of Allah upon you and His mercy in this world and the Hereafter}, O you who plunged into the affair of A'ishah, in that He accepted your repentance and your turning back to Him in this world, and pardoned you because of your faith with regard to the abode of the Hereafter, {a great punishment would have touched you for what you engaged in}, concerning the matter of the slander. This applies to those who possessed faith, for whose sake Allah granted them repentance to Him, such as Mistah, Hassan, and Hamnah bint Jahsh, the sister of Zaynab bint Jahsh. As for those among the hypocrites who plunged into it, such as Abdullah ibn Ubayy ibn Salul and his like, they are not intended in this verse, because they possessed no faith or righteous deed that would equal this or oppose it. This is the pattern of every threat that comes attached to a specific act: it is unqualified, conditioned upon the absence of repentance, or upon the absence of a corresponding righteous deed that balances it out or outweighs it.

Then the Almighty says: {when you received it with your tongues}. Mujahid and Sa'id ibn Jubayr said: meaning, some of you related it from others, one of you saying, "I heard it from so-and-so," and "so-and-so said such and such," and another mentioning something else.

Others read it as "idh talqunahu bi-alsinatikum" (with a different vocalization). In Sahih al-Bukhari it is reported from A'ishah that she used to recite it this way, and she would say: it is from "walq al-qawl" (fabricated speech), meaning the lie that its author persists in. The Arabs say: "so-and-so persisted (walaqa) in his journey" when he continued in it without stopping. The first reading is the more well known one, and the majority follow it, but the second reading is transmitted from the Mother of the Believers, A'ishah.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] from A'ishah, that she used to recite it as "idh talqunahu," saying: it is only "walq al-qawl," and walq means lying. Ibn Abi Mulaykah said: she knew it better than anyone else.

His saying: {and you say with your mouths what you have no knowledge of}, meaning: you say what you do not know.

Then the Almighty says: {and you consider it a small matter, while it is with Allah tremendous}, meaning: you say what you say concerning the Mother of the Believers and consider it a light and easy matter. Yet even if she were not the wife of the Prophet ﷺ, it would not have been a small matter, so how much more so when she is the wife of the unlettered Prophet, the Seal of the Prophets and the master of the messengers. It is a tremendous thing before Allah that such a thing be said about the wife of His Messenger. Allah is jealous over this, and He, glorified and exalted is He, does not allow such a thing to befall the wife of any of His prophets. Far be it, and by no means, and since that was not the case with any prophet's wife, how could it be so concerning the mistress of the women of the prophets, and the wife of the master of the children of Adam absolutely, in this world and the Hereafter? For this reason the Almighty said: {and you consider it a small matter, while it is with Allah tremendous}. And in the two Sahihs: "Indeed a man may speak a word that provokes Allah's wrath, not knowing how far it will reach, and it casts him into the Fire a distance farther than that between heaven and earth." And in another version: "not giving it any thought."

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ [اللَّهُ] : ﴿وَلَوْلا فَضْلُ اللَّهِ عَلَيْكُمْ وَرَحْمَتُهُ فِي الدُّنْيَا وَالآخِرَةِ﴾ أَيُّهَا الْخَائِضُونَ فِي شَأْنِ عَائِشَةَ، بِأَنْ قَبِلَ تَوْبَتَكُمْ وَإِنَابَتَكُمْ إِلَيْهِ فِي الدُّنْيَا، وَعَفَا عَنْكُمْ لِإِيمَانِكُمْ بِالنِّسْبَةِ إِلَى الدَّارِ الْآخِرَةِ، ﴿لَمَسَّكُمْ فِي مَا أَفَضْتُمْ فِيهِ﴾ ، مِنْ قَضِيَّةِ الْإِفْكِ، ﴿عَذَابٌ عَظِيمٌ﴾ . وَهَذَا فَيَمَنْ عِنْدَهُ إِيمَانٌ رَزَقَهُ اللَّهُ بِسَبَبِهِ التَّوْبَةَ إِلَيْهِ، كمِسْطَح، وَحَسَّانَ، وحَمْنةَ بِنْتِ جَحْشٍ، أُخْتِ زينبَ بِنْتِ جَحْشٍ. فَأَمَّا مَنْ خَاضَ فِيهِ مِنَ الْمُنَافِقِينَ كَعَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ أُبَيِّ بْنِ سَلُولٍ وَأَضْرَابِهِ، فَلَيْسَ أُولَئِكَ مُرَادِينَ فِي هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ؛ لِأَنَّهُ لَيْسَ عِنْدَهُمْ مِنَ الْإِيمَانِ وَالْعَمَلِ الصَّالِحِ مَا يُعَادِلُ هَذَا وَلَا مَا يُعَارِضُهُ. وَهَكَذَا شَأْنُ مَا يَرِدُ مِنَ الْوَعِيدِ عَلَى فِعْلٍ مُعَيَّنٍ، يَكُونُ مُطْلَقًا مَشْرُوطًا بِعَدَمِ التَّوْبَةِ، أَوْ مَا يُقَابِلُهُ مِنْ عَمَل صَالِحٍ يوازنُه أَوْ يَرجح عَلَيْهِ.

ثُمَّ قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿إِذْ تَلَقَّوْنَهُ بِأَلْسِنَتِكُمْ﴾ قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ، وَسَعِيدُ بْنُ جُبَيْرٍ: أَيْ: يَرْوِيهِ بَعْضُكُمْ عَنْ بَعْضٍ، يَقُولُ هَذَا: سَمِعْتُهُ مِنْ فُلَانٍ، وَقَالَ فَلَانٌ كَذَا، وَذَكَرَ بَعْضُهُمْ كَذَا.

وَقَرَأَ آخَرُونَ " إِذْ تَلقُونَه بِأَلْسِنَتِكُمْ ". وَفِي صَحِيحِ الْبُخَارِيِّ عَنْ عَائِشَةَ: أَنَّهَا كَانَتْ تَقْرَؤُهَا كَذَلِكَ وَتَقُولُ: هُوَ مِنْ وَلَق الْقَوْلِ. يَعْنِي: الْكَذِبَ الَّذِي يَسْتَمِرُّ صَاحِبُهُ عَلَيْهِ ، تَقُولُ الْعَرَبَ: وَلَق فُلَانٌ فِي السَّيْرِ: إِذَا اسْتَمَرَّ فِيهِ ، وَالْقِرَاءَةُ الْأُولَى أَشْهَرُ، وَعَلَيْهَا الْجُمْهُورُ، وَلَكِنَّ الثَّانِيَةَ مَرْويَّة عَنْ أُمِّ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ عَائِشَةَ.

قَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حدَّثنا أَبُو سَعِيدٍ الأشَجّ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو أُسَامَةَ، عَنْ نَافِعِ بْنِ عُمَرَ ، عَنِ ابْنِ أَبِي مُلَيْكَةَ، [عَنْ عَائِشَةَ أَنَّهَا كَانَتْ تَقْرَأُ: " إِذْ تَلقُونَه " وَتَقُولُ: إِنَّمَا هُوَ وَلَق الْقَوْلِ -والوَلَق: الْكَذِبُ. قَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي مُلَيْكَةَ ] : هِيَ أَعْلَمُ بِهِ مِنْ غَيْرِهَا.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَتَقُولُونَ بِأَفْوَاهِكُمْ مَا لَيْسَ لَكُمْ بِهِ عِلْمٌ﴾ أَيْ: تَقُولُونَ مَا لَا تَعْلَمُونَ.

ثُمَّ قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَتَحْسَبُونَهُ هَيِّنًا وَهُوَ عِنْدَ اللَّهِ عَظِيمٌ﴾ أَيْ: تَقُولُونَ مَا تَقُولُونَ فِي شَأْنِ أُمَّ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ، وَتَحْسَبُونَ ذَلِكَ يَسِيرًا [سَهْلًا] وَلَوْ لَمْ تَكُنْ زَوْجَةَ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ لَمَا كَانَ هَيِّنا، فَكَيْفَ وَهِيَ زَوْجَةُ النَّبِيِّ الْأُمِّيِّ، خَاتَمِ الْأَنْبِيَاءِ وَسَيِّدِ الْمُرْسَلِينَ، فَعَظِيمٌ عِنْدَ اللَّهِ أَنْ يُقَالَ فِي زَوْجَةِ رَسُولِهِ مَا قِيلَ! اللَّهُ يَغَارُ لِهَذَا، وَهُوَ سُبْحَانَهُ وَتَعَالَى، لَا يُقَدِّر عَلَى زَوْجَةِ نَبِيٍّ مِنْ أَنْبِيَائِهِ ذَلِكَ، حَاشَا وكَلا وَلَمَّا [لَمْ يَكُنْ ذَلِكَ] فَكَيْفَ يَكُونُ هَذَا فِي سَيِّدَةِ نِسَاءِ الْأَنْبِيَاءِ، وَزَوْجَةِ سَيِّدِ وَلَدِ آدَمَ عَلَى الْإِطْلَاقِ فِي الدُّنْيَا وَالْآخِرَةِ؟! وَلِهَذَا قَالَ تَعَالَى ﴿وَتَحْسَبُونَهُ هَيِّنًا وَهُوَ عِنْدَ اللَّهِ عَظِيمٌ﴾ ، وَفِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ: إِنَّ الرَّجُلَ لَيَتَكَلَّمُ بِالْكَلِمَةِ مِنْ سَخَط اللَّهِ، لَا يَدْرِي مَا تَبْلُغ، يَهْوِي بِهَا فِي النَّارِ أبْعَد مَا بَيْنَ السَّمَاءِ وَالْأَرْضِ" وَفِي رِوَايَةٍ: "لَا يُلْقِي لَهَا بَالًا" .

---

## 24:16-18 — verses 16-18 (shared commentary)

### Translation

This is another instruction following the first one: the command to think well, meaning that if something unbecoming is mentioned regarding the matter of the chosen one (the wife of the Prophet), it is all the more fitting that one should think well of them, and that one should not let his own soul feel otherwise. Then if something of that clings to a person, whether as a whispering (waswasa) or a mere fancy, he should not speak it aloud, for the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Indeed Allah has overlooked for my nation what their souls speak to them of, so long as they do not say it or act upon it." Both [Bukhari and Muslim] narrated it in the two Sahihs.

Allah, Exalted is He, said: {And why, when you heard it, did you not say, "It is not for us to speak of this"} meaning: it was not fitting for us to utter this speech at all, nor to mention it to anyone. {Glory be to You, this is a great slander} meaning: exalted and glorified is Allah above the idea that such speech should be said about the wife of [His Prophet and] His Messenger, the spouse of His close friend.

Then He, Exalted is He, said: {Allah admonishes you never to return to the like of it} meaning: Allah forbids you, warning you, that anything resembling this should ever occur from you again, that is, in what is to come. For this reason He said: {if you are believers} meaning: if you believe in Allah and His law, and revere His Messenger ﷺ. As for one characterized by disbelief, that person has another ruling altogether.

Then He said: {And Allah makes clear to you the signs} meaning: He explains to you the rulings of the sacred law and the wisdoms of the divine decree. {And Allah is All-Knowing, All-Wise} meaning: Knowing of what benefits His servants, Wise in His legislation and His decree.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

هَذَا تَأْدِيبٌ آخَرُ بَعْدَ الْأَوَّلِ: الْأمْرُ بِالظَّنِّ خَيْرًا أَيْ: إِذَا ذُكِرَ مَا لَا يَلِيقُ مِنَ الْقَوْلِ فِي شَأْنِ الْخِيَرَةِ فَأَوْلَى يَنْبَغِي الظَّنُّ بِهِمْ خَيْرًا، وَأَلَّا يُشْعِرَ نَفْسَهُ سِوَى ذَلِكَ، ثُمَّ إِنْ عَلِق بِنَفْسِهِ شَيْءٌ مِنْ ذَلِكَ -وَسْوَسَةً أَوْ خَيَالًا -فَلَا يَنْبَغِي أَنْ يَتَكَلَّمَ بِهِ، فَإِنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَ: "إِنَّ اللَّهَ تَجَاوَزَ لِأُمَّتِي عَمَّا حدَّثت بِهِ أَنْفُسَهَا مَا لَمْ تَقُلْ أَوْ تَعْمَلْ" أَخْرَجَاهُ فِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ .

وَقَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلَوْلا إِذْ سَمِعْتُمُوهُ قُلْتُمْ مَا يَكُونُ لَنَا أَنْ نَتَكَلَّمَ بِهَذَا﴾ أَيْ: مَا يَنْبَغِي لَنَا أَنْ نَتَفَوَّهَ بِهَذَا الْكَلَامِ وَلَا نَذْكُرَهُ لِأَحَدٍ ﴿سُبْحَانَكَ هَذَا بُهْتَانٌ عَظِيمٌ﴾ أَيْ: سُبْحَانَ اللَّهِ أَنْ يُقَالَ هَذَا الْكَلَامُ عَلَى زَوْجَةِ [نَبِيِّهِ وَ] رَسُولِهِ وَحَلِيلَةِ خَلِيلِهِ.
