وَكَذَا رَوَاهُ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ، عَنْ هُشَيْم، عَنْ يُونُسَ بْنِ عُبَيْدٍ، بِهِ. وَرَوَاهُ أبو داود والترمذي وَالنَّسَائِيُّ، مِنْ حَدِيثِهِ أَيْضًا . وَقَالَ التِّرْمِذِيُّ: حَسَنٌ صَحِيحٌ. وَفِي رِوَايَةٍ لِبَعْضِهِمْ: فَقَالَ: "أطرقْ بَصَرَكَ"، يَعْنِي: انْظُرْ إِلَى الْأَرْضِ. وَالصَّرْفُ أَعَمُّ؛ فَإِنَّهُ قَدْ يَكُونُ إِلَى الْأَرْضِ، وَإِلَى جِهَةٍ أُخْرَى، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

وَقَالَ أَبُو دَاوُدَ: حَدَّثَنَا إِسْمَاعِيلُ بْنُ مُوسَى الفَزَاري، حَدَّثَنَا شَريك، عَنْ أَبِي رَبِيعَةَ الْإِيَادِيِّ، عَنْ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ بُرَيْدة، عَنْ أَبِيهِ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ لَعَلِيٍّ: "يَا عَلِيُّ، لَا تُتْبِعِ النَّظْرَةَ النظرةَ، فَإِنَّ لَكَ الْأُولَى وَلَيْسَ لَكَ الْآخِرَةُ"

وَرَوَاهُ التِّرْمِذِيُّ مِنْ حَدِيثِ شَرِيكٍ ، وَقَالَ: غَرِيبٌ، لَا نَعْرِفُهُ إِلَّا مِنْ حَدِيثِهِ.

وَفِي الصَّحِيحِ عَنْ أَبِي سَعِيدٍ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "إِيَّاكُمْ وَالْجُلُوسَ عَلَى الطُّرُقَاتِ". قَالُوا: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، لَا بُدَّ لَنَا مِنْ مَجَالِسِنَا، نَتَحَدَّثُ فِيهَا. فَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "إِنْ أَبَيْتُمْ، فَأَعْطُوا الطَّرِيقَ حقَّه". قَالُوا: وَمَا حَقُّ الطَّرِيقِ يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ؟ قَالَ: "غَضُّ الْبَصَرِ، وكَفُّ الْأَذَى، وَرَدُّ السَّلَامِ، وَالْأَمْرُ بِالْمَعْرُوفِ، وَالنَّهْيُ عَنِ الْمُنْكَرِ" .

وَقَالَ أَبُو الْقَاسِمِ الْبَغَوِيُّ: حَدَّثَنَا طَالُوتُ بْنُ عَبَّادٍ، حَدَّثَنَا فَضْلُ بْنُ جُبَيْرٍ: سَمِعْتُ أَبَا أُمَامَةَ يَقُولُ: سَمِعْتُ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَقُولُ: "اكْفُلُوا لِي بِستّ أَكْفُلْ لَكُمْ بِالْجَنَّةِ: إِذَا حدَّث أَحَدُكُمْ فَلَا يَكْذِبْ، وَإِذَا اؤْتُمِنَ فَلَا يَخُن، وَإِذَا وَعَد فَلَا يُخْلِفْ. وغُضُّوا أَبْصَارَكُمْ، وكُفُّوا أَيْدِيَكُمْ، وَاحْفَظُوا فُرُوجَكُمْ" .

وَفِي صَحِيحِ الْبُخَارِيِّ: "مَنْ يَكْفُلْ لِي مَا بَيْنَ لَحْيَيه وَمَا بَيْنَ رِجْلَيْهِ، أَكْفُلْ لَهُ الْجَنَّةَ" .

وَقَالَ عَبْدُ الرَّزَّاقِ: أَنْبَأَنَا مَعْمَر، عَنْ أَيُّوبَ، عَنِ ابْنِ سِيرِينَ، عَنْ عُبَيْدَةَ قَالَ: كُلُّ مَا عُصي اللَّهُ بِهِ، فَهُوَ كَبِيرَةٌ. وَقَدْ ذَكَرَ الطَّرْفين فَقَالَ: ﴿قُلْ لِلْمُؤْمِنِينَ يَغُضُّوا مِنْ أَبْصَارِهِمْ﴾ .

وَلَمَّا كَانَ النَّظَرُ دَاعِيَةً إِلَى فَسَادِ الْقَلْبِ، كَمَا قَالَ بَعْضُ السَّلَفِ: "النَّظَرُ سِهَامُ سُمٍّ إِلَى الْقَلْبِ"؛ وَلِذَلِكَ أَمَرَ اللَّهُ بِحِفْظِ الْفُرُوجِ كَمَا أَمَرَ بِحِفْظِ الْأَبْصَارِ الَّتِي هِيَ بَوَاعِثُ إِلَى ذَلِكَ، فَقَالَ: ﴿قُلْ لِلْمُؤْمِنِينَ يَغُضُّوا مِنْ أَبْصَارِهِمْ وَيَحْفَظُوا فُرُوجَهُمْ﴾ . وحفظُ الفَرج تَارَةً يَكُونُ بِمَنْعِهِ مِنَ الزِّنَى، كَمَا قَالَ ﴿وَالَّذِينَ هُمْ لِفُرُوجِهِمْ حَافِظُونَ إِلا عَلَى أَزْوَاجِهِمْ أوْ مَا مَلَكَتْ أَيْمَانُهُمْ فَإِنَّهُمْ غَيْرُ مَلُومِينَ﴾ [الْمَعَارِجِ:٢٩، ٣٠] وَتَارَةً يَكُونُ بِحِفْظِهِ مِنَ النَّظَرِ إِلَيْهِ، كَمَا جَاءَ فِي الْحَدِيثِ في مسند أحمد والسنن: احْفَظْ عَوْرَتَكَ، إِلَّا مِنْ زَوْجَتِكَ أَوْ مَا مَلَكَتْ يَمِينُكَ" .

﴿ذَلِكَ أَزْكَى لَهُمْ﴾ أَيْ: أَطْهَرُ لِقُلُوبِهِمْ وَأَنْقَى لِدِينِهِمْ، كَمَا قِيلَ: "مَنْ حَفِظَ بَصَرَهُ، أَوْرَثَهُ اللَّهُ نُورًا فِي بَصِيرَتِهِ". وَيُرْوَى: "فِي قَلْبِهِ".

وَقَدْ قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا عَتَّابٌ، حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ الْمُبَارَكِ، أَخْبَرَنَا يَحْيَى بْنُ أَيُّوبَ، عَنْ عُبَيْد اللَّهِ بْنِ زَحْر، عَنْ عَلِيِّ بْنِ يَزِيدَ، عَنِ الْقَاسِمِ، عَنْ أَبِي أُمَامَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ قَالَ: "مَا مِنْ مُسْلِمٍ يَنْظُرُ إِلَى مَحَاسِنِ امْرَأَةٍ [أَوَّلَ مَرّة] ثُمَّ يَغُضّ بَصَرَهُ، إِلَّا أَخْلَفَ اللَّهُ لَهُ عِبَادَةً يَجِدُ حَلَاوَتَهَا" .

ورُوي هَذَا مَرْفُوعًا عَنِ ابْنِ عُمَرَ، وَحُذَيْفَةَ، وَعَائِشَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمْ وَلَكِنْ فِي إِسْنَادِهَا ضَعْفٌ، إِلَّا أَنَّهَا فِي التَّرْغِيبِ، وَمِثْلُهُ يُتَسَامَحُ فِيهِ.

وَفِي الطَّبَرَانِيِّ مِنْ طَرِيقِ عُبَيْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ زَحْر،، عَنْ عَلِيِّ بْنِ يَزِيدَ، عَنِ الْقَاسِمِ، عَنْ أبي أُمَامَةَ مَرْفُوعًا: "لَتغضُنَّ أَبْصَارَكُمْ، وَلَتَحْفَظُنَّ فُرُوجَكُمْ، ولتقيمُنّ وُجُوهَكُمْ -أَوْ: لَتُكْسَفَنَّ وُجُوهُكُمْ" .

وَقَالَ الطَّبَرَانِيُّ: حَدَّثَنَا أَحْمَدُ بْنُ زُهَيْرٍ التُّسْتُري قَالَ: قَرَأْنَا عَلَى مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ حَفْصِ بْنِ عُمَرَ الضَّرِيرِ الْمُقْرِئِ، حَدَّثَنَا يَحْيَى بْنُ أَبِي بُكَيْر، حَدَّثَنَا هُرَيْم بْنُ سُفْيَانَ، عَنْ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنِ إِسْحَاقَ، عَنِ الْقَاسِمُ بْنُ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ مَسْعُودٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "إِنَّ النَّظَرَ سَهْمٌ مِنْ سِهَامِ إِبْلِيسَ مَسْمُومٌ، مَنْ تَرَكَهُ مَخَافَتِي، أَبْدَلْتُهُ إِيمَانًا يَجِدُ حَلَاوَتَهُ فِي قَلْبِهِ" .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿إِنَّ اللَّهَ خَبِيرٌ بِمَا يَصْنَعُونَ﴾ ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿يَعْلَمُ خَائِنَةَ الأعْيُنِ وَمَا تُخْفِي الصُّدُورُ﴾ [غَافِرٍ:١٩] .

وَفِي الصَّحِيحِ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "كُتِبَ عَلَى ابْنِ آدَمَ حَظّه مِنَ الزِّنَى، أدرَكَ ذَلِكَ لَا مَحَالَةَ. فَزنى الْعَيْنَيْنِ: النَّظَرُ. وَزِنَى اللِّسَانِ: النطقُ. وَزِنَى الْأُذُنَيْنِ: الِاسْتِمَاعُ. وَزِنَى الْيَدَيْنِ: الْبَطْشُ. وَزِنَى الرِّجْلَيْنِ: الْخَطْيُ. وَالنَّفْسُ تمَنّى وَتَشْتَهِي، وَالْفَرْجُ يُصَدِّق ذَلِكَ أَوْ يُكذبه".

رَوَاهُ الْبُخَارِيُّ تَعْلِيقًا، وَمُسْلِمٌ مُسْنَدًا مِنْ وَجْهٍ آخَرَ بِنَحْوِ مَا تَقَدَّمَ.

وَقَدْ قَالَ كَثِيرٌ مِنَ السَّلَفِ: إِنَّهُمْ كَانُوا ينهَون أَنْ يحدَّ الرَّجُلُ بَصَره إِلَى الْأَمْرَدِ. وَقَدْ شَدَّد كَثِيرٌ مِنْ أَئِمَّةِ الصُّوفِيَّةِ فِي ذَلِكَ، وحَرَّمه طَائِفَةٌ مِنْ أَهْلِ الْعِلْمِ، لِمَا فِيهِ مِنَ الِافْتِتَانِ، وشَدّد آخَرُونَ فِي ذَلِكَ كَثِيرًا جَدًّا.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي الدُّنْيَا: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو سَعِيدٍ الْمَدَنِيُّ ، حَدَّثَنَا عُمَرُ بْنُ سَهْلٍ الْمَازِنِيُّ، حَدَّثَنِي عُمَرُ بْنُ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ صُهْبَان، حَدَّثَنِي صَفْوَانُ بْنُ سُلَيْمٍ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "كُلُّ عَيْنٍ بَاكِيَةٌ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ، إِلَّا عَيْنًا غَضّت عَنْ مَحَارِمِ اللَّهِ، وَعَيْنًا سهِرت فِي سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ، وَعَيْنًا يَخْرُجُ مِنْهَا مِثْلُ رَأْسِ الذُّبَابِ، مِنْ خَشْيَةِ اللَّهِ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ" .

---

## 24:31 — verse 31

### Translation

This is a command from Allah, Exalted is He, to believing women, and a manifestation of His jealous protectiveness over their husbands, His believing servants, and a distinguishing of them from the character of the women of pre-Islamic ignorance (Jahiliyyah) and the conduct of the polytheist women.

The occasion of the revelation of this verse was what Muqatil ibn Hayyan mentioned. He said: it has reached us, and Allah knows best, that Jabir ibn Abdullah al-Ansari reported that Asma bint Murshidah was in a dwelling of hers among the Banu Haritha, and women began entering upon her without wrapping their lower garments, so that what was on their legs of anklets showed, and their chests and the locks of their hair showed. Asma said: "How ugly this is." So Allah revealed: {And tell the believing women to lower their gaze and guard their private parts} and the rest of the verse.

His saying, Exalted is He: {And tell the believing women to lower their gaze}, meaning: from that which Allah has forbidden them to look at, namely other than their husbands. For this reason many scholars have held that it is not permissible for a woman to look at unrelated men, whether with desire or without desire at all. Many of them cited as evidence what Abu Dawud and al-Tirmidhi narrated from the hadith of al-Zuhri, from Nabhan, the freed slave of Umm Salamah, who reported that Umm Salamah told him that she was with the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, along with Maymunah. She said: while we were with him, Ibn Umm Maktum came and entered upon him, and this was after we had been commanded regarding the hijab. The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Veil yourselves from him." I said: "O Messenger of Allah, is he not blind, unable to see us or recognize us?" The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Are you two blind? Do you not see him?"

Al-Tirmidhi then said: this is a hasan sahih (sound and authentic) hadith.

Other scholars held that it is permissible for women to look at unrelated men without desire, as is established in the authentic collection: that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ used to watch the Abyssinians as they played with their spears on the day of the festival in the mosque, while Aisha, Mother of the Believers, watched them from behind him, and he shielded her from them, until she grew tired and went back.

Regarding His saying: {and guard their private parts}, Sa'id ibn Jubayr said: from indecent acts. Qatadah and Sufyan said: from that which is not permissible for them. Muqatil said: from fornication. Abu al-Aliyah said: every verse revealed in the Qur'an mentioning the guarding of private parts refers to fornication, except this verse, {and guard their private parts}, which means that no one should see them.

He said: {and not display their adornment except what is apparent of it}, meaning: they should not display any adornment to unrelated men, except what cannot possibly be concealed.

Ibn Mas'ud said: such as the outer wrap and garments, meaning according to what the women of the Arabs used to practice, of the head-covering that draped over their clothes, and what shows from the lower parts of the garments, there being no blame upon her in that, because this cannot possibly be concealed. A similar example in women's dress is what shows of the lower wrap, and what cannot be concealed. Holding the view of Ibn Mas'ud were al-Hasan, Ibn Sirin, Abu al-Jawza, Ibrahim al-Nakha'i, and others.

Al-A'mash reported from Sa'id ibn Jubayr, from Ibn Abbas: {and not display their adornment except what is apparent of it}, he said: her face, her two hands, and the ring. Similar has been reported from Ibn Umar, Ata, Ikrimah, Sa'id ibn Jubayr, Abu al-Sha'tha, al-Dahhak, Ibrahim al-Nakha'i, and others. It is possible that this is an explanation of the adornment which they were forbidden to display, as Abu Ishaq al-Sabi'i reported from Abu al-Ahwas, from Abdullah, who said regarding His statement: {and not display their adornment}: the adornment is the earring, the bracelet, the anklet, and the necklace. In another report from him, with this same chain, he said: adornment is of two kinds: an adornment that no one sees except the husband, namely the ring and the bracelet, and an adornment that unrelated men may see, which is what is apparent of the garments.

Al-Zuhri said: nothing should appear to these people whom Allah has named, among those for whom it is not permissible, except the bracelets, the head-coverings, and the earrings, without uncovering, whereas for people in general, nothing of hers should appear except the rings.

Malik reported from al-Zuhri: {except what is apparent of it} means the ring and the anklet.

It is possible that Ibn Abbas and those who followed him intended to explain "what is apparent of it" as the face and the two hands, and this is what is well known among the majority. Support for this may be found in the hadith narrated by Abu Dawud in his Sunan:

[chain] ... from Aisha, may Allah be pleased with her, that Asma bint Abi Bakr entered upon the Prophet ﷺ wearing thin garments, and he turned away from her and said: "O Asma, when a woman reaches the age of menstruation, it is not proper that anything of hers be seen except this," and he pointed to his face and his two hands.

However, Abu Dawud and Abu Hatim al-Razi said: this is mursal (a report with a missing link); Khalid ibn Durayk did not hear from Aisha. And Allah knows best.

His saying: {and let them draw their head-coverings over their bosoms}, meaning: the head-coverings that are made with folds hanging down over the chests of women, to conceal what is beneath them of the chest and collarbone area, so as to differ from the practice of the women of the Age of Ignorance. For they did not do that; rather, a woman would pass among men with her chest uncovered, nothing concealing it, and sometimes she would show her neck, the locks of her hair, and the earrings in her ears. So Allah commanded the believing women to cover themselves in their appearance and their conduct, as Allah, Exalted is He, said: {O Prophet, tell your wives and your daughters and the women of the believers to draw their outer garments close around themselves; that is more suitable, so that they will be known and not molested} [al-Ahzab: 59]. And He said in this noble verse: {and let them draw their head-coverings over their bosoms}. Khumur (head-coverings) is the plural of khimar, which is that with which one covers, that is, covers the head; it is what people call the maqani' (head-veils).

Sa'id ibn Jubayr said: {and let them draw} means: and let them fasten tightly {their head-coverings over their bosoms}, meaning: over the neck and chest, so that nothing of it is seen.

Al-Bukhari said, and Ahmad ibn Shabib said: [chain] ... from Aisha, may Allah be pleased with her, who said: may Allah have mercy on the earliest women emigrants; when Allah revealed {and let them draw their head-coverings over their bosoms}, they tore their outer wraps and made head-coverings from them.

He also said: [chain] ... from Safiyyah bint Shaybah, that Aisha, may Allah be pleased with her, used to say: when this verse was revealed, {and let them draw their head-coverings over their bosoms}, they took their lower wraps and tore them from the edges, and made head-coverings from them.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] ... from Safiyyah bint Shaybah, who said: while we were with Aisha, we mentioned the women of Quraysh and their excellence. Aisha, may Allah be pleased with her, said: the women of Quraysh indeed have excellence, but by Allah, I have not seen any better than the women of the Ansar in strength of belief in the Book of Allah and faith in what was revealed. When Surat al-Nur was revealed, {and let them draw their head-coverings over their bosoms}, their men returned to them reciting to them what Allah had revealed to them concerning it, each man reciting it to his wife, his daughter, his sister, and every relative of his. And there was not a woman among them but she got up to her patterned lower wrap and covered her head with it, out of belief and faith in what Allah had revealed of His Book. So they appeared behind the Messenger of Allah ﷺ at the dawn prayer wearing head-coverings, as though on their heads were crows.

Abu Dawud also narrated it through another route, from Safiyyah bint Shaybah, with the same content.

Ibn Jarir said: [chain] ... from Aisha, that she said: may Allah have mercy on the earliest women emigrants; when Allah revealed {and let them draw their head-coverings over their bosoms}, they tore the thickest of their lower wraps and made head-coverings from them. Abu Dawud also narrated it from the hadith of Ibn Wahb, with the same content.

His saying: {and not display their adornment except to their husbands}, meaning their spouses, {or their fathers, or their husbands' fathers, or their sons, or their husbands' sons, or their brothers, or their brothers' sons, or their sisters' sons}: all of these are mahram (unmarriageable relatives) of the woman, to whom it is permissible for her to display her adornment, but without excess or ostentatious display.

Ibn al-Mundhir said: Musa (meaning Ibn Harun) narrated to us, Abu Bakr (meaning Ibn Abi Shaybah) narrated to us, Affan narrated to us, Hammad ibn Salamah narrated to us, Dawud informed us, from al-Sha'bi and Ikrimah regarding this verse: {And let them not display their adornment except to their husbands, or their fathers, or the fathers of their husbands} until he finished it. He said: He did not mention the paternal uncle nor the maternal uncle, because they describe women to their own sons, and a woman does not remove her head covering in front of her paternal or maternal uncle. As for the husband, all of that is for his sake, so she adorns herself for him in a way that does not occur in the presence of anyone else.

Regarding His saying: {or their women}, meaning: she also displays her adornment to Muslim women, but not to the women of the dhimmis (protected non-Muslim subjects), lest they describe her to their men. Although this is forbidden with respect to all women, it is more severe in the case of dhimmi women, since nothing restrains them from that, whereas the Muslim woman knows that this is forbidden and so refrains from it. The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "A woman should not touch another woman and then describe her to her husband as though he were looking at her." Both of them (al-Bukhari and Muslim) recorded it in the two Sahihs, from Ibn Mas'ud.

Sa'id ibn Mansur said in his Sunan: Isma'il ibn Ayyash narrated to us, from Hisham ibn al-Ghaz, from Ubadah ibn Nusayy, from his father, from al-Harith ibn Qays, who said: The Commander of the Faithful, Umar ibn al-Khattab, wrote to Abu Ubaydah: "To proceed: it has reached me that some Muslim women enter the bathhouses along with the women of the polytheists. So forbid those under your authority from this, for it is not lawful for a woman who believes in Allah and the Last Day to let anyone look at her private area except those of her own faith."

Mujahid said regarding His saying {or their women}: their women are the Muslim women; the polytheist women are not among "their women," and it is not permissible for a Muslim woman to uncover herself in front of a polytheist woman.

Abd narrated in his Tafsir, from al-Kalbi, from Abu Salih, from Ibn Abbas, regarding {or their women}: he said: they are the Muslim women; she should not display it to a Jewish or Christian woman. And that (adornment referred to) is the neck ornament, the earring, and the sash, and whatever it is not lawful for anyone to see except a mahram (unmarriageable relative).

Sa'id narrated: Jarir narrated to us, from Layth, from Mujahid, who said: A Muslim woman should not remove her head covering in front of a polytheist woman, because Allah, Exalted is He, says: {or their women}, and she is not among "their women."

And from Makhul and Ubadah ibn Nusayy: they both disliked that a Christian, Jewish, or Zoroastrian woman should kiss a Muslim woman.

As for what Ibn Abi Hatim narrated: Ali ibn al-Husayn narrated to us, Abu Umayr narrated to us, Damrah narrated to us, who said: Ibn Ata said, from his father: "When the Companions of the Prophet ﷺ came to Jerusalem, the midwives of their women were Jewish and Christian women." This, if authentic, is to be understood as applying to a state of necessity, or that it falls under the category of what is done out of humble need, and in any case it does not necessarily involve uncovering the private area. And Allah knows best.

Regarding His saying: {or those whom their right hands possess}, Ibn Jurayj said: meaning from among the women of the polytheists, so it is permissible for her to display her adornment to her even if she is a polytheist, because she is her slave. This is the view held by Sa'id ibn al-Musayyab. The majority said: rather, it is permissible for her to display it to her slaves, whether male or female, and they cited as evidence the hadith narrated by Abu Dawud:

Muhammad ibn Isa narrated to us, Abu Jumay' Salim ibn Dinar narrated to us, from Thabit, from Anas: that the Prophet ﷺ brought Fatimah a slave whom he had given to her. He said: Fatimah was wearing a garment such that when she covered her head with it, it did not reach her feet, and when she covered her feet with it, it did not reach her head. When the Prophet ﷺ saw what she was struggling with, he said: "There is no harm upon you; he is only your father and your slave boy."

Al-Hafiz Ibn Asakir mentioned in his history, in the biography of Hudayj the eunuch, the freedman of Mu'awiyah, that Abdullah ibn Mas'adah al-Fazari was very dark-skinned, and that the Prophet ﷺ had given him to his daughter Fatimah, so she raised him and then freed him. After all of that, he was later with Mu'awiyah during the days of Siffin, and he was among the harshest of people against Ali ibn Abi Talib, may Allah be pleased with him.

Imam Ahmad said: Sufyan ibn Uyaynah narrated to us, from al-Zuhri, from Nabhan, from Umm Salamah, who mentioned that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "If one of you has a mukatab (slave under a contract to purchase his freedom) who has the means to pay it off, then let her veil herself from him."

Abu Dawud also narrated it, from Musaddad, from Sufyan, with the same chain.

Regarding His saying: {or those male attendants who have no desire}, meaning: such as hired workers and followers who are not suitable matches, and who, along with that, in their minds and dispositions have no inclination toward or desire for women.

Ibn Abbas said: he is the simple-minded one who has no desire.

Mujahid said: he is the dim-witted one.

Ikrimah said: he is the effeminate man whose member does not become erect. Others among the early generations said likewise.

In the Sahih, from the hadith of al-Zuhri, from Urwah, from Aishah: an effeminate man used to visit the household of the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, and they used to count him among those without desire. One day the Prophet ﷺ came in while he was describing a woman, saying that when she comes forward she comes forward with four (folds of flesh), and when she turns her back she turns with eight. The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Do I not see that this one knows what is here? He must not enter upon you again." So he had him removed, and thereafter he would go out to the open desert area every Friday to beg for food.

Imam Ahmad said: Abu Mu'awiyah narrated to us, Hisham ibn Urwah narrated to us, from his father, from Zaynab bint Abi Salamah, from Umm Salamah, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ came in to her while an effeminate man was present, and her brother Abdullah ibn Abi Umayyah was also there. The effeminate man was saying to Abdullah: "O Abdullah ibn Abi Umayyah, if Allah grants you conquest of Ta'if tomorrow, then take for yourself the daughter of Ghaylan, for she comes forward with four and turns her back with eight." The Messenger of Allah ﷺ heard this and said to Umm Salamah: "This one must not enter upon you again."

Both of them (al-Bukhari and Muslim) recorded it in the two Sahihs, from the hadith of Hisham ibn Urwah, with the same chain.

Imam Ahmad said: Abd al-Razzaq narrated to us, Ma'mar narrated to us, from al-Zuhri, from Urwah ibn al-Zubayr, from Aishah, may Allah be pleased with her, who said: There was a man, an effeminate one, who used to visit the wives of the Prophet ﷺ, and they used to count him among those without desire. One day the Prophet ﷺ came in while he was with one of his wives, and the man was describing a woman. He said: "When she comes forward she comes forward with four, and when she turns her back she turns with eight." The Prophet ﷺ said: "Do I not see that this one knows what is here? This one must not enter upon you." So they kept him from entering thereafter.

Muslim, Abu Dawud, and al-Nasa'i also narrated it, through the route of Abd al-Razzaq, with the same chain.

Regarding His saying: {or children who have no knowledge of the private aspects of women}, meaning: because of their young age they do not understand the states of women and their private matters, from women's soft speech, and their graceful bearing in walking, and their movements. So if the child is young and does not understand that, there is no harm in his entering upon women. But if he is adolescent or close to it, to the point that he recognizes and is aware of such things, and can distinguish between an unattractive woman and a beautiful one, then he should not be allowed to enter upon women. It is established in the two Sahihs, from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, that he said: "Beware of entering upon women." They said: "O Messenger of Allah, what do you say about the husband's brother?" He said: "The husband's brother is death itself."

Regarding His saying: {And let them not stamp their feet so as to make known what they conceal of their adornment}: In the pre-Islamic period, a woman, when walking along a path, if she had on her leg an anklet that was silent, its sound not being heard, would strike her foot against the ground so that men would notice its jingling. So Allah forbade the believing women from doing the like of that. Likewise, if some part of her adornment was concealed and she made some movement in order to reveal what was hidden, that falls under this same prohibition, because of His saying, Exalted is He: {And let them not stamp their feet so as to make known what they conceal of their adornment}. Also included in this is that she is forbidden from perfuming and scenting herself when going out from her house so that men might smell her fragrance. Abu Isa al-Tirmidhi said: Muhammad ibn Bashshar narrated to us, Yahya ibn Sa'id al-Qattan narrated to us, from Thabit ibn Umarah al-Hanafi, from Ghunaym ibn Qays, from Abu Musa, may Allah be pleased with him, from the Prophet ﷺ, who said: "Every eye commits fornication, and a woman, when she perfumes herself and then passes by a gathering, is such and such," meaning a fornicator.

He said: And on this subject there is also a report from Abu Hurayrah, and this is hasan sahih (good and authentic).

Abu Dawud and al-Nasa'i narrated it, from the hadith of Thabit ibn Umarah, with the same chain.

Abu Dawud said: Muhammad ibn Kathir told us, Sufyan informed us, from Asim ibn Ubaydillah, from Ubayd, the freedman of Abu Ruhm, from Abu Hurayrah, may Allah be pleased with him, who said: a woman met him, and he perceived the scent of perfume from her, and her train raised dust as it trailed. So he said: "O slave-girl of the Compeller (al-Jabbar), have you come from the mosque?" She said: "Yes." He said to her: "And for it you perfumed yourself?" She said: "Yes." He said: "I heard my beloved Abu al-Qasim ﷺ say: 'Allah does not accept the prayer of a woman who has perfumed herself for this mosque, until she returns and performs a full ritual washing (ghusl) like the ghusl for major impurity (janabah).'"

Ibn Majah also related it, from Abu Bakr ibn Abi Shaybah, from Sufyan, that is, Ibn Uyaynah, with the same chain.

Al-Tirmidhi also related, from the hadith of Musa ibn Ubaydah, from Ayyub ibn Khalid, from Maymunah bint Sa'd, that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, said: "The woman who flaunts her adornment before those who are not her own people is like the darkness of the Day of Resurrection, having no light."

Among these matters as well is that women are forbidden from walking in the middle of the road, because of the exposure and display (tabarruj) that this involves. Abu Dawud said:

Al-Qa'nabi told us, Abd al-Aziz, that is, ibn Muhammad, told us, from Abu al-Yaman, from Shaddad ibn Abi Amr ibn Himas, from his father, from Hamzah ibn Abi Usayd al-Ansari, from his father: that he heard the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, as he was coming out of the mosque, while the men and women were mixed together in the road, say to the women: "Keep back, for it is not for you to occupy the middle of the road; keep to the sides of the road." So a woman would press herself against the wall, so much so that her garment would catch on the wall from how closely she clung to it.

His saying, exalted is He: {And turn to Allah in repentance, all of you believers, that you may succeed} means: do what I command you regarding these beautiful qualities and noble character traits, and abandon what the people of the pre-Islamic era (Jahiliyyah) held to of base character traits and qualities. For true success, complete success, lies in doing what Allah and His Messenger have commanded, and abandoning what they have forbidden. And Allah, exalted is He, is the one from whom help is sought, and upon Him is reliance.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

هَذَا أمْرٌ مِنَ اللَّهِ تَعَالَى لِلنِّسَاءِ الْمُؤْمِنَاتِ، وغَيْرَة مِنْهُ لِأَزْوَاجِهِنَّ، عِبَادِهِ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ، وَتَمْيِيزٌ لَهُنَّ عَنْ صِفَةِ نِسَاءِ الْجَاهِلِيَّةِ وَفِعَالِ الْمُشْرِكَاتِ. وكان سَبَبَ نُزُولِ هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ مَا ذَكَرَهُ مُقَاتِلُ بْنُ حيَّان قَالَ: بَلَغَنَا -وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ -أَنَّ جَابِرَ بْنَ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ الْأَنْصَارِيَّ حَدَّث: أَنَّ "أَسْمَاءَ بِنْتَ مُرْشدَة" كَانَتْ فِي مَحِلٍّ لَهَا فِي بَنِي حَارِثَةَ، فَجَعَلَ النِّسَاءُ يَدْخُلْنَ عَلَيْهَا غَيْرَ مُتَأزّرات فَيَبْدُو مَا فِي أَرْجُلِهِنَّ مِنَ الْخَلَاخِلِ، وَتَبْدُو صُدُورُهُنَّ وَذَوَائِبُهُنَّ، فَقَالَتْ أَسْمَاءُ: مَا أَقْبَحَ هَذَا. فَأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ: ﴿وَقُلْ لِلْمُؤْمِنَاتِ يَغْضُضْنَ مِنْ أَبْصَارِهِنَّ وَيَحْفَظْنَ فُرُوجَهُنَّ﴾ الْآيَةَ.

فَقَوْلُهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَقُلْ لِلْمُؤْمِنَاتِ يَغْضُضْنَ مِنْ أَبْصَارِهِنَّ﴾ أَيْ: عَمَّا حَرَّم اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِنَّ مِنَ النَّظَرِ إِلَى غَيْرِ أَزْوَاجِهِنَّ. وَلِهَذَا ذَهَبَ [كَثِيرٌ مِنَ الْعُلَمَاءِ] إِلَى أَنَّهُ: لَا يَجُوزُ لِلْمَرْأَةِ أَنْ تَنْظُرَ إِلَى الْأَجَانِبِ بِشَهْوَةٍ وَلَا بِغَيْرِ شَهْوَةٍ أَصْلًا. وَاحْتَجَّ كَثِيرٌ مِنْهُمْ بِمَا رَوَاهُ أَبُو دَاوُدَ وَالتِّرْمِذِيُّ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ الزُّهْرِيِّ، عَنْ نَبْهَانَ -مَوْلَى أُمِّ سَلَمَةَ -أَنَّهُ حَدَّثَهُ: أَنَّ أُمَّ سَلَمَةَ حَدَّثته: أَنَّهَا كَانَتْ عِنْدَ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ وَمَيْمُونَةُ، قَالَتْ: فَبَيْنَمَا نَحْنُ عِنْدَهُ أَقْبَلَ ابنُ أُمِّ مَكْتُومٍ، فَدَخَلَ عَلَيْهِ، وَذَلِكَ بَعْدَمَا أُمِرْنا بِالْحِجَابِ، فَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "احْتَجِبَا مِنْهُ" فَقُلْتُ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، أَلَيْسَ هُوَ أَعْمَى لَا يُبْصِرُنَا ولا يعرفنا؟ فَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "أَوَ عَمْيَاوَانِ أَنْتُمَا؟ أَلَسْتُمَا تُبْصِرَانِهِ" .

ثُمَّ قَالَ التِّرْمِذِيُّ: هَذَا حَدِيثٌ حَسَنٌ صَحِيحٌ.

وَذَهَبَ آخَرُونَ مِنَ الْعُلَمَاءِ إِلَى جَوَازِ نَظَرِهِنَّ إِلَى الْأَجَانِبِ بِغَيْرِ شَهْوَةٍ، كَمَا ثَبَتَ فِي الصَّحِيحِ: أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ جَعَلَ يَنْظُرُ إِلَى الْحَبَشَةِ وَهُمْ يَلْعَبُونَ بِحِرَابِهِمْ يَوْمَ الْعِيدِ فِي الْمَسْجِدِ، وَعَائِشَةُ أُمُّ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ تَنْظُرُ إِلَيْهِمْ مِنْ وَرَائِهِ، وَهُوَ يَسْتُرُهَا مِنْهُمْ حَتَّى مَلَّت وَرَجَعَتْ .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَيَحْفَظْنَ فُرُوجَهُنَّ﴾ قَالَ سَعِيدُ بْنُ جُبَيْر:، عَنِ الْفَوَاحِشِ. وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ وَسُفْيَانُ: عَمَّا لَا يَحِلُّ لَهُنَّ. وَقَالَ مُقَاتِلٌ:، عَنِ الزِّنَى. وَقَالَ أَبُو الْعَالِيَةِ: كُلُّ آيَةٍ نَزَلَتْ فِي الْقُرْآنِ يُذْكَرُ فِيهَا حِفْظُ الْفُرُوجِ، فَهُوَ مِنَ الزِّنَى، إِلَّا هَذِهِ الْآيَةَ: ﴿وَيَحْفَظْنَ فُرُوجَهُنَّ﴾ أَلَّا يَرَاهَا أَحَدٌ.

وَقَالَ : ﴿وَلا يُبْدِينَ زِينَتَهُنَّ إِلا مَا ظَهَرَ مِنْهَا﴾ أَيْ: لَا يُظهرْنَ شَيْئًا مِنَ الزِّينَةِ لِلْأَجَانِبِ، إِلَّا مَا لَا يُمْكِنُ إِخْفَاؤُهُ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ مَسْعُودٍ: كَالرِّدَاءِ وَالثِّيَابِ. يَعْنِي: عَلَى مَا كَانَ يَتَعَانَاهُ نِسَاءُ الْعَرَبِ، مِنَ المِقْنعة الَّتِي تُجَلِّل ثِيَابَهَا، وَمَا يَبْدُو مِنْ أَسَافِلِ الثِّيَابِ فَلَا حَرَجَ عَلَيْهَا فِيهِ؛ لِأَنَّ هَذَا لَا يُمْكِنُ إِخْفَاؤُهُ. [وَنَظِيرُهُ فِي زِيِّ النِّسَاءِ مَا يَظْهَرُ مِنْ إِزَارِهَا، وَمَا لَا يُمْكِنُ إِخْفَاؤُهُ. وَقَالَ] بِقَوْلِ ابْنِ مَسْعُودٍ: الْحَسَنُ، وَابْنُ سِيرِينَ، وَأَبُو الْجَوْزَاءِ، وَإِبْرَاهِيمُ النَّخَعي، وَغَيْرُهُمْ.

وَقَالَ الْأَعْمَشِ، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَير، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: ﴿وَلا يُبْدِينَ زِينَتَهُنَّ إِلا مَا ظَهَرَ مِنْهَا﴾ قَالَ: وَجْهُهَا وَكَفَّيْهَا وَالْخَاتَمُ. ورُوي عَنِ ابْنِ عُمَرَ، وَعَطَاءٍ، وَعِكْرِمَةَ، وَسَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْرٍ، وَأَبِي الشَّعْثَاءِ، وَالضَّحَّاكِ، وَإِبْرَاهِيمَ النَّخَعي، وَغَيْرِهِمْ -نحوُ ذَلِكَ. وَهَذَا يُحْتَمَلُ أَنْ يَكُونَ تَفْسِيرًا لِلزِّينَةِ الَّتِي نُهِينَ عَنْ إِبْدَائِهَا، كَمَا قَالَ أَبُو إِسْحَاقَ السَّبيعي، عَنْ أَبِي الأحْوَص، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ قَالَ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَلا يُبْدِينَ زِينَتَهُنَّ﴾ : الزِّينَةُ القُرْط والدُّمْلُج وَالْخَلْخَالُ وَالْقِلَادَةُ. وَفِي رِوَايَةٍ عَنْهُ بِهَذَا الْإِسْنَادِ قَالَ: الزِّينَةُ زِينَتَانِ: فَزِينَةٌ لَا يَرَاهَا إِلَّا الزَّوْجُ: الْخَاتَمُ وَالسُّوَارُ، [وَزِينَةٌ يَرَاهَا الْأَجَانِبُ، وَهِيَ] الظَّاهِرُ مِنَ الثِّيَابِ.

وَقَالَ الزُّهْرِيُّ: [لَا يَبْدُو] لِهَؤُلَاءِ الَّذِينَ سَمَّى اللَّهُ مِمَّنْ لَا يَحِلُّ لَهُ إِلَّا الْأَسْوِرَةُ وَالْأَخْمِرَةُ والْأَقْرِطَةُ مِنْ غَيْرِ حَسْرٍ، وَأَمَّا عَامَّةُ النَّاسِ فَلَا يَبْدُو مِنْهَا إِلَّا الْخَوَاتِمُ.

وَقَالَ مَالِكٌ، عَنِ الزُّهْرِيِّ: ﴿إِلا مَا ظَهَرَ مِنْهَا﴾ الْخَاتَمُ وَالْخَلْخَالُ.

وَيُحْتَمَلُ أَنَّ ابْنَ عَبَّاسٍ وَمَنْ تَابَعَهُ أَرَادُوا تَفْسِيرَ مَا ظَهَرَ مِنْهَا بِالْوَجْهِ وَالْكَفَّيْنِ، وَهَذَا هُوَ الْمَشْهُورُ عِنْدَ الْجُمْهُورِ، وَيُسْتَأْنَسُ لَهُ بِالْحَدِيثِ الَّذِي رَوَاهُ أَبُو دَاوُدَ فِي سُنَنِهِ:

حَدَّثَنَا يَعْقُوبُ بْنُ كَعْبٍ الْإِنْطَاكِيُّ ومُؤَمَّل بْنُ الْفَضْلِ الحَرَّاني قَالَا حَدَّثَنَا الْوَلِيدُ، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ بَشِير، عَنْ قَتَادَةَ، عَنْ خَالِدِ بْنِ دُرَيك، عَنْ عَائِشَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهَا؛ أَنَّ أَسْمَاءَ بِنْتَ أَبِي بَكْرٍ دَخَلَتْ عَلَى النَّبِيِّ ﷺ وَعَلَيْهَا ثِيَابٌ رِقَاقٌ، فَأَعْرَضَ عَنْهَا وَقَالَ: "يَا أَسْمَاءُ، إن المرأة إذا بلغت المحيض لم يَصْلُحْ أَنْ يُرَى مِنْهَا إِلَّا هَذَا" وَأَشَارَ إِلَى وَجْهِهِ وَكَفَّيْهِ .

لَكِنْ قَالَ أَبُو دَاوُدَ وَأَبُو حَاتِمٍ الرَّازِيُّ: هَذَا مُرْسَلٌ؛ خَالِدُ بْنُ دُرَيك لَمْ يَسْمَعْ مِنْ عَائِشَةَ، فَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَلْيَضْرِبْنَ بِخُمُرِهِنَّ عَلَى جُيُوبِهِنَّ﴾ يَعْنِي: الْمَقَانِعَ يُعْمَلُ لَهَا صَنفات ضَارِبَاتٌ عَلَى صُدُورِ النِّسَاءِ، لِتُوَارِيَ مَا تَحْتَهَا مِنْ صَدْرِهَا وَتَرَائِبِهَا؛ لِيُخَالِفْنَ شعارَ نِسَاءِ أَهْلِ الْجَاهِلِيَّةِ، فَإِنَّهُنَّ لَمْ يَكُنَّ يَفْعَلْنَ ذَلِكَ، بَلْ كَانَتِ الْمَرْأَةُ تَمُرُّ بَيْنَ الرِّجَالِ مُسَفِّحَةً بِصَدْرِهَا، لَا يُوَارِيهِ شَيْءٌ، وَرُبَّمَا أَظْهَرَتْ عُنُقَهَا وَذَوَائِبَ شَعْرِهَا وَأَقْرِطَةَ آذَانِهَا. فَأَمَرَ اللَّهُ الْمُؤْمِنَاتِ أَنْ يَسْتَتِرْنَ فِي هَيْئَاتِهِنَّ وَأَحْوَالِهِنَّ، كَمَا قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿يَا أَيُّهَا النَّبِيُّ قُلْ لأزْوَاجِكَ وَبَنَاتِكَ وَنِسَاءِ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ يُدْنِينَ عَلَيْهِنَّ مِنْ جَلابِيبِهِنَّ ذَلِكَ أَدْنَى أَنْ يُعْرَفْنَ فَلا يُؤْذَيْنَ﴾ [الْأَحْزَابِ: ٥٩] . وَقَالَ فِي هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ الْكَرِيمَةِ: ﴿وَلْيَضْرِبْنَ بِخُمُرِهِنَّ عَلَى جُيُوبِهِنَّ﴾ والخُمُر: جَمْعُ خِمار، وَهُوَ مَا يُخَمر بِهِ، أَيْ: يُغَطَّى بِهِ الرَّأْسُ، وَهِيَ الَّتِي تُسَمِّيهَا النَّاسُ الْمَقَانِعَ.

قَالَ سَعِيدُ بْنُ جُبَيْرٍ: ﴿وَلْيَضْرِبْن﴾ : وَلِيَشْدُدْنَ ﴿بِخُمُرِهِنَّ عَلَى جُيُوبِهِنَّ﴾ يَعْنِي: عَلَى النَّحْرِ وَالصَّدْرِ، فَلَا يُرَى مِنْهُ شَيْءٌ.

وَقَالَ الْبُخَارِيُّ: وَقَالَ أَحْمَدُ بْنُ شَبِيب : حدَّثنا أَبِي، عَنْ يُونُسَ، عَنِ ابْنِ شِهَاب، عَنْ عُرْوَةَ، عَنْ عَائِشَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهَا، قَالَتْ: يَرْحَمُ اللَّهُ نِسَاءَ الْمُهَاجِرَاتِ الْأُوَلِ، لَمَّا أَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ: ﴿وَلْيَضْرِبْنَ بِخُمُرِهِنَّ عَلَى جُيُوبِهِنَّ﴾ شقَقْنَ مُرُوطهن فَاخْتَمَرْنَ بِهِ .

وَقَالَ أَيْضًا: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو نُعَيم، حَدَّثَنَا إِبْرَاهِيمُ بْنُ نَافِعٍ، عَنِ الْحَسَنِ بْنِ مُسْلِمٍ، عَنْ صَفيّة بِنْتِ شَيْبَةَ؛ أَنَّ عَائِشَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهَا، كَانَتْ تَقُولُ : لَمَّا نَزَلَتْ هَذِهِ الْآيَةُ: ﴿وَلْيَضْرِبْنَ بِخُمُرِهِنَّ عَلَى جُيُوبِهِنَّ﴾ : أَخَذْنَ أُزُرَهُنَّ فَشَقَقنها مِنْ قِبَلِ الْحَوَاشِي، فَاخْتَمَرْنَ بِهَا .

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا أَحْمَدُ بْنُ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ يُونُسَ، حَدَّثَنِي الزِّنْجِيُّ بْنُ خَالِدٍ، حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ عُثْمَانَ بْنِ خُثَيْم، عَنْ صَفِيَّةَ بِنْتِ شَيْبَةَ قَالَتْ: بَيْنَا نَحْنُ عِنْدَ عَائِشَةَ، قَالَتْ: فَذَكَرْنَا نِسَاءَ قُرَيْشٍ وَفَضْلَهُنَّ. فَقَالَتْ عَائِشَةُ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهَا: إِنَّ لِنِسَاءِ قُرَيْشٍ لَفَضْلًا وَإِنِّي -وَاللَّهِ -وَمَا رَأَيْتُ أفضلَ مِنْ نِسَاءِ الْأَنْصَارِ أَشَدَّ تَصْدِيقًا بِكِتَابِ اللَّهِ، وَلَا إِيمَانًا بِالتَّنْزِيلِ. لَقَدْ أُنْزِلَتْ سُورَةُ النُّورِ: ﴿وَلْيَضْرِبْنَ بِخُمُرِهِنَّ عَلَى جُيُوبِهِنَّ﴾ ، انْقَلَبَ إِلَيْهِنَّ رِجَالُهُنَّ يَتْلُونَ عَلَيْهِنَّ مَا أَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ إِلَيْهِمْ فِيهَا، وَيَتْلُو الرَّجُلُ عَلَى امْرَأَتِهِ وَابْنَتِهِ وَأُخْتِهِ، وَعَلَى كُلِّ ذِي قَرَابَةٍ ، فَمَا مِنْهُنَّ امْرَأَةٌ إِلَّا قَامَتْ إِلَى مِرْطها المُرَحَّل فَاعْتَجَرَتْ بِهِ، تَصْدِيقًا وَإِيمَانًا بِمَا أَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ مِنْ كِتَابِهِ، فأصبحْنَ وَرَاءَ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ الصُّبْحَ مُعْتَجَرَاتٍ، كأن على رؤوسهن الغربان.

وَرَوَاهُ أَبُو دَاوُدَ مِنْ غَيْرِ وَجْهٍ، عَنْ صَفِيَّةَ بِنْتِ شَيْبَةَ، بِهِ .

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنَا يُونُسُ، أَخْبَرَنَا ابْنُ وَهْبٍ، أَنَّ قُرَّةَ بْنَ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ أَخْبَرَهُ، عَنِ ابْنِ شِهَابٍ، عَنْ عُرْوَة، عَنْ عَائِشَةَ؛ أَنَّهَا قَالَتْ: يَرْحَمُ اللَّهُ النِّسَاءَ الْمُهَاجِرَاتِ الأوَل، لَمَّا أَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ: ﴿وَلْيَضْرِبْنَ بِخُمُرِهِنَّ عَلَى جُيُوبِهِنَّ﴾ شَقّقن أكثَف مُرُوطِهِنَّ فَاخْتَمَرْنَ بِهِ. وَرَوَاهُ أَبُو دَاوُدَ مِنْ حَدِيثِ ابْنِ وَهْبٍ، بِهِ .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَلا يُبْدِينَ زِينَتَهُنَّ إِلا لِبُعُولَتِهِنَّ﴾ يَعْنِي: أَزْوَاجَهُنَّ، ﴿أَوْ آبَائِهِنَّ أَوْ آبَاءِ بُعُولَتِهِنَّ أَوْ أَبْنَائِهِنَّ أَوْ أَبْنَاءِ بُعُولَتِهِنَّ أَوْ إِخْوَانِهِنَّ أَوْ بَنِي إِخْوَانِهِنَّ أَوْ بَنِي أَخَوَاتِهِنَّ﴾ كُلُّ هَؤُلَاءِ مَحَارِمُ الْمَرْأَةِ يَجُوزُ لَهَا أَنْ تَظْهَرَ عَلَيْهِمْ بِزِينَتِهَا، وَلَكِنْ مِنْ غَيْرِ اقْتِصَادٍ وَتُبَهْرُجٍ .

وَقَالَ ابْنُ الْمُنْذِرِ: حَدَّثَنَا مُوسَى -يَعْنِي: ابْنَ هَارُونَ -حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو بَكْرٍ -يَعْنِي ابْنَ أَبِي شَيْبَةَ -حَدَّثَنَا عَفَّانُ، حَدَّثَنَا حَمَّادُ بْنُ سَلَمَةَ، أَخْبَرَنَا دَاوُدُ، عَنِ الشَّعْبِيِّ وعِكْرمَة فِي هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ: ﴿وَلا يُبْدِينَ زِينَتَهُنَّ إِلا لِبُعُولَتِهِنَّ أَوْ آبَائِهِنَّ أَوْ آبَاءِ بُعُولَتِهِنَّ﴾ -حَتَّى فَرَغَ مِنْهَا قَالَ: لَمْ يَذْكُرِ الْعَمَّ وَلَا الْخَالَ؛ لِأَنَّهُمَا ينعَتان لِأَبْنَائِهِمَا، وَلَا تَضَعُ خِمَارَهَا عِنْدَ الْعَمِّ وَالْخَالِ فَأَمَّا الزَّوْجُ فَإِنَّمَا ذَلِكَ كُلُّهُ مِنْ أَجْلِهِ، فَتَتَصَنَّعُ لَهُ مَا لَا يَكُونُ بِحَضْرَةِ غَيْرِهِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿أَوْ نِسَائِهِنَّ﴾ يَعْنِي: تُظهر زِينَتَهَا أَيْضًا لِلنِّسَاءِ الْمُسَلِمَاتِ دُونَ نِسَاءِ أَهْلِ الذِّمَّةِ؛ لِئَلَّا تَصِفَهُنَّ لِرِجَالِهِنَّ، وَذَلِكَ -وَإِنْ كَانَ مَحْذُورًا فِي جَمِيعِ النِّسَاءِ -إِلَّا أَنَّهُ فِي نِسَاءِ أَهْلِ الذِّمَّةِ أَشَدُّ، فَإِنَّهُنَّ لَا يَمْنَعُهُنَّ مِنْ ذَلِكَ مَانِعٌ، وَأَمَّا الْمُسْلِمَةُ فَإِنَّهَا تَعْلَمُ أَنَّ ذَلِكَ حَرَامٌ فَتَنْزَجِرُ عَنْهُ. وَقَدْ قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "لَا تُبَاشِرُ المرأةَ المرأةَ، تَنْعَتُهَا لِزَوْجِهَا كَأَنَّهُ يَنْظُرُ إِلَيْهَا". أَخْرَجَاهُ فِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ، عَنِ ابْنِ مَسْعُودٍ .

وَقَالَ سَعِيدُ بْنُ مَنْصُورٍ فِي سُنَنِهِ: حَدَّثَنَا إِسْمَاعِيلُ بْنُ عَيَّاشٍ، عَنْ هِشَامِ بْنِ الْغَازِّ،، عَنْ عُبَادَةَ بْنِ نُسَيّ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنِ الْحَارِثِ بْنِ قَيْسٍ قَالَ: كَتَبَ أَمِيرُ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ عُمَرُ بْنُ الْخَطَّابِ إِلَى أَبِي عُبَيْدَةَ: أَمَّا بَعْدُ، فَإِنَّهُ بَلَغَنِي أَنَّ نِسَاءً مِنْ نِسَاءِ الْمُسْلِمِينَ يَدْخُلْنَ الْحَمَّامَاتِ مَعَ نِسَاءِ أَهْلِ الشِّرْكِ، فانْهَ مَنْ قِبَلَك فَلَا يَحِلُّ لِامْرَأَةٍ تُؤْمِنُ بِالْلَّهِ وَالْيَوْمِ الْآخِرِ أَنْ يَنْظُرَ إِلَى عَوْرَتِهَا إِلَّا أَهْلُ مِلَّتِهَا .

وَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿أَوْ نِسَائِهِنَّ﴾ قَالَ: نِسَاؤُهُنَّ الْمُسْلِمَاتُ، لَيْسَ الْمُشْرِكَاتُ مِنْ نِسَائِهِنَّ، وَلَيْسَ لِلْمَرْأَةِ الْمُسْلِمَةِ أَنْ تَنْكَشِفَ بَيْنَ يَدَيِ الْمُشْرِكَةِ.

وَرَوَى عَبد فِي تَفْسِيرِهِ عَنِ الْكَلْبِيِّ، عَنْ أَبِي صَالِحٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: ﴿أَوْ نِسَائِهِنَّ﴾ ، قَالَ: هُنَّ الْمُسْلِمَاتُ لَا تُبْدِيهِ لِيَهُودِيَّةٍ وَلَا نَصْرَانِيَّةٍ، وَهُوَ النَّحْر والقُرْط والوٍشَاح، وَمَا لَا يَحِلُّ أَنْ يَرَاهُ إلا محرم.

وَرَوَى سَعِيدٌ: حَدَّثَنَا جَرِيرٌ، عَنْ لَيْثٍ، عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ قَالَ: لَا تَضَعُ الْمُسْلِمَةُ خِمَارَهَا عِنْدَ مُشْرِكَةٍ؛ لِأَنَّ اللَّهَ تَعَالَى يَقُولُ: ﴿أَوْ نِسَائِهِنَّ﴾ فَلَيْسَتْ مِنْ نِسَائِهِنَّ.

وَعَنْ مَكْحُولٍ وَعُبَادَةَ بْنِ نُسَيّ: أَنَّهُمَا كَرِهَا أَنْ تُقَبِّلَ النصرانيةُ وَالْيَهُودِيَّةُ وَالْمَجُوسِيَّةُ الْمُسْلِمَةَ.

فَأَمَّا مَا رَوَاهُ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا عَلِيُّ بْنُ الْحُسَيْنِ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو عُمَيْرٍ، حَدَّثَنَا ضَمْرَة قَالَ: قَالَ ابْنُ عَطَاءٍ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ: وَلَمَّا قَدِمَ أَصْحَابُ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ بَيْتَ الْمَقْدِسِ، كَانَ قَوَابل نِسَائِهِمُ الْيَهُودِيَّاتُ وَالنَّصْرَانِيَّاتُ فَهَذَا -إِنْ صَحَّ -مَحمولٌ عَلَى حَالِ الضَّرُورَةِ، أَوْ أَنَّ ذَلِكَ مِنْ بَابِ الِامْتِهَانِ، ثُمَّ إِنَّهُ لَيْسَ فِيهِ كَشَفُ عَوْرَةٍ وَلَا بُدَّ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿أَوْ مَا مَلَكَتْ أَيْمَانُهُنَّ﴾ قَالَ ابْنُ جُرَيج : يَعْنِي: مِنْ نِسَاءِ الْمُشْرِكِينَ، فَيَجُوزُ لَهَا أَنْ تُظْهِرَ [زَينَتَهَا لَهَا وَإِنْ كَانَتْ مُشْرِكَةً؛ لِأَنَّهَا أَمَتُهَا. وَإِلَيْهِ ذَهَبَ سَعِيدُ بْنُ المسيَّب. وَقَالَ الْأَكْثَرُونَ: بَلْ يَجُوزُ لَهَا أَنْ تَظْهَرَ] عَلَى رَقِيقِهَا مِنَ الرِّجَالِ وَالنِّسَاءِ، وَاسْتَدَلُّوا بِالْحَدِيثِ الَّذِي رَوَاهُ أَبُو دَاوُدَ:

حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ عِيسَى، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو جُمَيْعٍ سَالِمُ بْنُ دِينَارٍ، عَنْ ثَابِتٍ، عَنْ أَنَسٍ، أَنَّ النَّبِيَّ ﷺ أَتَى فَاطِمَةَ بِعَبْدٍ قَدْ وَهَبَهُ لَهَا. قَالَ: وَعَلَى فَاطِمَةَ ثَوْبٌ إِذَا قَنَّعت بِهِ رَأْسَهَا لَمْ يَبْلُغْ رِجْلَيْهَا، وَإِذَا غَطَّتْ بِهِ رِجْلَيْهَا لَمْ يَبْلُغْ رَأْسَهَا، فَلَمَّا رَأَى النَّبِيُّ ﷺ مَا تَلْقَى قَالَ: "إِنَّهُ لَيْسَ عَلَيْكِ بَأْسٌ، إِنَّمَا هُوَ أَبُوكِ وَغُلَامُكِ" .

وَقَدْ ذَكَرَ الْحَافِظُ ابْنُ عَسَاكِرَ فِي تَارِيخِهِ [فِي] تَرْجَمَةِ حُدَيْج الخَصِيّ -مُوَلَى مُعَاوِيَةَ -أَنَّ عَبْدَ اللَّهِ بْنَ مَسْعَدَة الْفَزَارِيَّ كَانَ أَسْوَدَ شَدِيدَ الْأَدْمَةِ، وَأَنَّهُ قَدْ كَانَ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ وَهَبَهُ لِابْنَتِهِ فَاطِمَةَ، فَرَبَّتْهُ ثُمَّ أَعْتَقَتْهُ، ثُمَّ قَدْ كَانَ بَعْدَ ذَلِكَ كُلِّهِ مَعَ مُعَاوِيَةَ أَيَّامَ صِفِّينَ، وَكَانَ مِنْ أَشَدِّ النَّاسِ عَلَى عَلِيِّ بْنِ أَبِي طَالِبٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ .

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا سُفْيَانُ بْنُ عُيَيْنَة، عَنِ الزُّهْرِيِّ، عَنْ نَبْهَان، عَنْ أُمِّ سَلَمَةَ، ذَكَرَتْ أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَ: "إِذَا كَانَ لِإِحْدَاكُنَّ مُكَاتَب، وَكَانَ لَهُ مَا يُؤَدِّي، فَلْتَحْتَجِبْ مِنْهُ".

وَرَوَاهُ أَبُو دَاوُدَ، عَنْ مُسَدَّد، عَنْ سُفْيَانَ، بِهِ .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿أَوِ التَّابِعِينَ غَيْرِ أُولِي الإرْبَةِ مِنَ الرِّجَالِ﴾ يَعْنِي: كَالْأُجَرَاءِ وَالْأَتْبَاعِ الَّذِينَ لَيْسُوا بِأَكْفَاءَ، وَهُمْ مَعَ ذَلِكَ فِي عُقُولِهِمْ وَله وخَوَث ، وَلَا همَّ لَهُمْ إِلَى النِّسَاءِ وَلَا يَشْتَهُونَهُنَّ.

قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: هُوَ الْمُغَفَّلُ الَّذِي لَا شَهْوَةَ لَهُ.

وَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: هُوَ الأبْلَه.

وَقَالَ عِكْرِمَةُ: هُوَ المخَنَّث الَّذِي لَا يَقُومُ زُبُّه. وَكَذَلِكَ قَالَ غَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ مِنَ السَّلَفِ.

وَفِي الصَّحِيحِ مِنْ حَدِيثِ الزُّهْرِيِّ، عَنْ عُرْوَةَ، عَنْ عَائِشَةَ؛ أَنَّ مُخَنَّثًا كَانَ يدخل على أهل رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ، وَكَانُوا يعدونه من غير أولي الإربة، فدخل النبي ﷺ وَهُوَ ينَعت امْرَأَةً: يَقُولُ إِنَّهَا إِذَا أَقْبَلَتْ أَقْبَلَتْ بِأَرْبَعٍ، وَإِذَا أَدْبَرَتْ أَدْبَرَتْ بِثَمَانٍ. فَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "أَلَا أَرَى هَذَا يَعْلَمُ مَا هَاهُنَا، لَا يدخلَنّ عليكُنَ" فَأَخْرَجَهُ، فَكَانَ بِالْبَيْدَاءِ يَدْخُلُ يَوْمَ كُلِّ جُمُعَةٍ يَسْتَطْعِمُ .

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو مُعَاوِيَةَ، حَدَّثَنَا هِشَامِ بْنِ عُرْوَةَ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنْ زَيْنَبَ بِنْتِ أَبِي سَلَمَةَ، عَنْ أُمِّ سَلَمَةَ قَالَتْ: دَخَلَ عَلَيْهَا [رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ] وَعِنْدَهَا مُخَنَّثٌ، وَعِنْدَهَا [أَخُوهَا] عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ أَبِي أُمَيَّةَ [وَالْمُخَنَّثُ يَقُولُ لِعَبْدِ اللَّهِ: يَا عَبْدَ اللَّهِ بْنَ أَبِي أُمَيَّةَ] إِنْ فَتَحَ اللَّهُ عَلَيْكُمُ الطَّائِفَ غَدًا، فَعَلَيْكَ بِابْنَةِ غَيْلَانَ، فَإِنَّهَا تُقْبِلُ بِأَرْبَعٍ وَتُدْبِرْ بِثَمَانٍ. قَالَ: فَسَمِعَهُ رسول الله صلى الله عليه وسلم فقال لِأُمِّ سَلَمَةَ: "لَا يَدْخُلَنَّ هَذَا عَلَيْكِ".

أَخْرَجَاهُ فِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ هِشَامِ بْنِ عُرْوَةَ، بِهِ .

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الرَّزَّاقِ، حَدَّثَنَا مَعْمَر، عَنِ الزُّهْرِيِّ، عَنْ عُرْوَةَ بْنِ الزُّبَيْرِ، عَنْ عَائِشَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهَا، قَالَتْ: كَانَ رَجُلٌ يَدْخُلُ عَلَى أَزْوَاجِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ مُخَنَّثٌ، وَكَانُوا يَعُدّونه مِنْ غير أولي الإربة، فدخل النبي صلى الله عَلَيْهِ وَسَلَّمَ يَوْمًا وَهُوَ عِنْدَ بَعْضِ نِسَائِهِ، وَهُوَ يَنْعَتُ امْرَأَةً. فَقَالَ: إِنَّهَا إِذَا أَقْبَلَتْ أَقْبَلَتْ بِأَرْبَعٍ، وَإِذَا أَدْبَرَتْ أَدْبَرَتْ بِثَمَانٍ. فَقَالَ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ: "أَلَا أَرَى هَذَا يَعْلَمُ مَا هَاهُنَا؟ لَا يدخلَنَّ عَلَيْكُمْ هَذَا" فَحَجَبُوهُ.

وَرَوَاهُ مُسْلِمٌ، وَأَبُو دَاوُدَ، وَالنَّسَائِيُّ مِنْ طَرِيقِ عَبْدِ الرَّزَّاقِ، بِهِ .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿أَوِ الطِّفْلِ الَّذِينَ لَمْ يَظْهَرُوا عَلَى عَوْرَاتِ النِّسَاءِ﴾ يَعْنِي: لِصِغَرِهِمْ لَا يَفْهَمُونَ أَحْوَالَ النِّسَاءِ وَعَوْرَاتِهِنَّ مِنْ كَلَامِهِنَّ الرَّخِيمِ، وَتَعَطُّفِهِنَّ فِي الْمِشْيَةِ وَحَرَكَاتِهِنَّ، فَإِذَا كَانَ الطِّفْلُ صَغِيرًا لَا يَفْهَمُ ذَلِكَ، فَلَا بَأْسَ بِدُخُولِهِ عَلَى النِّسَاءِ.فَأَمَّا إِنْ كَانَ مُرَاهِقًا أَوْ قَرِيبًا مِنْهُ، بِحَيْثُ يَعْرِفُ ذَلِكَ وَيَدْرِيهِ، وَيُفَرِّقُ بَيْنَ الشَّوْهَاءِ وَالْحَسْنَاءِ، فَلَا يُمَكَّنُ مِنَ الدُّخُولِ عَلَى النِّسَاءِ. وَقَدْ ثَبَتَ فِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ، عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: "إِيَّاكُمْ وَالدُّخُولَ عَلَى النِّسَاءِ". قَالُوا: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، أَفَرَأَيْتَ الحَمْو؟ قَالَ: "الحَمْو الْمَوْتُ".

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَلا يَضْرِبْنَ بِأَرْجُلِهِنَّ لِيُعْلَمَ مَا يُخْفِينَ مِنْ زِينَتِهِنَّ﴾ كَانَتِ الْمَرْأَةُ فِي الْجَاهِلِيَّةِ إِذَا كَانَتْ تَمْشِي فِي الطَّرِيقِ وَفِي رَجْلِهَا خَلْخَالٌ صَامِتٌ -لَا يُسْمَعُ صَوْتُهُ -ضَرَبَتْ بِرِجْلِهَا الْأَرْضَ، فَيَعْلَمُ الرِّجَالُ طَنِينَهُ، فَنَهَى اللَّهُ الْمُؤْمِنَاتِ عَنْ مَثَلِ ذَلِكَ. وَكَذَلِكَ إِذَا كَانَ شَيْءٌ مِنْ زِينَتِهَا مَسْتُورًا، فَتَحَرَّكَتْ بِحَرَكَةٍ لِتُظْهِرَ مَا هُوَ خَفِيٌّ، دَخَلَ فِي هَذَا النَّهْيِ؛ لِقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلا يَضْرِبْنَ بِأَرْجُلِهِنَّ لِيُعْلَمَ مَا يُخْفِينَ مِنْ زِينَتِهِنَّ﴾ : وَمِنْ ذَلِكَ أَيْضًا أَنَّهَا تُنْهَى عَنِ التَّعَطُّرِ وَالتَّطَيُّبِ عِنْدَ خُرُوجِهَا مِنْ بَيْتِهَا ليَشْتَمَّ الرِّجَالُ طِيبَهَا، فَقَدْ قَالَ أبو عيسى الترمذي: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ بَشَّارٍ، حَدَّثَنَا يَحْيَى بْنُ سَعِيدٍ القَّطَّان، عَنْ ثَابِتِ بْنِ عُمَارة الْحَنَفِيِّ، عَنْ غُنَيْم بْنِ قَيْسٍ، عَنْ أَبِي مُوسَى رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ قَالَ: "كُلُّ عَيْنٍ زَانِيَةٌ، وَالْمَرْأَةُ إِذَا اسْتَعْطَرَتْ فمرَّت بِالْمَجْلِسِ فَهِيَ كَذَا وَكَذَا" يَعْنِي زَانِيَةً .

قَالَ: وَفِي الْبَابِ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، وَهَذَا حَسَنٌ صَحِيحٌ.

رَوَاهُ أَبُو دَاوُدَ وَالنَّسَائِيُّ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ ثَابِتِ بْنِ عُمَارَةَ، بِهِ.

وَقَالَ أَبُو دَاوُدَ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ كَثِيرٍ، أَخْبَرَنَا سُفْيَانُ، عَنِ عَاصِمِ بْنِ عُبَيْدِ اللَّهِ، عَنْ عُبَيْدٍ مَوْلَى أَبِي رُهْم، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: لقيتْه امْرَأَةٌ وَجَدَ مِنْهَا رِيحَ الطِيبِ، وَلِذَيْلِهَا إِعْصَارٌ فَقَالَ: يَا أَمَةَ الْجَبَّارِ، جِئْتِ مِنَ الْمَسْجِدِ؟ قَالَتْ: نَعَمْ. قَالَ لَهَا: [وَلَهُ] تَطَيَّبتِ؟ قَالَتْ: نَعَمْ. قَالَ: إِنِّي سَمِعْتُ حِبِّي أَبَا الْقَاسِمِ ﷺ يَقُولُ: "لَا يَقْبَلُ اللَّهُ صَلَاةَ امْرَأَةٍ تَطَيبت لِهَذَا الْمَسْجِدِ، حَتَّى تَرْجِعَ فَتَغْتَسِلَ غُسلها مِنَ الْجَنَابَةِ".

وَرَوَاهُ ابْنُ مَاجَهْ، عَنْ أَبِي بَكْرِ بْنِ أبي شيبة، عن سُفْيَانَ -هُوَ ابْنُ عُيَيْنَةَ - بِهِ.

وَرَوَى التِّرْمِذِيُّ أَيْضًا مِنْ حَدِيثِ مُوسَى بْنِ عُبَيدة، عَنْ أَيُّوبَ بْنِ خَالِدٍ، عَنْ مَيْمُونَةَ بِنْتِ سَعْدٍ؛ أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ صَلَّى اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ وسلم قَالَ: "الرَّافِلَةُ فِي الزِّينَةِ فِي غَيْرِ أَهْلِهَا، كَمَثَلِ ظُلْمَةِ يَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ لَا نُورَ لَهَا" .

وَمِنْ ذَلِكَ أَيْضًا أَنَّهُنَّ يُنهَين عَنِ الْمَشْيِ فِي وَسَطِ الطَّرِيقِ؛ لِمَا فِيهِ مِنَ التَّبَرُّجِ. قَالَ أَبُو دَاوُدَ:

حَدَّثَنَا القَعْنَبِيّ، حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الْعَزِيزِ -يَعْنِي: ابْنَ مُحَمَّدٍ -عَنْ أَبِي الْيَمَانِ، عَنْ شَدَّادِ بْنِ أَبِي عَمْرِو بْنِ حِمَاسٍ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنْ حَمْزَةَ بْنِ أَبِي أُسَيْدٍ الْأَنْصَارِيِّ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ: أَنَّهُ سَمِعَ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَقُولُ وَهُوَ خَارِجٌ مِنَ الْمَسْجِدِ -وَقَدِ اخْتَلَطَ الرِّجَالُ مَعَ النِّسَاءِ فِي الطَّرِيقِ -فَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ لِلنِّسَاءِ: "اسْتَأْخِرْنَ، فَإِنَّهُ لَيْسَ لَكُنَّ أَنْ تَحْققْن الطَّرِيقَ، عَلَيْكُنَّ بِحَافَّاتِ الطَّرِيقِ"، فَكَانَتِ الْمَرْأَةُ تُلْصَقُ بِالْجِدَارِ، حَتَّى إِنَّ ثَوْبَهَا لِيَتَعَلَّقُ بِالْجِدَارِ، مِنْ لُصُوقِهَا بِهِ .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَتُوبُوا إِلَى اللَّهِ جَمِيعًا أَيُّهَا الْمُؤْمِنُونَ لَعَلَّكُمْ تُفْلِحُونَ﴾ أَيْ: افْعَلُوا مَا آمُرُكُمْ بِهِ مِنْ هَذِهِ الصِّفَاتِ الْجَمِيلَةِ وَالْأَخْلَاقِ الْجَلِيلَةِ، وَاتْرُكُوا مَا كَانَ عَلَيْهِ أَهْلُ الْجَاهِلِيَّةِ مِنَ الْأَخْلَاقِ وَالصِّفَاتِ الرَّذِيلَةِ، فَإِنَّ الفَلاح كُلَّ الفَلاح فِي فِعْلِ مَا أَمَرَ اللَّهُ بِهِ وَرَسُولُهُ، وَتَرْكِ مَا نَهَيَا عَنْهُ، والله تعالى هو المستعان [وعليه التكلان] .

---

## 24:32-34 — verses 32-34 (shared commentary)

### Translation

These noble, clarifying verses comprise several rulings that are firmly established and decisive commands.

His statement, exalted is He: {And marry those among you who are single, and the righteous among your male slaves and female slaves} is a command to marry. A group of scholars held that it is obligatory upon everyone who is able to do so. They cited as evidence the apparent meaning of his ﷺ statement: "O assembly of young men, whoever among you is able to marry should marry, for it is more restraining of the gaze and more protective of chastity. And whoever is not able should fast, for it is a suppressant for him." Both [Bukhari and Muslim] narrated it from the hadith of Ibn Mas'ud.

It has come in the Sunan, through more than one route, that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Marry, procreate, multiply, for I will boast of you before the nations on the Day of Resurrection." In one narration: "even by the miscarried fetus."

Al-Ayama (the unmarried) is the plural of ayyim, and this term is applied both to a woman who has no husband and to a man who has no wife, whether either of them was previously married and then separated, or never married at all. Al-Jawhari related this from the linguists, saying: one says "a man is ayyim" and "a woman is ayyim" as well.

His statement, exalted is He: {If they are poor, Allah will enrich them from His bounty, and Allah is All-Encompassing, All-Knowing}. Ali ibn Abi Talha reported from Ibn Abbas: Allah encouraged them toward marriage and commanded it for both free persons and slaves, and He promised them enrichment for it, saying: {If they are poor, Allah will enrich them from His bounty}.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] Sa'id, that is, Ibn Abd al-Aziz, said: It has reached me that Abu Bakr al-Siddiq, may Allah be pleased with him, said: Obey Allah in what He has commanded you regarding marriage, and He will fulfill for you what He promised of enrichment. He said: {If they are poor, Allah will enrich them from His bounty}.

And from Ibn Mas'ud: Seek enrichment through marriage, for Allah, exalted is He, says: {If they are poor, Allah will enrich them from His bounty}. Ibn Jarir narrated this, and al-Baghawi mentioned something similar from Umar.

From al-Layth, from Muhammad ibn Ajlan, from Sa'id al-Maqburi, from Abu Hurayrah, may Allah be pleased with him, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Three have a right upon Allah to help them: the one who marries seeking chastity, the mukatab (slave under a manumission contract) seeking to fulfill his payment, and the one fighting in the way of Allah." Imam Ahmad, al-Tirmidhi, al-Nasa'i, and Ibn Majah narrated it. The Messenger of Allah ﷺ married that man who found nothing but his lower garment and could not even afford an iron ring, and yet he married him to that woman, making her dowry his teaching her whatever he had memorized of the Qur'an.

What is known of Allah's generosity and kindness, exalted is He, is that He will provide for him and her what suffices them both. As for what many people cite as if it were a hadith: "Marry the poor and Allah will enrich you," it has no basis, and I have not seen it with any chain, strong or weak, up to now. The Qur'an suffices in place of it, as does this hadith which we have mentioned. Praise be to Allah.

His statement, exalted is He: {And let those who do not find [the means for] marriage abstain until Allah enriches them from His bounty}. This is a command from Allah, exalted is He, to whoever cannot find the means to marry, to abstain from what is forbidden, just as he, upon him be prayer and peace, said: "O assembly of young men, whoever among you is able to marry should marry, for it is more restraining of the gaze and more protective of chastity. And whoever is not able should fast, for it is a suppressant for him."

This verse is unrestricted, while the verse in Surat al-Nisa is more specific than it, namely His statement, exalted is He: {And whoever among you cannot afford to marry free believing women, then [he may marry] from those believing girls whom your right hands possess}, up to His saying: {That is for whoever among you fears sin, and that you be patient is better for you} [al-Nisa: 25], meaning: your patience in refraining from marrying female slaves is better, because the child born would be a slave. {And Allah is Forgiving, Merciful}.

Ikrimah said regarding His statement: {And let those who do not find [the means for] marriage abstain}: This refers to a man who sees a woman and feels desire as a result; if he has a wife, let him go to her and fulfill his need through her, and if he has no wife, let him reflect upon the dominion of the heavens [and the earth] until Allah enriches him.

His statement: {And those who seek a kitabah (manumission contract) from among those your right hands possess, then grant them the kitabah if you know any good in them}. This is a command from Allah, exalted is He, to masters, that when their slaves request a kitabah from them, they should grant it, on condition that the slave has some means and earning capacity by which he can pay his master the sum agreed upon. Many scholars held that this command is one of guidance and recommendation, not one of strict obligation, but rather that the master has a choice: if his slave requests a kitabah from him, he may grant it if he wishes, or decline if he wishes.

Al-Thawri said, from Jabir, from al-Sha'bi: If he wishes he may grant the kitabah, and if he wishes he may not.

Ibn Wahb said, from Isma'il ibn Ayyash, from a man, from Ata ibn Abi Rabah: If he wishes he grants the kitabah, and if he does not wish, he does not. Muqatil ibn Hayyan and al-Hasan al-Basri said likewise.

Others held that it is obligatory upon the master, when his slave requests this of him, to grant what he requested, taking the apparent meaning of this command.

Al-Bukhari said: Rawh said, from Ibn Jurayj: I said to Ata: [Is it obligatory upon me, if I know he has wealth, to grant him a kitabah? He said: I see it as nothing but obligatory. And Amr ibn Dinar said: I said to Ata], do you attribute this to anyone? He said: No. Then he informed me that Musa ibn Anas informed him that Sirin asked Anas for a kitabah, and Anas had much wealth, but he refused.

So Sirin went to Umar ibn al-Khattab, who said: Grant him the kitabah. He refused, so Umar struck him with the whip, reciting, may Allah be pleased with him: {Then grant them the kitabah if you know any good in them}. So he granted him the kitabah.

Al-Bukhari mentioned this as a mu'allaq (suspended) report. Abd al-Razzaq narrated it: Ibn Jurayj informed us, saying: I said to Ata: Is it obligatory upon me, if I know he has wealth, to grant him a kitabah? He said: I see it as nothing but obligatory. Amr ibn Dinar said: I said to Ata: Do you attribute this to anyone? He said: No.

Ibn Jarir said: [chain] from Anas ibn Malik: that Sirin wanted him to grant a kitabah, and he hesitated with him, so Umar said to him: You will surely grant him the kitabah. This is a sound (sahih) chain.

Sa'id ibn Mansur said: [chain] from al-Dahhak, who said: It is an azimah (a firm binding command).

This is the older of the two positions of al-Shafi'i, may Allah have mercy on him, while in the newer position he held that it is not obligatory, based on his ﷺ statement: "The property of a Muslim man is not lawful except with his willing consent."

Ibn Wahb said: Malik said: The position among us is that it is not incumbent upon a slave's master to grant him a kitabah when he requests it, and I have not heard of any of the imams compelling anyone to grant his slave a kitabah. Malik said: This is merely a command from Allah and a permission from Him to the people, not an obligation.

Al-Thawri, Abu Hanifah, Abd al-Rahman ibn Zayd ibn Aslam, and others said likewise. Ibn Jarir chose the position of obligation, based on the apparent meaning of the verse.

His statement: {If you know any good in them}. Some said: trustworthiness. Some said: honesty. [Some said: wealth]. Some said: means and earning capacity.

Abu Dawud narrated in Kitab al-Marasil, from Yahya ibn Abi Kathir, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said regarding {Then grant them the kitabah if you know any good in them}: "If you know they have a trade or craft, and do not send them out to be a burden upon the people."

His statement: {And give them from the wealth of Allah which He has given you}. The exegetes differed concerning it. Some said its meaning is: reduce for them some portion of the kitabah payment. Some of them said: a quarter of it. It was said: a third. It was said: a half. It was said: some portion of the kitabah, according to more than one report.

Others said: rather what is meant by His statement {And give them from the wealth of Allah which He has given you} is the share which Allah has ordained for them from the wealth of zakat. This is the position of al-Hasan, Abd al-Rahman ibn Zayd ibn Aslam and his father, and Muqatil ibn Hayyan. Ibn Jarir chose this view.

Ibrahim al-Nakha'i said regarding His statement {And give them from the wealth of Allah which He has given you}: He urged the people, both his master and others, toward it. Buraydah ibn al-Husayb al-Aslami and Qatadah said likewise.

Ibn Abbas said: Allah commanded the believers to assist in freeing slaves.

It has already come earlier in the hadith, from the Prophet ﷺ, that he said: "Three have a right to God's help": and he mentioned among them the mukatab (one bound by a manumission contract) who wants to fulfill his payment. But the first opinion is more well known.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: Muhammad ibn Isma'il narrated to us, Waki' narrated to us, from Ibn Shabib, from Ikrimah, from Ibn Abbas, from Umar: that he made a manumission contract (kitabah) with a slave of his, known as Abu Umayyah, and the slave brought his installment payment when it fell due. Umar said: "O Abu Umayyah, go and use it to help yourself with your contract payments." He said: "O Commander of the Faithful, what if you left it until it were the last installment?" Umar said: "I fear I will not live to see that." Then he recited: {So make contracts with them if you know good in them, and give them from the wealth of God which He has given you}. Ikrimah said: This was the first installment ever remitted in Islam.

Ibn Jarir said: Ibn Humayd narrated to us, Harun ibn al-Mughirah narrated to us, from Anbasah, from Salim al-Aftas, from Sa'id ibn Jubayr, who said: Ibn Umar, when he made a manumission contract with his mukatab, would not remit anything from the first of his installments, fearing that he might fail and his charity would then revert to him. But when it came to the last of his contract payments, he would remit whatever he wished.

Ali ibn Abi Talhah said, from Ibn Abbas, regarding {and give them from the wealth of God which He has given you}: it means, remit for them part of their contract payment. Mujahid, Ata', al-Qasim ibn Abi Bazzah, Abd al-Karim ibn Malik al-Jazari, and al-Suddi said likewise.

Muhammad ibn Sirin said concerning His statement, {and give them from the wealth of God which He has given you}: they used to like for a man to leave for his mukatab a portion of his contract payment.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: al-Fadl ibn Shadhan al-Muqri informed us, Ibrahim ibn Musa informed us, Hisham ibn Yusuf informed us, from Ibn Jurayj, Ata' ibn al-Sa'ib informed me: that Abdullah ibn Jundab informed him, from Ali, may God be pleased with him, from the Prophet ﷺ, who said: "A quarter of the contract payment."

This is a gharib (singular) hadith, and its being raised to the Prophet ﷺ (marfu') is objectionable (munkar). The more likely view is that it is mawquf (halted report) upon Ali, may God be pleased with him, as Abu Abd al-Rahman al-Sulami, may God have mercy on him, narrated it from him.

* *

His statement: {And do not compel your slave girls to prostitution if they desire chastity, seeking the goods of the life of this world} to the end of the verse: The people of the Jahiliyyah (pre-Islamic ignorance), when one of them had a slave girl, would send her out to commit adultery and impose upon her a levy that he would take from her at every set time. Then when Islam came, God forbade the Muslims from that.

The reason for the revelation of this noble verse, as mentioned by more than one of the commentators among the earlier and later scholars, concerned the matter of Abdullah ibn Ubayy ibn Salul [the hypocrite], for he had slave girls whom he would compel to prostitution, seeking their earnings, desiring their children, and out of a kind of leadership he claimed for himself [may God disfigure and curse him]. [Mention of the reports transmitted concerning this]

The hafiz Abu Bakr Ahmad ibn Amr ibn Abd al-Khaliq al-Bazzar, may God have mercy on him, said in his Musnad: Ahmad ibn Dawud al-Wasiti narrated to us, Abu Amr al-Lakhmi, that is, Muhammad ibn al-Hajjaj, narrated to us, Muhammad ibn Ishaq narrated to us, from al-Zuhri, who said: Abdullah ibn Ubayy ibn Salul had a slave girl called Mu'adhah, whom he would compel to fornication. Then when Islam came, this was revealed: {And do not compel your slave girls to prostitution} up to His statement: {then indeed God, after their compulsion, is Forgiving and Merciful}.

Al-A'mash said, from Abu Sufyan, from Jabir, regarding this verse, {And do not compel your slave girls to prostitution}: it was revealed concerning a slave girl of Abdullah ibn Ubayy ibn Salul called Musaykah, whom he would compel to immorality, and she was a decent girl who refused. So God, Mighty and Majestic, revealed this verse up to His statement, {and whoever compels them, then indeed God, after their compulsion, is Forgiving and Merciful}.

Al-Nasa'i narrated, from the hadith of Ibn Jurayj, from Abu al-Zubayr, from Jabir, something similar.

The hafiz Abu Bakr al-Bazzar said: Amr ibn Ali narrated to us, Ali ibn Sa'id narrated to us, al-A'mash narrated to us, Abu Sufyan narrated to me, from Jabir, who said: Abdullah ibn Ubayy ibn Salul had a slave girl called Musaykah, whom he would compel to prostitution. So God revealed: {And do not compel your slave girls to prostitution}, up to His statement: {and whoever compels them, then indeed God, after their compulsion, is Forgiving and Merciful}.

Al-A'mash explicitly stated that he heard directly from Abu Sufyan Talhah ibn Nafi', which proves the falsity of the claim of those who said "he did not hear from him, it is only a written document (sahifah)." Al-Bazzar related this.

Abu Dawud al-Tayalisi said, from Sulayman ibn Mu'adh, from Simak, from Ikrimah, from Ibn Abbas: that a slave girl of Abdullah ibn Ubayy used to commit adultery during the Jahiliyyah, and she bore children from that adultery. Then he said to her: "What is wrong with you, why do you not commit adultery?" She said: "No, by God, I will not commit adultery." So he beat her, and God, Mighty and Majestic, revealed: {And do not compel your slave girls to prostitution if they desire chastity}.

Abd al-Razzaq said: Ma'mar informed us, from al-Zuhri: that a man of the Quraysh was taken captive on the day of Badr, and he was held captive by Abdullah ibn Ubayy. Abdullah ibn Ubayy had a slave girl called Mu'adhah, and the Qurayshi captive wanted her for himself, but she was a Muslim and refused him because of her Islam. Abdullah ibn Ubayy would compel her toward that and beat her, hoping that she would conceive from the Qurayshi so that he could demand ransom for the child. So He, Blessed and Exalted, said: {And do not compel your slave girls to prostitution if they desire chastity}.

Al-Suddi said: this noble verse was revealed concerning Abdullah ibn Ubayy ibn Salul, the leader of the hypocrites, who had a slave girl called Mu'adhah. Whenever a guest came to stay with him, he would send her to him so that he might have relations with her, seeking reward and honor from him for this, as he claimed. The slave girl came to Abu Bakr, may God be pleased with him, and complained to him about this. Abu Bakr mentioned it to the Prophet ﷺ, who ordered that she be taken from him. Abdullah ibn Ubayy then cried out: "Who will excuse me from Muhammad, who overpowers us regarding our own property?" So God revealed this concerning them.

Muqatil ibn Hayyan said: it has reached us, and God knows best, that this verse was revealed concerning two men who used to compel two slave girls of theirs, one of them named Musaykah, who belonged to the Ansari man, while Umaymah, the mother of Musaykah, belonged to Abdullah ibn Ubayy, and Mu'adhah and Arwa were in the same position. Musaykah and her mother came to the Prophet ﷺ and mentioned this to him, so God revealed concerning that: {And do not compel your slave girls to prostitution}, meaning adultery.

* *

His statement: {if they desire chastity}: this is expressed according to the general case, so it has no restrictive implication (there is no exclusion implied for the other case). His statement: {seeking the goods of the life of this world}, that is, from their earnings, their bride prices, and their children. The Messenger of God ﷺ forbade the earnings of the cupper, the fee of the prostitute, and the fee of the soothsayer (hulwan al-kahin), and in another version: "The fee of the prostitute is filthy, the earnings of the cupper are filthy, and the price of the dog is filthy."

* *

His statement: {and whoever compels them, then indeed God, after their compulsion, is Forgiving and Merciful}, that is, forgiving toward them, as already came in the hadith from Jabir.

Ibn Abi Talhah said, from Ibn Abbas: "if you do that, then indeed God is Forgiving and Merciful toward them," and their sin falls upon whoever compelled them. Mujahid, Ata' al-Khurasani, al-A'mash, and Qatadah said likewise.

Abu Ubayd said: Ishaq al-Azraq narrated to me, from Awf, from al-Hasan, regarding this verse, {then indeed God, after their compulsion, is Forgiving and Merciful}: he said, "for them, by God. For them, by God."

From al-Zuhri, he said: "Forgiving toward them for what they were compelled to do."

From Zayd ibn Aslam, he said: "Forgiving and Merciful toward the women who were compelled."

Ibn al-Mundhir related these in his tafsir with their chains of transmission.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: Abu Zur'ah narrated to us, Yahya ibn Abdullah narrated to us, Ibn Lahi'ah narrated to me, Ata' narrated to me, from Sa'id ibn Jubayr, who said: in the reading of Abdullah ibn Mas'ud: "then indeed God, after their compulsion, is Forgiving and Merciful toward them," and their sin falls upon whoever compelled them.

And in the hadith raised to the Messenger of God ﷺ, he said: "Lifted from my nation is error, forgetfulness, and what they were compelled to do."

When the Exalted had detailed and clarified these rulings, He said: {And We have certainly sent down to you verses making things clear}, meaning: the Qur'an, in which there are clear, explanatory verses, {and an example from those who passed away before you}, meaning: news of the past nations and what befell them for their opposition to the commands of God, the Exalted, as He, the Exalted, said: {So We made them a precedent and an example for the later people} [al-Zukhruf: 56].

{and an admonition}

That is: a deterrent against committing sins and forbidden acts. {For the God-fearing} means: for whoever fears Allah and is in awe of Him.

Ali ibn Abi Talib, may Allah be pleased with him, said in describing the Qur'an: In it is the judgment concerning what is between you, the report of what came before you, and the news of what comes after you. It is the decisive word, not one of jest. Whoever among the tyrants abandons it, Allah will break him, and whoever seeks guidance from other than it, Allah will lead him astray.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

اشْتَمَلَتْ هَذِهِ الْآيَاتُ الْكَرِيمَاتُ الْمُبِينَةُ عَلَى جُمَلٍ مِنَ الْأَحْكَامِ الْمُحْكَمَةِ، وَالْأَوَامِرِ الْمُبْرَمَةِ، فَقَوْلُهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَأَنْكِحُوا الأيَامَى مِنْكُمْ وَالصَّالِحِينَ مِنْ عِبَادِكُمْ وَإِمَائِكُمْ﴾ : هَذَا أَمْرٌ بِالتَّزْوِيجِ. وَقَدْ ذَهَبَ طَائِفَةٌ مِنَ الْعُلَمَاءِ إِلَى وُجُوبِهِ، عَلَى كُلِّ مَنْ قَدَر عَلَيْهِ. وَاحْتَجُّوا بِظَاهِرِ قَوْلِهِ ﷺ: "يَا مَعْشَرَ الشَّبَابِ، مَنِ اسْتَطَاعَ مِنْكُمُ الْبَاءَةَ فَلْيَتَزَوَّجْ، فَإِنَّهُ أَغَضُّ لِلْبَصَرِ، وَأَحْصَنُ لِلْفَرْجِ، وَمَنْ لَمْ يَسْتَطِعْ فَعَلَيْهِ بِالصَّوْمِ فَإِنَّهُ لَهُ وِجَاءٌ". أَخْرَجَاهُ مِنْ حَدِيثِ ابْنِ مَسْعُودٍ .

وَجَاءَ فِي السُّنَنِ -مِنْ غَيْرِ وَجْهٍ -أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ صَلَّى الله عليه وسلم قال: "تَزَوَّجوا، تَوَالَدُوا، تَنَاسَلُوا، فَإِنِّي مُبَاهٍ بِكُمُ الْأُمَمَ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ" وَفِي رِوَايَةٍ: "حَتَّى بِالسِّقْطِ".

الْأَيَامَى: جَمْعُ أيِّم، وَيُقَالُ ذَلِكَ لِلْمَرْأَةِ الَّتِي لَا زَوْجَ لَهَا، وَلِلرَّجُلِ الَّذِي لَا زَوْجَةَ لَهُ. وَسَوَاءٌ كَانَ قَدْ تَزَوَّجَ ثُمَّ فَارَقَ، أَوْ لَمْ يَتَزَوَّجْ وَاحِدٌ مِنْهُمَا، حَكَاهُ الْجَوْهَرِيُّ عَنْ أَهْلِ اللُّغَةِ، يُقَالُ: رَجُلٌ أَيِّمٌ وَامْرَأَةٌ أَيِّمٌ أَيْضًا.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿إِنْ يَكُونُوا فُقَرَاءَ يُغْنِهِمُ اللَّهُ مِنْ فَضْلِهِ وَاللَّهُ وَاسِعٌ عَلِيمٌ﴾ ، قَالَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: رَغَّبَهُمُ اللَّهُ فِي التَّزْوِيجِ، وَأَمَرَ بِهِ الْأَحْرَارَ وَالْعَبِيدَ، وَوَعَدَهُمْ عَلَيْهِ الْغِنَى، فَقَالَ: ﴿إِنْ يَكُونُوا فُقَرَاءَ يُغْنِهِمُ اللَّهُ مِنْ فَضْلِهِ﴾ .

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا مَحْمُودُ بْنُ خَالِدٍ الْأَزْرَقُ، حَدَّثَنَا عُمَرُ بْنُ عَبْدِ الْوَاحِدِ، عَنْ سَعِيدٍ -يَعْنِي: ابْنَ عَبْدِ الْعَزِيزِ -قَالَ: بَلَغَنِي أَنَّ أَبَا بَكْرٍ الصِّدِّيقَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: أَطِيعُوا اللَّهَ فِيمَا أَمَرَكُمْ بِهِ مِنَ النِّكَاحِ، يُنْجِزْ [لَكُمْ] مَا وَعَدَكُمْ مِنَ الْغِنَى، قَالَ: ﴿إِنْ يَكُونُوا فُقَرَاءَ يُغْنِهِمُ اللَّهُ مِنْ فَضْلِهِ﴾ .

وَعَنِ ابْنِ مَسْعُودٍ: الْتَمِسُوا الْغِنَى فِي النِّكَاحِ، يَقُولُ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿إِنْ يَكُونُوا فُقَرَاءَ يُغْنِهِمُ اللَّهُ مِنْ فَضْلِهِ﴾ رَوَاهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ، وَذَكَرَ الْبَغَوِيُّ عَنْ عُمَرَ بِنَحْوِهِ.

وَعَنِ اللَّيْثِ، عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ عَجْلان، عَنْ سَعِيدٍ المقْبُرِي، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "ثَلَاثَةٌ حَقٌّ عَلَى اللَّهِ عَوْنهم: النَّاكِحُ يُرِيدُ الْعَفَافَ، والمكاتَب يُرِيدُ الْأَدَاءَ، وَالْغَازِي فِي سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ". رَوَاهُ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ، وَالتِّرْمِذِيُّ، وَالنَّسَائِيُّ، وَابْنُ مَاجَهْ وَقَدْ زوَّج رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ ذَلِكَ الرَّجُلَ الَّذِي لَمْ يَجِدْ إِلَّا إِزَارَهُ ، وَلَمْ يَقْدِرْ عَلَى خَاتَمٍ مِنْ حَدِيدٍ، وَمَعَ هَذَا فَزَوَّجَهُ بِتِلْكَ الْمَرْأَةِ، وَجَعَلَ صَدَاقَهَا عَلَيْهِ أَنْ يُعَلِّمَهَا مَا يَحْفَظُهُ مِنَ الْقُرْآنِ.

وَالْمَعْهُودُ مِنْ كَرَمِ اللَّهِ تَعَالَى وَلُطْفِهِ أَنْ يَرْزُقَهُ [وَإِيَّاهَا] مَا فِيهِ كِفَايَةٌ لَهُ وَلَهَا. فَأَمَّا مَا يُورِدُهُ كَثِيرٌ مِنَ النَّاسِ عَلَى أَنَّهُ حَدِيثُ: "تَزَوَّجُوا فُقَرَاءَ يُغْنِكُمُ اللَّهُ"، فَلَا أَصْلَ لَهُ، وَلَمْ أَرَهُ بِإِسْنَادٍ قَوِيٍّ وَلَا ضَعِيفٍ إِلَى الْآنَ، وَفِي الْقُرْآنِ غَنِيَّةٌ عَنْهُ، وَكَذَا هَذَا الْحَدِيثُ الَّذِي أَوْرَدْنَاهُ. وَلِلَّهِ الْحَمْدُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلْيَسْتَعْفِفِ الَّذِينَ لَا يَجِدُونَ نِكَاحًا حَتَّى يُغْنِيَهُمُ اللَّهُ مِنْ فَضْلِهِ﴾ . هَذَا أَمْرٌ مِنَ اللَّهِ تَعَالَى لِمَنْ لَا يَجِدُ تَزْوِيجًا [بِالتَّعَفُّفِ] عَنِ الْحَرَامِ، كَمَا قَالَ -عَلَيْهِ الصَّلَاةُ وَالسَّلَامُ -: "يَا مَعْشَرَ الشَّبَابِ، مَنِ اسْتَطَاعَ مِنْكُمُ الْبَاءَةَ فَلْيَتَزَوَّجْ، فَإِنَّهُ أغَضُّ لِلْبَصَرِ، وأحْصَنُ لِلْفَرْجِ. وَمَنْ لَمْ يَسْتَطِعْ فَعَلَيْهِ بِالصَّوْمِ فَإِنَّهُ لَهُ وِجَاء".

وَهَذِهِ الْآيَةُ مُطْلَقَةٌ، وَالَّتِي فِي سُورَةِ النِّسَاءِ أَخَصُّ مِنْهَا، وَهِيَ قَوْلُهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَمَنْ لَمْ يَسْتَطِعْ مِنْكُمْ طَوْلا أَنْ يَنْكِحَ الْمُحْصَنَاتِ الْمُؤْمِنَاتِ فَمِنْ مَا مَلَكَتْ أَيْمَانُكُمْ مِنْ فَتَيَاتِكُمُ الْمُؤْمِنَاتِ﴾ ، إِلَى أَنْ قَالَ: ﴿ذَلِكَ لِمَنْ خَشِيَ الْعَنَتَ مِنْكُمْ وَأَنْ تَصْبِرُوا خَيْرٌ لَكُمْ﴾ [النِّسَاءِ: ٢٥] أَيْ صَبْرُكُمْ عَنْ تَزْوِيجِ الْإِمَاءِ خَيْرٌ؛ لِأَنَّ الْوَلَدَ يَجِيءُ رَقِيقًا، ﴿وَاللَّهُ غَفُورٌ رَحِيمٌ﴾ .

قَالَ عِكْرِمَةُ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَلْيَسْتَعْفِفِ الَّذِينَ لَا يَجِدُونَ نِكَاحًا﴾ قَالَ: هُوَ الرَّجُلُ يَرَى الْمَرْأَةَ فَكَأَنَّهُ يَشْتَهِي، فَإِنْ كَانَتْ لَهُ امْرَأَةٌ فَلْيَذْهَبْ إِلَيْهَا وَلْيَقْضِ حَاجَتَهُ مِنْهَا، وَإِنْ لَمْ يَكُنْ لَهُ امرأة فلينظر في ملكوت السموات [وَالْأَرْضِ] حَتَّى يُغْنِيَهُ اللَّهُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَالَّذِينَ يَبْتَغُونَ الْكِتَابَ مِمَّا مَلَكَتْ أَيْمَانُكُمْ فَكَاتِبُوهُمْ إِنْ عَلِمْتُمْ فِيهِمْ خَيْرًا﴾ هَذَا أَمْرٌ مِنَ اللَّهِ تَعَالَى لِلسَّادَةِ إِذَا طَلَبَ مِنْهُمْ عَبِيدُهُمُ الْكِتَابَةَ أَنْ يُكَاتِبُوا ، بِشَرْطِ أَنْ يَكُونَ لِلْعَبْدِ حِيلَةٌ وَكَسْبٌ يُؤَدِّي إِلَى سيِّده الْمَالَ الَّذِي شَارَطَهُ عَلَى أَدَائِهِ. وَقَدْ ذَهَبَ كَثِيرٌ مِنَ الْعُلَمَاءِ إِلَى أَنَّ هَذَا الْأَمْرَ أمرُ إِرْشَادٍ وَاسْتِحْبَابٍ، لَا أَمْرَ تَحَتُّمٍ وَإِيجَابٍ، بَلِ السَّيِّدُ مُخَيَّرٌ، إِذَا طَلَبَ مِنْهُ عَبْدُهُ الْكِتَابَةَ إِنْ شَاءَ كَاتَبَهُ، وَإِنْ شَاءَ لَمْ يُكَاتِبْهُ.

وَقَالَ الثَّوْرِيُّ، عَنْ جَابِرٍ، عَنِ الشَّعْبِيِّ: إِنْ شَاءَ كَاتَبَهُ وَإِنْ شَاءَ لَمْ يُكَاتِبْهُ.

وَقَالَ ابْنِ وَهْبٍ، عَنْ إِسْمَاعِيلَ بْنِ عَيَّاشٍ، عَنْ رَجُلٍ، عَنْ عَطَاءِ بْنِ أَبِي رَبَاح: إِنْ يَشَأْ يُكَاتِبْهُ وَإِنْ لَمْ يَشَأْ لَمْ يُكَاتِبْهُ ، وَكَذَا قَالَ مُقاتل بْنُ حَيَّان، وَالْحَسَنُ الْبَصْرِيُّ.

وَذَهَبَ آخَرُونَ إِلَى أَنَّهُ يَجِبُ عَلَى السَّيِّدِ إِذَا طَلَبَ مِنْهُ عبدُه ذَلِكَ، أَنْ يُجِيبَهُ إِلَى مَا طَلَبَ؛ أَخْذًا بِظَاهِرِ هَذَا الْأَمْرِ:

قَالَ الْبُخَارِيُّ: وَقَالَ رَوْحٌ، عَنِ ابْنِ جُرَيْج قُلْتُ لِعَطَاءٍ: [أَوَاجِبٌ عَلَيَّ إِذَا عَلِمْتُ لَهُ مَالًا أَنْ أُكَاتِبَهُ؟ قَالَ: مَا أَرَاهُ إِلَّا وَاجِبًا. وَقَالَ عَمْرُو بْنُ دِينَارٍ: قُلْتُ لِعَطَاءٍ] ، أتأثُرُه عَنْ أَحَدٍ؟ قَالَ: لَا. ثُمَّ أَخْبَرَنِي أَنَّ مُوسَى بْنَ أَنَسٍ أَخْبَرَهُ، أَنَّ سِيرِينَ سَأَلَ أَنَسًا المكاتبةَ -وكان كثير المال، فأبى.

فَانْطَلَقَ إِلَى عُمَرَ بْنِ الْخَطَّابِ فَقَالَ: كَاتِبْهُ. فَأَبَى، فَضَرَبَهُ بِالدُّرَّةِ، وَيَتْلُو عُمَرُ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ: ﴿فَكَاتِبُوهُمْ إِنْ عَلِمْتُمْ فِيهِمْ خَيْرًا﴾ ، فَكَاتَبَهُ 

هَكَذَا ذَكَرَهُ الْبُخَارِيُّ تَعْلِيقًا . وَرَوَاهُ عَبْدُ الرَّزَّاقِ: أَخْبَرَنَا ابْنُ جِرَيْجٍ قَالَ: قُلْتُ لِعَطَاءٍ: أَوَاجِبٌ عَلَيَّ إِذَا عَلِمْتُ لَهُ مَالًا أَنْ أُكَاتِبَهُ؟ قَالَ: مَا أَرَاهُ إِلَّا وَاجِبًا. وَقَالَ عَمْرُو بْنُ دِينَارٍ، قَالَ: قُلْتُ لِعَطَاءٍ: أَتَأْثِرُهُ عَنْ أَحَدٍ؟ قَالَ: لَا 

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ بَشَّار، حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ بَكْرٍ، حَدَّثَنَا سَعِيدٌ، عَنْ قَتَادَةَ، عَنْ أَنَسِ بْنِ مَالِكٍ: أَنَّ سِيرِينَ أَرَادَ أَنْ يُكَاتِبَهُ، فَتَلَكَّأَ عَلَيْهِ، فَقَالَ لَهُ عُمَرُ: لتكاتِبَنَّه. إِسْنَادٌ صَحِيحٌ .

وَقَالَ سَعِيدُ بْنُ مَنْصُورٍ: حَدَّثَنَا هُشَيْم بْنُ جُوَيْبِر، عَنِ الضَّحَّاكِ قَالَ: هِيَ عَزْمة.

وَهَذَا هُوَ الْقَوْلُ الْقَدِيمُ مِنْ قَوْلَيِ الشَّافِعِيِّ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ، وَذَهَبَ فِي الْجَدِيدِ إِلَى أَنَّهُ لَا يَجِبُ؛ لِقَوْلِهِ عَلَيْهِ الصَّلَاةُ وَالسَّلَامُ: لَا يَحِلُّ مَالُ امْرِئٍ مُسْلِمٍ إِلَّا بِطِيبٍ مِنْ نَفْسِهِ" .

وَقَالَ ابْنُ وَهْبٍ: قَالَ مَالِكٌ: الْأَمْرُ عِنْدَنَا أنْ لَيْسَ عَلَى سَيِّدِ الْعَبْدِ أَنْ يُكَاتِبَهُ إِذَا سَأَلَهُ ذَلِكَ، وَلَمْ أَسْمَعْ أَحَدًا مِنَ الْأَئِمَّةِ أَكْرَهَ أَحَدًا عَلَى أَنْ يُكَاتِبَ عَبْدَهُ. قَالَ مَالِكٌ: وَإِنَّمَا ذَلِكَ أَمْرٌ مِنَ اللَّهِ، وَإِذَنٌ مِنْهُ لِلنَّاسِ، وَلَيْسَ بِوَاجِبٍ.

وَكَذَا قَالَ الثَّوْرِيُّ، وَأَبُو حَنِيفَةَ، وَعَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ، وَغَيْرُهُمْ. وَاخْتَارَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ قَوْلَ الْوُجُوبِ لِظَاهِرِ الْآيَةِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿إِنْ عَلِمْتُمْ فِيهِمْ خَيْرًا﴾ ، قَالَ بَعْضُهُمْ: أَمَانَةً. وَقَالَ بَعْضُهُمْ: صِدْقًا. [وَقَالَ بَعْضُهُمْ: مَالًا] وَقَالَ بَعْضُهُمْ: حِيلَةً وَكَسْبًا.

وَرَوَى أَبُو دَاوُدَ فِي كِتَابِ الْمَرَاسِيلِ، عَنْ يَحْيَى بْنِ أَبِي كَثِيرٍ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: ﴿فَكَاتِبُوهُمْ إِنْ عَلِمْتُمْ فِيهِمْ خَيْرًا﴾ قَالَ: "إِنْ عَلِمْتُمْ فِيهِمْ حِرْفَةً، وَلَا تُرْسِلُوهُمْ كَلا عَلَى النَّاسِ".

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَآتُوهُمْ مِنْ مَالِ اللَّهِ الَّذِي آتَاكُمْ﴾ اخْتَلَفَ الْمُفَسِّرُونَ فِيهِ، فَقَالَ قَائِلُونَ: مَعْنَاهُ اطْرَحُوا لَهُمْ مِنَ الْكِتَابَةِ بَعْضَهَا، ثُمَّ قَالَ بَعْضُهُمْ: مِقْدَارَ الرُّبْعِ. وَقِيلَ: الثُّلُثُ. وَقِيلَ: النِّصْفُ. وَقِيلَ: جُزْءٌ مِنَ الْكِتَابَةِ مِنْ غَيْرِ وَاحِدٍ.

وَقَالَ آخَرُونَ: بَلِ الْمُرَادُ مِنْ قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَآتُوهُمْ مِنْ مَالِ اللَّهِ الَّذِي آتَاكُمْ﴾ هُوَ النَّصِيبُ الَّذِي فَرَضَ اللَّهُ لَهُمْ مِنْ أَمْوَالِ الزِّكَوَاتِ. وَهَذَا قَوْلُ الْحَسَنُ، وَعَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ، وَأَبِيهِ، وَمُقَاتِلِ بْنِ حَيَّانَ. وَاخْتَارَهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ.

وَقَالَ إِبْرَاهِيمُ النَّخَعِيّ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَآتُوهُمْ مِنْ مَالِ اللَّهِ الَّذِي آتَاكُمْ﴾ قَالَ: حَثَّ النَّاسَ عَلَيْهِ مَوْلَاهُ وَغَيْرُهُ. وَكَذَلِكَ قَالَ بُرَيْدة بْنُ الحُصَيب الْأَسْلَمِيُّ، وَقَتَادَةُ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: أَمَرَ اللَّهِ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ أَنْ يُعِينُوا فِي الرِّقَابِ. وَقَدْ تقدَّمَ فِي الْحَدِيثِ، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: "ثَلَاثَةٌ حَقٌّ عَلَى اللَّهِ عَوْنُهُمْ": فَذَكَرَ مِنْهُمُ المكاتَب يُرِيدُ الْأَدَاءَ، وَالْقَوْلُ الْأَوَّلُ أَشْهَرُ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْمَاعِيلَ، حَدَّثَنَا وَكِيع، عَنِ ابْنِ شَبِيب، عَنْ عِكْرِمَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، عَنْ عُمَرَ؛ أَنَّهُ كَاتَبَ عَبْدًا لَهُ، يُكَنَّى أَبَا أُمَيَّةَ، فَجَاءَ بِنَجْمِهِ حِينَ حُلَّ، فَقَالَ: يَا أَبَا أُمَيَّةَ، اذْهَبْ فَاسْتَعِنْ بِهِ فِي مُكَاتَبَتِكَ. قَالَ: يَا أَمِيرَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ، لَوْ تركتَه حَتَّى يَكُونَ مِنْ آخِرِ نَجْمٍ؟ قَالَ: أَخَافُ أَلَّا أُدْرِكَ ذَلِكَ. ثُمَّ قَرَأَ: ﴿فَكَاتِبُوهُمْ إِنْ عَلِمْتُمْ فِيهِمْ خَيْرًا وَآتُوهُمْ مِنْ مَالِ اللَّهِ الَّذِي آتَاكُمْ﴾ قَالَ عِكْرِمَةُ: كَانَ أَوَّلَ نَجْمٍ أُدِّيَ فِي الْإِسْلَامِ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ حُمَيْدٍ، حَدَّثَنَا هَارُونُ بْنُ الْمُغِيرَةِ، عَنْ عنبسَةَ، عَنْ سَالِمٍ الْأَفْطَسِ، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْرٍ قَالَ: كَانَ ابْنُ عُمَرَ إِذَا كَاتَبَ مكاتَبه لَمْ يَضَعْ عَنْهُ شَيْئًا مِنْ أَوَّلِ نُجُومِهِ، مَخَافَةَ أَنْ يَعْجَزَ فَتَرْجِعَ إِلَيْهِ صَدَقَتُهُ. وَلَكِنَّهُ إِذَا كَانَ فِي آخِرِ مُكَاتَبَتِهِ، وَضَعَ عَنْهُ مَا أَحَبَّ .

وَقَالَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: ﴿وَآتُوهُمْ مِنْ مَالِ اللَّهِ الَّذِي آتَاكُمْ﴾ قَالَ: يَعْنِي: ضَعُوا عَنْهُمْ مِنْ مُكَاتَبَتِهِمْ. وَكَذَلِكَ قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ، وَعَطَاءٌ، وَالْقَاسِمُ بْنُ أَبِي بَزَّة، وَعَبْدُ الْكَرِيمِ بْنُ مَالِكٍ الجَزَريّ، وَالسُّدِّيُّ.

وَقَالَ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ سِيرِينَ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَآتُوهُمْ مِنْ مَالِ اللَّهِ الَّذِي آتَاكُمْ﴾ : كَانَ يُعْجِبُهُمْ أَنْ يَدَعَ الرَّجُلُ لمكاتَبه طَائِفَةً مِنْ مُكَاتَبَتِهِ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: أَخْبَرَنَا الْفَضْلُ بْنُ شَاذَانَ الْمُقْرِئُ، أَخْبَرَنَا إِبْرَاهِيمُ بْنُ مُوسَى، أَخْبَرَنَا هِشَامُ بْنُ يُوسُفَ، عَنِ ابْنِ جُرَيْج، أَخْبَرَنِي عَطَاءُ بْنُ السَّائِبِ: أَنَّ عَبْدَ اللَّهِ بْنَ جُنْدَبٍ أَخْبَرَهُ، عَنْ عَلِيٍّ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ قَالَ: "رُبْعُ الْكِتَابَةِ" .

وَهَذَا حَدِيثٌ غَرِيبٌ، وَرَفْعُهُ مُنْكَرٌ، وَالْأَشْبَهُ أَنَّهُ مَوْقُوفٌ عَلَى عَلِيٍّ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، كَمَا رَوَاهُ عَنْهُ أَبُو عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ السُّلَمِيُّ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَلا تُكْرِهُوا فَتَيَاتِكُمْ عَلَى الْبِغَاءِ إِنْ أَرَدْنَ تَحَصُّنًا لِتَبْتَغُوا عَرَضَ الْحَيَاةِ الدُّنْيَا﴾ الْآيَةَ: كَانَ أَهْلُ الْجَاهِلِيَّةِ إِذَا كَانَ لِأَحَدِهِمْ أَمَةٌ، أَرْسَلَهَا تَزْنِي، وَجَعَلَ عَلَيْهَا ضَرِيبَةً يَأْخُذُهَا مِنْهَا كُلَّ وَقْتٍ. فَلَمَّا جَاءَ الْإِسْلَامُ، نَهَى اللَّهُ الْمُسْلِمِينَ عَنْ ذَلِكَ.

وَكَانَ سَبَبُ نُزُولِ هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ الْكَرِيمَةِ -فِيمَا ذَكَرَهُ غَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ مِنَ الْمُفَسِّرِينَ، مِنَ السَّلَفِ وَالْخَلَفِ -فِي شَأْنِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ أُبَيِّ بْنِ سَلُولٍ [الْمُنَافِقِ] فَإِنَّهُ كَانَ لَهُ إِمَاءٌ، فَكَانَ يُكْرِهْهُنَّ عَلَى البِغاء طَلَبًا لخَراجهن، وَرَغْبَةً فِي أَوْلَادِهِنَّ، وَرِئَاسَةً مِنْهُ فِيمَا يَزْعُمُ [قبحه الله ولعنه] [ذِكْرُ الْآثَارِ الْوَارِدَةِ فِي ذَلِكَ]
