قَالَ الْحَافِظُ أَبُو بَكْرٍ أَحْمَدُ بْنُ عَمْرٍو بْنِ عَبْدِ الْخَالِقِ البزَّار، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ، فِي مَسْنَدِهِ: حَدَّثَنَا أَحْمَدُ بْنُ دَاوُدَ الْوَاسِطِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو عَمْرٍو اللَّخْمِيُّ -يَعْنِي: مُحَمَّدَ بْنَ الْحَجَّاجِ -حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ ابن إِسْحَاقَ، عَنِ الزُّهْرِيِّ قَالَ: كَانَتْ جَارِيَةٌ لِعَبْدِ الله بن أبي ابن سَلُولٍ، يُقَالُ لَهَا: مُعَاذَةُ، يُكْرِهُهَا عَلَى الزِّنَى، فَلَمَّا جَاءَ الْإِسْلَامُ نَزَلَتْ: ﴿وَلا تُكْرِهُوا فَتَيَاتِكُمْ عَلَى الْبِغَاءِ﴾ إِلَى قَوْلِهِ: ﴿فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ مِنْ بَعْدِ إِكْرَاهِهِنَّ غَفُورٌ رَحِيمٌ﴾ 

وَقَالَ الْأَعْمَشُ، عَنْ أَبِي سُفْيَانَ، عَنْ جَابِرٍ فِي هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ: ﴿وَلا تُكْرِهُوا فَتَيَاتِكُمْ عَلَى الْبِغَاءِ﴾ قَالَ: نَزَلَتْ فِي أَمَةٍ لِعَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ أُبَيِّ بْنِ سَلُولٍ يُقَالُ لَهَا: مُسَيْكَة، كَانَ يُكْرِهُهَا عَلَى الْفُجُورِ -وَكَانَتْ لَا بَأْسَ بِهَا -فَتَأْبَى. فَأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، هَذِهِ الْآيَةَ إِلَى قَوْلِهِ ﴿وَمَنْ يُكْرِهْهُنَّ فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ مِنْ بَعْدِ إِكْرَاهِهِنَّ غَفُورٌ رَحِيمٌ﴾ .

وَرَوَى النَّسَائِيُّ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ ابْنِ جُرَيْج، عَنْ أَبِي الزُّبَيْرِ، عَنْ جَابِرِ نَحْوَهُ 

وَقَالَ الْحَافِظُ أَبُو بَكْرٍ الْبَزَّارُ: حَدَّثَنَا عَمْرُو بْنُ عَلِيٍّ، حَدَّثَنَا عَلِيُّ بْنُ سَعِيدٍ، حَدَّثَنَا الْأَعْمَشُ، حَدَّثَنِي أَبُو سُفْيَانَ، عَنْ جَابِرٍ قَالَ: كان لعبد الله بن أُبَيٍّ ابنِ سلولَ جَارِيَةٌ يُقَالُ لَهَا: مُسَيْكَةُ، وَكَانَ يُكْرِهُهَا عَلَى الْبِغَاءِ، فَأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ: ﴿وَلا تُكْرِهُوا فَتَيَاتِكُمْ عَلَى الْبِغَاءِ﴾ ، إِلَى قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَمَنْ يُكْرِهْهُنَّ فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ مِنْ بَعْدِ إِكْرَاهِهِنَّ غَفُورٌ رَحِيمٌ﴾ .

صَرَّحَ الْأَعْمَشُ بِالسَّمَاعِ مِنْ أَبِي سُفْيَانَ طَلْحَةَ بْنِ نَافِعٍ، فَدَلَّ عَلَى بُطْلَانِ قَوْلِ مَنْ قَالَ: "لَمْ يَسْمَعْ مِنْهُ، إِنَّمَا هُوَ صَحِيفَةٌ" حَكَاهُ الْبَزَّارُ.

قَالَ أَبُو دَاوُدَ الطَّيَالِسِيُّ، عَنْ سُلَيْمَانَ بْنِ مُعَاذٍ، عَنْ سِمَاك، عَنْ عِكْرِمة، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ؛ أَنَّ جَارِيَةً لِعَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ أُبَيٍّ كَانَتْ تَزْنِي فِي الْجَاهِلِيَّةِ، فَوَلَدَتْ أَوْلَادًا مِنَ الزِّنَى، فَقَالَ لَهَا: مَا لَكِ لَا تَزْنِينَ؟ قَالَتْ لَا وَاللَّهِ لَا أَزْنِي. فَضَرَبَهَا، فَأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ: ﴿وَلا تُكْرِهُوا فَتَيَاتِكُمْ عَلَى الْبِغَاءِ إِنْ أَرَدْنَ تَحَصُّنًا﴾ 

وَقَالَ عَبْدُ الرَّزَّاقِ: أَخْبَرَنَا مَعْمَر، عَنِ الزُّهْرِيِّ: أَنَّ رَجُلًا مَنْ قُرَيْشٍ أُسر يَوْمَ بَدْرٍ، وَكَانَ عِنْدَ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ أُبَيّ أَسِيرًا، وَكَانَتْ لِعَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ أُبيّ جَارِيَةٌ يُقَالُ لَهَا: مُعَاذَةُ، وَكَانَ الْقُرَشِيُّ الْأَسِيرُ يُرِيدُهَا عَلَى نَفْسِهَا، وَكَانَتْ مُسْلِمَةً . وَكَانَتْ تَمْتَنِعُ مِنْهُ لِإِسْلَامِهَا، وَكَانَ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنِ أُبَيٍّ يُكْرِهُهَا عَلَى ذَلِكَ وَيَضْرِبُهَا، رَجَاءَ أَنْ تَحْمِلَ لِلْقُرَشِيِّ، فَيَطْلُبَ فِدَاءَ وَلَدِهِ، فَقَالَ تَبَارَكَ وَتَعَالَى: ﴿وَلا تُكْرِهُوا فَتَيَاتِكُمْ عَلَى الْبِغَاءِ إِنْ أَرَدْنَ تَحَصُّنًا﴾ وَقَالَ السُّدِّيُّ: أُنْزَلَتْ هَذِهِ الْآيَةُ الْكَرِيمَةُ فِي عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ أُبَيِّ بْنِ سَلُولٍ رأس الْمُنَافِقِينَ، وَكَانَتْ لَهُ جَارِيَةٌ تُدْعَى مُعَاذَةُ، وَكَانَ إِذَا نَزَلَ بِهِ ضَيْفٌ أَرْسَلَهَا إِلَيْهِ لِيُوَاقِعَهَا، إِرَادَةَ الثَّوَابِ مِنْهُ وَالْكَرَامَةِ لَهُ. فَأَقْبَلَتِ الْجَارِيَةُ إِلَى أَبِي بَكْرٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ فَشَكَتْ إِلَيْهِ ذَلِكَ، فَذَكَرَهُ أَبُو بَكْرٍ لِلنَّبِيِّ ﷺ، فَأَمَرَهُ بِقَبْضِهَا. فَصَاحَ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنِ أُبَيٍّ: مَنْ يَعْذُرني مِنْ مُحَمَّدٍ، يَغْلِبُنَا عَلَى مَمْلُوكَتِنَا؟ فَأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ فِيهِمْ هَذَا.

وَقَالَ مُقَاتِل بْنُ حَيَّان: بَلَغَنَا -وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ -أَنَّ هَذِهِ الْآيَةَ نَزَلَتْ فِي رَجُلَيْنِ كَانَا يُكْرِهَانِ أَمَتَيْنِ لَهُمَا، إِحْدَاهُمَا اسْمُهَا مُسَيْكَة، وَكَانَتْ لِلْأَنْصَارِيِّ، وَكَانَتْ أُمَيْمَةُ أُمُّ مُسَيْكَةَ لِعَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ أُبَيٍّ، وَكَانَتْ مُعَاذَةُ وَأَرْوَى بِتِلْكَ الْمَنْزِلَةِ، فَأَتَتْ مُسَيْكَةُ وَأُمُّهَا النَّبِيَّ ﷺ، فَذَكَرَتَا ذَلِكَ لَهُ، فَأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ فِي ذَلِكَ ﴿وَلا تُكْرِهُوا فَتَيَاتِكُمْ عَلَى الْبِغَاءِ﴾ يَعْنِي: الزِّنَى.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿إِنْ أَرَدْنَ تَحَصُّنًا﴾ هَذَا خَرَجَ مَخْرَجَ الْغَالِبِ، فَلَا مَفْهُومَ لَهُ. وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿لِتَبْتَغُوا عَرَضَ [الْحَيَاةِ] الدُّنْيَا﴾ أَيْ: مِنْ خَرَاجهن وَمُهُورِهِنَّ وَأَوْلَادِهِنَّ. وَقَدْ نَهَى رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ، عَنْ كَسْبِ الحجَّام، وَمَهْرِ البَغيّ وحُلْوان الْكَاهِنِ -وَفِي رِوَايَةٍ: "مَهْرُ الْبَغِيِّ خَبِيثٌ، وَكَسْبُ الحجَّام خَبِيثٌ، وَثَمَنُ الْكَلْبِ خَبِيثٌ" 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَمَنْ يُكْرِهْهُنَّ فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ مِنْ بَعْدِ إِكْرَاهِهِنَّ غَفُورٌ رَحِيمٌ﴾ [أَيْ: لَهُنَّ، كَمَا تَقَدَّمَ فِي الْحَدِيثِ عَنْ جَابِرٍ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: فَإِنْ فَعَلْتُمْ فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ لهن غفور رحيم] وإثمهن على من أكرههن: وَكَذَا قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ، وَعَطَاءٌ الْخُرَاسَانِيُّ، وَالْأَعْمَشُ، وَقَتَادَةُ.

وَقَالَ أَبُو عُبَيْدٍ: حَدَّثَنِي إِسْحَاقُ الْأَزْرَقُ، عَنْ عَوْف، عَنِ الْحَسَنِ فِي هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ: ﴿فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ مِنْ بَعْدِ إِكْرَاهِهِنَّ غَفُورٌ رَحِيمٌ﴾ قَالَ: لَهُنَّ وَاللَّهِ. لَهُنَّ وَاللَّهِ.

وَعَنِ الزُّهْرِيِّ قَالَ: غَفُورٌ لَهُنَّ مَا أُكْرهْن عَلَيْهِ.

وَعَنْ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ قَالَ: غَفُورٌ رَحِيمٌ لِلْمُكْرَهَاتِ.

حَكَاهُنَّ ابْنُ الْمُنْذِرِ فِي تَفْسِيرِهِ بِأَسَانِيدِهِ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو زُرْعَة، حَدَّثَنَا يَحْيَى بْنُ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ، حَدَّثَنِي ابْنُ لَهِيعَة، حَدَّثَنِي عَطَاءٌ، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْر قَالَ: فِي قِرَاءَةِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ مَسْعُودٍ: "فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ مِنْ بَعْدِ إِكْرَاهِهِنَّ لَهُنَّ غَفُورٌ رَّحِيمٌ" وَإِثْمُهُنَّ عَلَى مَنْ أَكْرَهَهُنَّ.

وَفِي الْحَدِيثِ الْمَرْفُوعِ، عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ أنه قَالَ: "رُفِع عَنْ أمَّتي الْخَطَأَ وَالنِّسْيَانَ، وَمَا اسْتُكْرِهُوا عَلَيْهِ". وَلَمَّا فَصَّلَ تَعَالَى هَذِهِ الْأَحْكَامَ وبَيَّنها قَالَ: ﴿وَلَقَدْ أَنزلْنَا إِلَيْكُمْ آيَاتٍ مُبَيِّنَاتٍ﴾ يَعْنِي: الْقُرْآنَ فِيهِ آيَاتٌ وَاضِحَاتٌ مُفَسِّرَاتٌ، ﴿وَمَثَلا مِنَ الَّذِينَ خَلَوْا مِنْ قَبْلِكُمْ﴾ أَيْ: خَبَرًا عَنِ الْأُمَمِ الْمَاضِيَةِ، وَمَا حلَّ بِهِمْ فِي مُخَالَفَتِهِمْ أوامرَ اللَّهِ تَعَالَى ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿فَجَعَلْنَاهُمْ سَلَفًا وَمَثَلا لِلآخِرِينَ﴾ [الزُّخْرُفِ: ٥٦]

﴿وَمَوْعِظَةً﴾ أَيْ: زَاجِرًا عَنِ ارْتِكَابِ الْمَآثِمِ وَالْمَحَارِمِ ﴿لِلْمُتَّقِينَ﴾ أَيْ: لِمَنِ اتَّقَى اللَّهَ وَخَافَهُ.

قَالَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَالِبٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، فِي صِفَةِ الْقُرْآنِ: فِيهِ حَكْمُ مَا بَيْنَكُمْ، وَخَبَرُ مَا قَبْلَكُمْ، وَنَبَأُ مَا بَعْدَكُمْ، وَهُوَ الفَصْل لَيْسَ بالهَزْل، مَنْ تَرَكَهُ مِنْ جَبَّار قَصَمَه اللَّهُ، وَمَنِ ابْتَغَى الْهُدَى مِنْ غَيْرِهِ أَضَلَّهُ اللَّهُ.

---

## 24:35 — verse 35

### Translation

Ali ibn Abi Talha said, from Ibn Abbas: {Allah is the Light of the heavens and the earth} means: the guide of the people of the heavens and the earth.

Ibn Jurayj said: Mujahid and Ibn Abbas said concerning His saying {Allah is the Light of the heavens and the earth}: He manages the affair within them, their stars, their sun, and their moon.

Ibn Jarir said: [chain] Anas ibn Malik said: My God says: My light is My guidance.

Ibn Jarir, may God have mercy on him, preferred this view.

Abu Ja'far al-Razi said, from al-Rabi' ibn Anas, from Abu al-Aliyah, from Ubayy ibn Ka'b, concerning the saying of Allah Most High {Allah is the Light of the heavens and the earth}: He said: This is the believer in whose breast [Allah] has placed faith and the Qur'an. Allah struck for him a parable, saying: {Allah is the Light of the heavens and the earth}, beginning with the light of His own Self, then mentioning the light of the believer, saying: the parable of the light of one who believes in Him. He said: Ubayy ibn Ka'b used to recite it: "the parable of the light of one who believes in Him: he is the believer in whose breast faith and the Qur'an have been placed."

Sa'id ibn Jubayr and Qays ibn Sa'd said likewise, from Ibn Abbas, that he recited it thus: "the light of one who believes in Allah."

Some recited it: "Allah nawwara (illuminated) the heavens and the earth."

And from al-Dahhak: "Allah nawwara the heavens and the earth."

Al-Suddi said concerning His saying {Allah is the Light of the heavens and the earth}: By His light the heavens and the earth were illuminated.

In the hadith narrated by Muhammad ibn Ishaq in the Sirah, from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, that he said in his supplication on the day the people of Ta'if harmed him: "I seek refuge in the light of Your Face, by which the darknesses are illuminated, and by which the affairs of this world and the next are set right, from Your anger descending upon me or Your wrath alighting upon me. Yours is the right to be satisfied until You are pleased, and there is no power nor strength except by You."

In the two Sahihs, from Ibn Abbas: When the Messenger of Allah ﷺ rose at night he would say: "O Allah, to You belongs praise, You are the Sustainer (Qayyim) of the heavens and the earth and all that is in them, and to You belongs praise, You are the Light of the heavens and the earth and all that is in them," the hadith continuing.

From Ibn Mas'ud, may Allah be pleased with him, he said: Your Lord has with Him neither night nor day; the light of the Throne is from the light of His Face.

Concerning His saying {the parable of His light}, there are two views regarding this pronoun.

The first: that it refers back to Allah, Mighty and Majestic, meaning: the parable of His guidance in the heart of the believer, as Ibn Abbas said, {is as a niche}.

The second: that the pronoun refers back to the believer, indicated by the context of the speech, its meaning being: the parable of the light of the believer which is in his heart is as a niche. Thus the heart of the believer, and the guidance upon which he was innately created, together with what he receives of the Qur'an which corresponds to what he was innately created upon, is likened, as He Most High said: {Is he who is upon a clear proof from his Lord, and a witness from Him follows it} [Hud: 17]. So the heart of the believer, in its inner clarity, is likened to a lamp of transparent, jewel-like glass, and what guides him from the Qur'an and the Law is likened to good, pure, radiant, well-balanced oil, in which there is no murkiness and no deviation.

As for His saying: {as a niche}: Ibn Abbas, Mujahid, Muhammad ibn Ka'b, and others said: it is the place for the wick within the lamp. This is the well-known view; that is why He says after it {within it is a lamp}, which is the wick that gives light.

Al-Awfi said, from Ibn Abbas, concerning His saying {Allah is the Light of the heavens and the earth. The parable of His light is as a niche within which is a lamp}: This was because the Jews said to Muhammad ﷺ: How can the light of Allah reach below the heaven? So Allah struck a parable of that for His light, saying: {Allah is the Light of the heavens and the earth. The parable of His light}. The mishkat (niche) is an opening (kuwwah) in a house. He said: it is a parable Allah struck for obedience to Him. So Allah named obedience to Him "light," then He named it various kinds.

Ibn Abi Najih said, from Mujahid: "al-kuwwah" is in the language of Abyssinia. Others added, saying: the mishkat is an opening that has no passage through it. And from Mujahid: the mishkat is the iron fittings from which the lamp is hung.

The first view is preferable, namely that the mishkat is the place for the wick within the lamp; that is why He says {within it is a lamp}, which is the light that is in the wick.

Ubayy ibn Ka'b said: the lamp is the light, and it is the Qur'an and faith that are in his breast.

Al-Suddi said: it is the lamp flame (siraj).

{The lamp is within a glass}, meaning: this radiance shines within a clear glass.

Ubayy ibn Ka'b and others said: it is the counterpart of the believer's heart. {The glass is as though it were a pearl-like star}: some recited with dammah on the dal without a hamzah, from al-durr (pearl), meaning: as though it were a star made of pearl.

Others recited it "dirri'" and "durri'" with kasrah and dammah on the dal along with a hamzah, from al-dar' meaning repelling; this is because a star, when it is cast down (as a shooting star), is more intensely luminous than in its other states, and the Arabs call unrecognized stars "darari."

Ubayy ibn Ka'b said: a shining star. Qatadah said: shining, clear, and large. {It is lit from a blessed tree}, meaning: it draws from the oil of the olive of a blessed tree, {an olive tree}, in apposition or as an explanatory clause, {neither of the east nor of the west}, meaning: it is not situated in the eastern part of its location such that the sun would not reach it at the beginning of the day, nor in its western part such that the shade would withdraw from it before sunset; rather it is in a middle location, over which the sun spreads from the start of the day to its end, so that its oil comes out balanced, pure, and radiant.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] Ibn Abbas said, concerning His saying {an olive tree, neither of the east nor of the west}: a tree in open desert land, shaded by no mountain, tree, or cave, and nothing conceals it; and that makes its oil better.

Yahya ibn Sa'id al-Qattan said, from Imran ibn Hudayr, from Ikrimah, concerning His saying {neither of the east nor of the west}: it is in open desert land, and that gives it purer beauty (or oil).

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] a man asked Ikrimah about {an olive tree, neither of the east nor of the west}; he said: that is an olive tree in open flat land; when the sun rises it shines upon it, and when it sets it shines upon it too; so that is the purest oil there can be.

Mujahid said concerning His saying {an olive tree, neither of the east nor of the west}: it is not eastern such that the sun would not reach it when it sets, nor western such that the sun would not reach it when it rises; rather it is both eastern and western, the sun reaching it both when it rises and when it sets.

Sa'id ibn Jubayr said concerning His saying {an olive tree, neither of the east nor of the west, whose oil would almost glow}: it is the best of oil. He said: when the sun rises, it strikes it from the direction of the east, and when it begins to set, the sun strikes it too; so the sun strikes it morning and evening; thus it is counted as neither eastern nor western.

Al-Suddi said concerning His saying {an olive tree, neither of the east nor of the west}: it means: it is not eastern, monopolized by the east, nor western, monopolized by the west to the exclusion of the east; rather it is on top of a mountain, or in open desert land, and the sun strikes it the whole day.

It was also said that what is meant by His saying {an olive tree, neither of the east nor of the west} is that it is in the middle of the trees, not exposed to the east or to the west.

Abu Ja'far al-Razi said, from al-Rabi' ibn Anas, from Abu al-Aliyah, from Ubayy ibn Ka'b, concerning the saying of Allah Most High {an olive tree, neither of the east nor of the west}: he said: it is green and tender, the sun does not touch it in any of its states, neither when it rises nor when it sets. He said: likewise is this believer; he has been shielded from being afflicted by any of the trials, yet he is tested by them, and Allah makes him firm within them. So he is characterized by four qualities: if he speaks, he speaks truthfully; if he judges, he judges justly; if he is tested, he is patient; and if he is given something, he is grateful. He is, among the rest of the people, like a living man walking among the graves of the dead.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] Sa'id ibn Jubayr said concerning His saying {an olive tree, neither of the east nor of the west}: it is in the middle of the trees, the sun not reaching it from the east or from the west.

Atiyyah al-Awfi said: {neither of the east nor of the west}

He said: it is a tree in a location among the trees where the shade of its fruit can be seen in its leaves, and this is among the trees upon which the sun neither rises nor sets.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: Muhammad ibn Ammar told us, Abd al-Rahman al-Dashtaki told us, Amr ibn Abi Qays told us, from Ata, from Sa'id ibn Jubayr, from Ibn Abbas, may Allah be pleased with both of them, concerning His saying {neither of the east nor of the west}: it is not of the east such that it has no west, nor of the west such that it has no east, rather it is both of the east and of the west.

Muhammad ibn Ka'b al-Qurazi said, concerning {neither of the east nor of the west}: it is the one facing the qiblah.

Zayd ibn Aslam said, concerning {neither of the east nor of the west}: it is the Levant (al-Sham).

Al-Hasan al-Basri said: if this tree were on the earth it would be either eastern or western, but it is a parable which Allah has set forth for His light.

Al-Dahhak reported from Ibn Abbas concerning {kindled from a blessed tree}: he said, a righteous man; and concerning {an olive, neither of the east nor of the west}: he said, neither a Jew nor a Christian.

The most fitting of these sayings is the first one, namely that it is on level ground, in a spacious, open, exposed, sun-lit place, where the sun's rays reach it from the beginning of the day to its end, so that this makes its beauty purer and more delicate, as more than one of those mentioned before have said. This is why He said: {its oil would almost glow forth even if no fire touched it}. Abd al-Rahman ibn Zayd ibn Aslam said: meaning, from the glow of the oil's radiance.

Concerning His saying {light upon light}: al-Awfi reported from Ibn Abbas that this means the servant's faith and his deeds.

Mujahid and al-Suddi said: it means the light of the fire and the light of the oil.

Ubayy ibn Ka'b said, concerning {light upon light}: he moves about within five lights: his speech is light, his deed is light, his entering is light, his going out is light, and his final return on the Day of Resurrection is to light, to Paradise.

Shimr ibn Atiyyah said: Ibn Abbas came to Ka'b al-Ahbar and said, tell me about Allah's saying {its oil would almost glow forth even if no fire touched it}.

He said: Muhammad almost makes clear to people, even without speaking, that he is a prophet, just as that oil almost glows.

Al-Suddi said concerning {light upon light}: he said, the light of the fire and the light of the oil; when the two combine they give light, and neither one gives light without the other. [Likewise the light of the Qur'an and the light of faith: when the two combine, neither of them exists except together with the other.]

Concerning His saying {Allah guides to His light whom He wills}, that is: Allah directs to His guidance whomever He chooses, as has come in the hadith reported by Imam Ahmad:

[chain] Mu'awiyah ibn Amr told us, Ibrahim ibn Muhammad al-Fazari told us, al-Awza'i told us, Rabi'ah ibn Yazid told me, from Abdullah ibn al-Daylami, from Abdullah ibn Amr, who said: I heard the Messenger of Allah ﷺ say: "Indeed Allah created His creation in darkness, then He cast upon them from His light on that day. Whoever was struck that day by His light was guided, and whoever missed it went astray. That is why I say: the pen has dried according to Allah's, the Mighty and Majestic's, knowledge."

Another route for this: al-Bazzar said: [chain] Ayyub ibn Suwayd, from Yahya ibn Abi Amr al-Shaybani, from his father, from Abdullah ibn Umar, who said: I heard the Messenger of Allah ﷺ say: "Indeed Allah created His creation in darkness, then He cast upon them a light from His light. Whoever was struck by that light was guided, and whoever missed it went astray." [Al-Bazzar also narrated it from Abdullah ibn Amr through another route, with its wording and letters.]

Concerning His saying {And Allah sets forth parables for people, and Allah is knowing of all things}: after mentioning this parable of the light of His guidance in the heart of the believer, He concluded the verse by saying {And Allah sets forth parables for people, and Allah is knowing of all things}, that is: He knows best who deserves guidance and who deserves to be led astray.

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Abu al-Nadr told us, Abu Mu'awiyah, that is Shayban, told us, from Layth, from Amr ibn Murrah, from Abu al-Bakhtari, from Abu Sa'id al-Khudri, who said: the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Hearts are of four kinds: a bare heart within which there is something like a lamp that glows; a covered heart bound over by its covering; an inverted heart; and a heart with layers. As for the bare heart, it is the heart of the believer, its lamp is within it giving its light. As for the covered heart, it is the heart of the disbeliever. As for the inverted heart, it is the heart of the hypocrite, he knew then denied. As for the heart with layers, it is a heart in which there is both faith and hypocrisy, and the likeness of faith within it is like a plant nourished by wholesome water, while the likeness of hypocrisy within it is like a sore nourished by pus and blood, and whichever of the two nourishments prevails over the other will dominate it." Its chain of transmission is good, and they did not include it [in the two Sahihs].

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

قَالَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عباس: ﴿اللَّهُ نُورُ السَّموَاتِ وَالأرْضِ﴾ يقول: هادي أهل السموات وَالْأَرْضِ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جُرَيْج: قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ وَابْنُ عباس في قوله: ﴿اللَّهُ نُورُ السَّمَوَاتِ وَالأرْضِ﴾ يُدْبِّرُ الْأَمْرَ فِيهِمَا، نُجُومِهِمَا وَشَمْسِهِمَا وَقَمَرِهِمَا.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنَا سُلَيْمَانُ بْنُ عُمَرَ بْنُ خَالِدٍ الرَقِّي، حَدَّثَنَا وَهْبُ بْنُ رَاشِدٍ، عَنْ فَرْقَد، عَنْ أَنَسِ بْنِ مَالِكٍ قَالَ: إِنَّ إِلَهِي يَقُولُ: نُورِي هُدَايَ.

وَاخْتَارَ هَذَا الْقَوْلَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ.

وَقَالَ أَبُو جَعْفَرٍ الرَّازِيُّ، عَنِ الرَّبِيعِ بْنِ أَنَسٍ، عَنْ أَبِي الْعَالِيَةِ، عَنْ أُبيّ بْنِ كَعْبٍ في قول الله تعالى: ﴿اللَّهُ نُورُ السَّمَوَاتِ وَالأرْضِ﴾ قَالَ: هُوَ الْمُؤْمِنُ الَّذِي جَعَلَ [اللَّهُ] الْإِيمَانَ وَالْقُرْآنَ فِي صَدْرِهِ، فَضَرَبَ اللَّهُ مَثَلَهُ فقال: ﴿اللَّهُ نُورُ السَّمَوَاتِ وَالأرْضِ﴾ فَبَدَأَ بِنُورِ نَفْسِهِ، ثُمَّ ذَكَرَ نُورَ الْمُؤْمِنُ فَقَالَ: مَثَلُ نُورِ مَنْ آمَنَ بِهِ. قَالَ: فَكَانَ أُبي بْنُ كَعْبٍ يَقْرَؤُهَا: "مَثَلُ نُورِ مَنْ آمَنَ بِهِ فَهُوَ الْمُؤْمِنُ جُعِلَ الْإِيمَانُ وَالْقُرْآنُ فِي صَدْرِهِ.

وَهَكَذَا قَالَ سَعِيدُ بْنُ جُبير، وَقَيْسُ بْنُ سَعْدٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ أَنَّهُ قَرَأَهَا كَذَلِكَ: "نُورِ مَنْ آمَنَ بالله".

وقرأ بعضهم:"اللَّهُ نَوَّر السَّمَوَاتِ وَالأرْضِ" ".

وعن الضحاك: "اللَّهُ نَوَّر السَّمَوَاتِ وَالأرْضِ ".

وقال السدي في قوله: ﴿اللَّهُ نُورُ السَّمَوَاتِ وَالأرْضِ﴾ : فبنوره أضاءت السموات وَالْأَرْضُ.

وَفِي الْحَدِيثِ الَّذِي رَوَاهُ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ فِي السِّيرَةِ، عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ أَنَّهُ قَالَ فِي دُعَائِهِ يَوْمَ آذَاهُ أَهْلُ الطَّائِفِ: "أُعُوذُ بِنُورِ وَجْهِكَ الَّذِي أَشْرَقَتْ لَهُ الظُّلُمَاتُ، وَصَلُحَ عَلَيْهِ أَمْرُ الدُّنْيَا وَالْآخِرَةِ، أَنْ يَحِلَّ بِيَ غَضبك أَوْ يَنْزِلَ بِي سَخَطُك، لَكَ الْعُتْبَى حَتَّى تَرْضَى، وَلَا حَوْلَ وَلَا قُوَّةَ إِلَّا بِكَ " .

وَفِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: كَانَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ صَلَّى اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ سَلَّمَ إِذَا قَامَ مِنَ اللَّيْلِ يَقُولُ: "اللَّهُمَّ لَكَ الْحَمْدُ، أَنْتَ قَيّم السموات وَالْأَرْضِ وَمِنْ فِيهِنَّ، وَلَكَ الْحَمْدُ، أَنْتَ نُورُ السموات وَالْأَرْضِ وَمِنْ فِيهِنَّ" الْحَدِيثَ .

وَعَنِ ابْنِ مَسْعُودٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: إِنَّ رَبَّكُمْ لَيْسَ عِنْدَهُ لَيْلٌ وَلَا نَهَارٌ، نُورُ الْعَرْشِ مِنْ نُورِ وَجْهِهِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿مَثَلُ نُورِهِ﴾ فِي هَذَا الضَّمِيرِ قَوْلَانِ:

أَحَدُهُمَا: أَنَّهُ عَائِدٌ إِلَى اللَّهِ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، أَيْ: مَثَلُ هُدَاهُ فِي قَلْبِ الْمُؤْمِنِ، قَالَهُ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ ﴿كَمِشْكَاةٍ﴾ .

وَالثَّانِي: أَنَّ الضَّمِيرَ عَائِدٌ إِلَى الْمُؤْمِنِ الَّذِي دَلَّ عَلَيْهِ سِيَاقُ الْكَلَامِ: تَقْدِيرُهُ: مَثَلُ نُورِ الْمُؤْمِنِ الَّذِي فِي قَلْبِهِ، كَمِشْكَاةٍ. فَشَبَّهَ قَلْبَ الْمُؤْمِنِ وَمَا هُوَ مَفْطُورٌ عَلَيْهِ مِنَ الْهُدَى، وَمَا يَتَلَقَّاهُ مِنَ الْقُرْآنِ الْمُطَابِقِ لِمَا هُوَ مَفْطُورٌ عَلَيْهِ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿أَفَمَنْ كَانَ عَلَى بَيِّنَةٍ مِنْ رَبِّهِ وَيَتْلُوهُ شَاهِدٌ مِنْهُ﴾ [هُودٍ: ١٧] ، فَشَبَّهَ قَلْبَ الْمُؤْمِنِ فِي صَفَائِهِ فِي نَفْسِهِ بِالْقِنْدِيلِ مِنَ الزُّجَاجِ الشَّفَّافِ الْجَوْهَرِيِّ، وَمَا يَسْتَهْدِيهِ مِنَ الْقُرْآنِ وَالشَّرْعِ بِالزَّيْتِ الْجَيِّدِ الصَّافِي الْمُشْرِقِ الْمُعْتَدِلِ، الَّذِي لَا كَدَرَ فِيهِ وَلَا انْحِرَافَ.

فَقَوْلُهُ : ﴿كَمِشْكَاةٍ﴾ : قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ، وَمُجَاهِدٌ، وَمُحَمَّدُ بْنُ كَعْبٍ، وَغَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ: هُوَ مَوْضِعُ الْفَتِيلَةِ مِنَ الْقِنْدِيلِ. هَذَا هُوَ الْمَشْهُورُ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ بَعْدَهُ: ﴿فِيهَا مِصْبَاحٌ﴾ ، وَهُوَ الذُّبالة الَّتِي تُضِيءُ.

وَقَالَ الْعَوْفِيُّ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ [فِي] قَوْلِهِ: ﴿اللَّهُ نُورُ السَّمَوَاتِ وَالأرْضِ مَثَلُ نُورِهِ كَمِشْكَاةٍ فِيهَا مِصْبَاحٌ﴾ : وَذَلِكَ أَنَّ الْيَهُودَ قَالُوا لِمُحَمَّدٍ ﷺ: كَيْفَ يَخْلُصُ نُورُ اللَّهِ مَنْ دُونِ السَّمَاءِ؟ فَضَرَبَ اللَّهُ مَثَلَ ذَلِكَ لِنُورِهِ، فَقَالَ: ﴿اللَّهُ نُورُ السَّمَوَاتِ وَالأرْضِ مَثَلُ نُورِهِ﴾ . وَالْمِشْكَاةُ: كوَّة فِي الْبَيْتِ -قَالَ: وَهُوَ مَثَلٌ ضَرَبه اللَّهُ لِطَاعَتِهِ . فسمَّى اللَّهُ طاعَتَه نُورًا، ثُمَّ سَمَاها أَنْوَاعًا شَتَّى.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي نَجِيح، عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ: الْكُوَّةُ بلُغة الْحَبَشَةِ. وَزَادَ غَيْرُهُ فَقَالَ: الْمِشْكَاةُ: الْكُوَّةُ الَّتِي لَا مَنْفَذَ لَهَا. وَعَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ: الْمِشْكَاةُ: الْحَدَائِدُ الَّتِي يُعَلَّقُ بِهَا الْقِنْدِيلُ.

وَالْقَوْلُ الْأَوَّلُ أَوْلَى، وَهُوَ: أَنَّ الْمِشْكَاةَ هِيَ مَوْضِعُ الفَتيلة مِنَ الْقِنْدِيلِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿فِيهَا مِصْبَاحٌ﴾ وَهُوَ النور الذي في الذُّبالة.

قَالَ أُبَيُّ بْنُ كَعْبٍ: الْمِصْبَاحُ: النُّورُ، وَهُوَ الْقُرْآنُ وَالْإِيمَانُ الَّذِي فِي صَدْرِهِ.

وَقَالَ السُّدِّي: هُوَ السِّرَاجُ.

﴿الْمِصْبَاحُ فِي زُجَاجَةٍ﴾ أَيْ: هَذَا الضَّوْءُ مُشْرِقٌ فِي زُجَاجَةٍ صَافِيَةٍ.

قَالَ أُبَيُّ بْنُ كَعْبٍ وَغَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ: وَهِيَ نَظِيرُ قَلْبِ الْمُؤْمِنِ. ﴿الزُّجَاجَةُ كَأَنَّهَا كَوْكَبٌ دُرِّيٌّ﴾ : قَرَأَ بَعْضُهُمْ بِضَمِّ الدَّالِ مِنْ غَيْرِ هَمْزَةٍ، مِنَ الدُّرِّ، أَيْ: كَأَنَّهَا كَوْكَبٌ مِنْ دُرّ.

وَقَرَأَ آخَرُونَ: "دِرّيء" وَ"دُرِّيء" بِكَسْرِ الدَّالِ وَضَمِّهَا مَعَ الْهَمْزِ، مِنَ الدَرْء وَهُوَ الدَّفْعُ؛ وَذَلِكَ أَنَّ النَّجْمَ إِذَا رُمي بِهِ يَكُونُ أَشَدُّ اسْتِنَارَةً مِنْ سَائِرِ الْأَحْوَالِ، وَالْعَرَبُ تُسَمِّي مَا لَا يُعْرَفُ مِنَ الْكَوَاكِبِ دَرَارِيَّ.

قَالَ أُبَيُّ بْنُ كَعْبٍ: كَوْكَبٌ مُضِيءٌ. وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: مُضِيءٌ مُبِينٌ ضَخْمٌ. ﴿يُوقَدُ مِنْ شَجَرَةٍ مُبَارَكَةٍ﴾ أَيْ: يَسْتَمِدُّ مِنْ زَيْتِ زَيْتُونِ شَجَرَةٍ مُبَارَكَةٍ ﴿زَيْتُونَةٍ﴾ بَدَلٌ أَوْ عَطْفُ بَيَانٍ ﴿لَا شَرْقِيَّةٍ وَلا غَرْبِيَّةٍ﴾ أَيْ: لَيْسَتْ فِي شَرْقِيِّ بُقْعَتِهَا فَلَا تَصِلُ إِلَيْهَا الشَّمْسُ مِنْ أَوَّلِ النَّهَارِ، وَلَا فِي غَرْبِيِّهَا فَيَتَقَلَّصُ عَنْهَا الْفَيْءُ قَبْلَ الْغُرُوبِ، بَلْ هِيَ فِي مَكَانٍ وَسَطٍ، تَفْرَعه الشَّمْسُ مِنْ أَوَّلِ النَّهَارِ إِلَى آخِرِهِ، فَيَجِيءُ زَيْتُهَا مُعْتَدِلًا صَافِيًا مُشْرِقًا.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ عَمَّارٍ قَالَ: حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ سَعْدٍ، أَخْبَرَنَا عَمْرُو بْنُ أَبِي قَيْسٍ، عَنْ سِمَاك بْنِ حَرْبٍ، عَنْ عِكْرِمة، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿زَيْتُونَةٍ لَا شَرْقِيَّةٍ وَلا غَرْبِيَّةٍ﴾ قَالَ: شَجَرَةٌ بِالصَّحْرَاءِ، لَا يُظِلُّهَا جَبَلٌ وَلَا شَجَرٌ وَلَا كَهْفٌ، وَلَا يُوَارِيهَا شَيْءٌ، وَهُوَ أَجْوَدُ لِزَيْتِهَا.

وَقَالَ يَحْيَى بْنُ سَعِيدٍ القَطَّان، عَنْ عِمْرَانَ بْنِ حُدَيْر، عَنْ عِكْرِمَةَ، فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿لَا شَرْقِيَّةٍ وَلا غَرْبِيَّةٍ﴾ قَالَ: هِيَ بِصَحْرَاءَ، وَذَلِكَ أَصْفَى لِزِينَتِهَا.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو نُعَيْم، حَدَّثَنَا عُمَر بْنُ فَرُّوخ، عَنْ حَبِيبِ بْنِ الزُّبَيْرِ، عَنْ عِكْرِمَةَ -وَسَأَلَهُ رَجُلٌ عَنْ: ﴿زَيْتُونَةٍ لَا شَرْقِيَّةٍ وَلا غَرْبِيَّةٍ﴾ قَالَ تِلْكَ [زَيْتُونَةٌ] بِأَرْضِ فَلَاةٍ، إِذَا أَشْرَقَتِ الشَّمْسُ أَشْرَقَتْ عَلَيْهَا، وَإِذَا غَرُبَتْ غَرُبَتْ عَلَيْهَا فَذَاكَ أَصْفَى مَا يَكُونُ مِنَ الزَّيْتِ.

وَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿ [زَيْتُونَةٍ] لَا شَرْقِيَّةٍ وَلا غَرْبِيَّةٍ﴾ قَالَ: لَيْسَتْ بِشَرْقِيَّةٍ، لَا تُصِيبُهَا الشَّمْسُ إِذَا غَرُبَتْ، وَلَا غَرْبِيَّةٍ لَا تُصِيبُهَا الشَّمْسُ إِذَا طَلَعَتْ، [وَلَكِنَّهَا شَرْقِيَّةٌ وَغَرْبِيَّةٌ، تُصِيبُهَا إِذَا طَلَعَتْ] وَإِذَا غَرُبَتْ.

وَقَالَ سَعِيدُ بْنُ جُبَيْر فِي قَوْلِهِ ﴿زَيْتُونَةٍ لَا شَرْقِيَّةٍ وَلا غَرْبِيَّةٍ يَكَادُ زَيْتُهَا يُضِيءُ﴾ قَالَ: هُوَ أَجْوَدُ الزَّيْتِ. قَالَ: إِذَا طَلَعَتِ الشَّمْسُ أَصَابَتْهَا مِنْ صَوْبِ الْمَشْرِقِ، فَإِذَا أَخَذَتْ فِي الْغُرُوبِ أَصَابَتْهَا الشَّمْسُ، فَالشَّمْسُ تُصِيبُهَا بِالْغَدَاةِ والعَشِيّ، فَتِلْكَ لَا تُعَدُّ شَرْقِيَّةً وَلَا غَرْبِيَّةً.

وَقَالَ السُّدِّيُّ [فِي] قَوْلِهِ: ﴿زَيْتُونَةٍ لَا شَرْقِيَّةٍ وَلا غَرْبِيَّةٍ﴾ يَقُولُ: ليست بشرقية يحوزها الْمَشْرِقُ، وَلَا غَرْبِيَّةٍ يَحُوزُهَا الْمَغْرِبُ دُونَ الْمَشْرِقِ، وَلَكِنَّهَا عَلَى رَأْسِ جَبَلٍ، أَوْ فِي صَحْرَاءَ، تُصِيبُهَا الشَّمْسُ النهارَ كلَّه.

وَقِيلَ: الْمُرَادُ بِقَوْلِهِ: ﴿زَيْتُونَةٍ لَا شَرْقِيَّةٍ وَلا غَرْبِيَّةٍ﴾ أَنَّهَا فِي وَسَطِ الشَّجَرِ، وَلَيْسَتْ بَادِيَةً لِلْمَشْرِقِ وَلَا لِلْمَغْرِبِ.

وَقَالَ أَبُو جَعْفَرٍ الرَّازِيُّ، عَنِ الرَّبِيعِ بْنِ أَنَسٍ، عَنْ أَبِي الْعَالِيَةِ، عَنْ أُبي بْنِ كَعْبٍ، فِي قَوْلِ اللَّهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿زَيْتُونَةٍ لَا شَرْقِيَّةٍ وَلا غَرْبِيَّةٍ﴾ قَالَ: فَهِيَ خَضْرَاءُ نَاعِمَةٌ، لَا تُصِيبُهَا الشَّمْسُ عَلَى أَيِّ حَالٍ كَانَتْ، لَا إِذَا طَلَعَتْ وَلَا إِذَا غَرُبَتْ. قَالَ: فَكَذَلِكَ هَذَا الْمُؤْمِنُ، قَدْ أُجِيرَ مِنْ أَنْ يُصِيبَهُ شَيْءٌ مِنَ الْفِتَنِ، وَقَدِ ابْتُلِيَ بِهَا فَيُثَبِّتُهُ اللَّهُ فِيهَا، فَهُوَ بَيْنَ أَرْبَعِ خِلَالٍ: إِنْ قَالَ صَدَق، وَإِنْ حَكَمَ عَدَلَ، وَإِنِ ابْتُلِيَ صَبَرَ، وَإِنْ أُعْطِيَ شَكَرَ، فَهُوَ فِي سَائِرِ النَّاسِ كَالرَّجُلِ الْحَيِّ يَمْشِي فِي قُبُورِ الْأَمْوَاتِ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا عَلِيُّ بْنُ الْحُسَيْنِ، حَدَّثَنَا مُسَدَّد قَالَ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو عَوَانة، عَنْ أَبِي بِشْرٍ، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْرٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿زَيْتُونَةٍ لَا شَرْقِيَّةٍ وَلا غَرْبِيَّةٍ﴾ قَالَ: هِيَ وَسَطَ الشَّجَرِ، لَا تُصِيبُهَا الشَّمْسُ شَرْقًا وَلَا غَرْبًا.

وَقَالَ عَطِيَّةُ الْعَوْفِيُّ: ﴿لَا شَرْقِيَّةٍ وَلا غَرْبِيَّةٍ﴾ قَالَ: هِيَ شَجَرَةٌ فِي مَوْضِعٍ مِنَ الشَّجَرِ، يُرَى ظِلُّ ثَمَرِهَا فِي وَرَقِهَا، وَهَذِهِ مِنَ الشَّجَرِ لَا تَطْلُعُ عَلَيْهَا الشَّمْسُ وَلَا تَغْرُبُ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ عَمَّارٍ، حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ الدَّشْتَكِي، حَدَّثَنَا عَمْرُو بْنُ أَبِي قَيْسٍ، عَنْ عَطَاءٍ، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْرٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمَا، فِي قَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿لَا شَرْقِيَّةٍ وَلا غَرْبِيَّةٍ﴾ لَيْسَتْ شَرْقِيَّةً لَيْسَ فِيهَا غَرْبٌ، وَلَا غَرْبِيَّةً لَيْسَ فِيهَا شَرْقٌ، وَلَكِنَّهَا شَرْقِيَّةٌ غَرْبِيَّةٌ.

وَقَالَ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ كَعْبٍ القُرَظي: ﴿لَا شَرْقِيَّةٍ وَلا غَرْبِيَّةٍ﴾ قَالَ: هِيَ القبْلية.

وَقَالَ زَيْدُ بْنُ أَسْلَمَ: ﴿لَا شَرْقِيَّةٍ وَلا غَرْبِيَّةٍ﴾ قَالَ: الشَّامُ.

وَقَالَ الْحَسَنُ الْبَصْرِيُّ: لَوْ كَانَتْ هَذِهِ الشَّجَرَةُ فِي الْأَرْضِ لَكَانَتْ شَرْقِيَّةً أَوْ غَرْبِيَّةً، وَلَكِنَّهُ مَثَلٌ ضَرَبَهُ اللَّهُ لِنُورِهِ.

وَقَالَ الضَّحَّاكُ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: ﴿توقَدُ مِنْ شَجَرَةٍ مُبَارَكَةٍ﴾ قَالَ: رَجُلٌ صَالِحٌ ﴿زَيْتُونَةٍ لَا شَرْقِيَّةٍ وَلا غَرْبِيَّةٍ﴾ قَالَ: لَا يَهُودِيٍّ وَلَا نَصْرَانِيٍّ.

وَأَوْلَى هَذِهِ الْأَقْوَالِ القولُ الْأَوَّلُ، وَهُوَ أَنَّهَا فِي مُسْتَوًى مِنَ الْأَرْضِ، فِي مَكَانٍ فَسِيحٍ بَارِزٍ ظَاهِرٍ ضَاحٍ لِلشَّمْسِ، تَفْرعه مِنْ أَوَّلِ النَّهَارِ إِلَى آخِرِهِ، لِيَكُونَ ذَلِكَ أَصْفَى لِزِينَتِهَا وَأَلْطَفُ، كَمَا قَالَ غَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ مِمَّنْ تَقَدَّمَ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿يَكَادُ زَيْتُهَا يُضِيءُ وَلَوْ لَمْ تَمْسَسْهُ نَارٌ﴾ قَالَ عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ: يَعْنِي: لِضَوْءِ إِشْرَاقِ الزَّيْتِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿نُورٌ عَلَى نُورٍ﴾ قَالَ الْعَوْفِيُّ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: يَعْنِي بِذَلِكَ إِيمَانَ الْعَبْدِ وَعَمَلَهُ.

وَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ، وَالسُّدِّيُّ: يَعْنِي نُورَ النَّارِ وَنُورَ الزَّيْتِ.

وَقَالَ أُبَيُّ بْنُ كَعْبٍ: ﴿نُورٌ عَلَى نُورٍ﴾ فَهُوَ يَتَقَلَّبُ فِي خَمْسَةٍ مِنَ النُّورِ، فَكَلَامُهُ نُورٌ، وَعَمَلُهُ نُورٌ، وَمَدْخَلُهُ نُورٌ، وَمَخْرَجُهُ نُورٌ، وَمَصِيرُهُ إِلَى النُّورِ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ إِلَى الْجَنَّةِ.

وَقَالَ شِمْر بْنُ عَطية: جَاءَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ إِلَى كَعْبِ الْأَحْبَارِ فَقَالَ: حَدِّثْنِي عَنْ قَوْلِ اللَّهِ: ﴿يَكَادُ زَيْتُهَا يُضِيءُ وَلَوْ لَمْ تَمْسَسْهُ نَارٌ﴾

قَالَ: يَكَادُ مُحَمَّدٌ يُبَيِّنُ لِلنَّاسِ، وَإِنْ لَمْ يَتَكَلَّمْ، أَنَّهُ نَبِيٌّ، كَمَا يَكَادُ ذَلِكَ الزَّيْتُ أَنْ يُضِيءَ.

وَقَالَ السُّدِّي فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿نُورٌ عَلَى نُورٍ﴾ قَالَ: نُورُ النَّارِ وَنُورُ الزَّيْتِ، حِينَ اجْتَمَعَا أَضَاءَا، وَلَا يُضِيءُ وَاحِدٌ بِغَيْرِ صَاحِبِهِ [كَذَلِكَ نُورُ الْقُرْآنِ وَنُورُ الْإِيمَانِ حِينَ اجْتَمَعَا، فَلَا يَكُونُ وَاحِدٌ مِنْهُمَا إِلَّا بِصَاحِبِهِ] 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿يَهْدِي اللَّهُ لِنُورِهِ مَنْ يَشَاءُ﴾ أَيْ: يُرْشِدُ اللَّهُ إِلَى هِدَايَتِهِ مَنْ يَخْتَارُهُ، كَمَا جَاءَ فِي الْحَدِيثِ الَّذِي رَوَاهُ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ:

حَدَّثَنَا مُعَاوِيَةُ بْنُ عَمْرٍو، حَدَّثَنَا إِبْرَاهِيمُ بْنُ مُحَمَّدٍ الْفَزَارِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا الْأَوْزَاعِيُّ، حَدَّثَنِي رَبِيعَةُ بْنُ يَزِيدَ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ [بْنِ] الدَّيْلَمِيِّ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عَمْرٍو، سَمِعْتُ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَقُولُ: "إِنَّ اللَّهَ خَلَقَ خَلْقَهُ فِي ظُلْمَةٍ، ثُمَّ أَلْقَى عَلَيْهِمْ مِنْ نُورِهِ يَوْمَئِذٍ، فَمَنْ أَصَابَ يَوْمَئِذٍ مِنْ نُورِهِ اهْتَدَى، وَمَنْ أَخْطَأَهُ ضَلَّ. فَلِذَلِكَ أَقُولُ: جفَّ الْقَلَمُ عَلَى عِلْمِ اللَّهِ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ" 

طَرِيقٌ أُخْرَى عَنْهُ: قَالَ الْبَزَّارُ: حَدَّثَنَا أَيُّوبُ بْنُ سُوَيْد، عَنْ يَحْيَى بْنِ أَبِي عَمْرٍو الشَّيباني، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنْ عَبْدَ اللَّهِ بْنَ عُمَرَ: سَمِعْتُ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَقُولُ: "إِنَّ اللَّهَ خَلَقَ خَلْقَهُ فِي ظُلْمَةٍ، فَأَلْقَى عَلَيْهِمْ نُورًا مِنْ نُورِهِ، فَمَنْ أَصَابَهُ مِنْ ذَلِكَ النُّورِ اهْتَدَى، وَمَنْ أَخْطَأَهُ ضَلَّ. [وَرَوَاهُ الْبَزَّارُ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عَمْرٍو مِنْ طَرِيقٍ آخَرَ، بِلَفْظِهِ وَحُرُوفِهِ] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَيَضْرِبُ اللَّهُ الأمْثَالَ لِلنَّاسِ وَاللَّهُ بِكُلِّ شَيْءٍ عَلِيمٌ﴾ لَمَّا ذَكَرَ تَعَالَى هَذَا مَثَلًا لِنُورِ هُدَاهُ فِي قَلْبِ الْمُؤْمِنِ، خَتَمَ الْآيَةَ بِقَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَيَضْرِبُ اللَّهُ الأمْثَالَ لِلنَّاسِ وَاللَّهُ بِكُلِّ شَيْءٍ عَلِيمٌ﴾ أَيْ: هُوَ أَعْلَمُ بِمَنْ يَسْتَحِقُّ الْهِدَايَةَ مِمَّنْ يَسْتَحِقُّ الْإِضْلَالَ.

قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو النَّضْرِ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو مُعَاوِيَةَ -يَعْنِي شَيْبَانَ -، عَنْ لَيْثٍ، عَنْ عَمْرِو بْنِ مُرَّة، عَنْ أَبِي البَخْتَري، عَنْ أَبِي سَعِيدٍ الْخُدْرِيِّ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "الْقُلُوبُ أَرْبَعَةٌ: قَلْبٌ أَجْرَدُ فِيهِ مِثْلُ السِّرَاجِ يُزهرُ، وَقَلْبٌ أَغْلَفُ مَرْبُوطٌ عَلَى غِلَافِهِ، وَقَلْبٌ مَنْكُوسٌ، وَقَلْبٌ مُصْفَح: فَأَمَّا الْقَلْبُ الْأَجْرَدُ فَقَلْبُ الْمُؤْمِنِ، سِرَاجُهُ فِيهِ نُورُهُ. وَأَمَّا الْقَلْبُ الْأَغْلَفُ فَقَلْبُ الْكَافِرِ. وَأَمَّا الْقَلْبُ الْمَنْكُوسُ فَقَلْبُ [الْمُنَافِقِ] عَرَفَ ثُمَّ أَنْكَرَ. وَأَمَّا الْقَلْبُ المُصْفَح فَقَلْبٌ فِيهِ إِيمَانٌ وَنِفَاقٌ، وَمَثَلُ الْإِيمَانِ فِيهِ كَمَثَلِ الْبَقْلَةِ يَمُدّها الْمَاءُ الطَّيِّبُ، وَمَثَلُ النِّفَاقِ فِيهِ كَمَثَلِ القُرحة يَمُدَّها الْقَيْحُ وَالدَّمُ، فَأَيُّ الْمَدَّتَيْنِ غَلَبَتْ عَلَى الْأُخْرَى غَلَبَتْ عَلَيْهِ". إِسْنَادُهُ جيد ولم يخرجوه.

---

## 24:36-38 — verses 36-38 (shared commentary)

### Translation

When Allah the Exalted set forth [the parable] of the believer's heart, and what is within it of guidance and knowledge, by the likeness of the lamp within the clear glass, kindled from blessed oil, that being like the lantern, He then mentioned the place of that lamp, which is the mosques, which are the dearest of places on earth to Allah the Exalted, and are His houses in which He is worshipped and declared One. So He said: {In houses which Allah has permitted to be raised} meaning: Allah the Exalted commanded that they be raised, that is, that they be purified from filth and idle talk, and from deeds and words unbefitting them. This is as Ali ibn Abi Talhah said, from Ibn Abbas, concerning this noble verse: {In houses which Allah has permitted to be raised}, he said: Allah, glory be to Him, forbade idle talk within them. Ikrimah, Abu Salih, al-Dahhak, Nafi ibn Jubayr, Abu Bakr ibn Sulayman ibn Abi Hathmah, Sufyan ibn Husayn, and others among the scholars of the commentators said likewise.

Qatadah said: These are the mosques; Allah, glory be to Him, commanded their building and their raising, and commanded their upkeep and their purification. It has been mentioned to us that Ka'b used to say: It is written in the Torah: "Indeed My houses on earth are the mosques, and whoever performs ablution and perfects his ablution, then visits Me in My house, I honor him, and it is a right due upon the one visited to honor the visitor." Abd al-Rahman ibn Abi Hatim related this in his tafsir.

Many hadiths have come down concerning the building of mosques, their reverence and honoring, their being perfumed and fumigated with incense. That has its own separate place where it is discussed, and I have written a separate treatise on that matter, and to Allah belongs praise and grace. We shall, with the help of Allah the Exalted, mention here a portion of that, if Allah the Exalted wills, and in Him is trust and upon Him is reliance:

From the Commander of the Faithful, Uthman ibn Affan, may Allah be pleased with him, who said: I heard the Messenger of Allah ﷺ say: "Whoever builds a mosque seeking thereby the Face of Allah, Allah builds for him its like in Paradise." Both [Bukhari and Muslim] related it in the two Sahihs.

Ibn Majah related, from Umar ibn al-Khattab, may Allah be pleased with him, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Whoever builds a mosque in which the name of Allah is remembered, Allah builds for him a house in Paradise."

Al-Nasa'i has a similar report from Amr ibn Abasah. Hadiths on this subject are very numerous.

From Aishah, may Allah be pleased with her, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ commanded that mosques be built within residential quarters, and that they be cleaned and perfumed. Ahmad and the compilers of the Sunan related it, except al-Nasa'i. Ahmad and Abu Dawud have a similar report from Samurah ibn Jundub.

Al-Bukhari said: Umar said: Build for the people what shelters them, but beware of coloring [walls] red or yellow, lest you tempt the people [into distraction].

Ibn Majah related from him that he said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "The deeds of no people ever became corrupt except that they [then] adorned their mosques." Its chain contains weakness.

Abu Dawud related from Ibn Abbas, may Allah be pleased with both of them, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "I have not been commanded to build mosques high and elaborate." Ibn Abbas said: You will surely adorn them as the Jews and Christians adorned [their places of worship].

From Anas, may Allah be pleased with him, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "The Hour will not come until people vie with one another in [ornamenting] mosques." Imam Ahmad and the compilers of the Sunan related it, except al-Tirmidhi.

From Buraydah, that a man recited poetry aloud in the mosque, then said: Who has called for the red camel? The Prophet ﷺ said: "May you not find it; mosques were only built for that for which they were built." Muslim related it.

From Amr ibn Shu'ayb, from his father, from his grandfather, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ forbade buying and selling, and the recitation of poetry, in mosques. Ahmad and the compilers of the Sunan related it, and al-Tirmidhi said: hasan (sound).

From Abu Hurayrah, may Allah be pleased with him, that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "If you see someone selling or buying in the mosque, say: May Allah not make your trade profitable. And if you see someone seeking a lost item in the mosque, say: May Allah not return it to you." Al-Tirmidhi related it and said: hasan gharib (sound, singular in transmission).

Ibn Majah and others related, from the hadith of Ibn Umar, as a raised report (marfu'): "There are traits unbefitting the mosque: it is not to be used as a thoroughfare, no weapon is to be brandished in it, no bow is to be drawn taut in it, no arrows are to be scattered in it, no raw meat is to be carried through it, no legal punishment is to be carried out in it, no retaliatory penalty is to be exacted in it, and it is not to be turned into a marketplace."

From Wathilah ibn al-Asqa, from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, who said: "Keep away from your mosques your children and your insane ones, your buying and selling, your disputes and the raising of your voices, the carrying out of your legal punishments and the drawing of your swords, and set up places of ablution at their doors, and fumigate them with incense on Fridays."

Ibn Majah also related this, and the chains of both contain weakness.

As for its not being "used as a thoroughfare," some scholars disliked passing through it except from necessity, when one finds no way to avoid it. And in the reported saying: "The angels indeed marvel at a man who passes by the mosque without praying in it."

As for its being said that "no weapon is to be brandished in it, no bow is to be drawn taut in it, and no arrows are to be scattered in it," this is because of the fear that some person might be struck by it, due to the great number of worshippers within it. For this reason the Messenger of Allah ﷺ commanded that when someone passes by carrying arrows, he should grip them by their heads, so as not to harm anyone, as is established in the Sahih.

As for the prohibition of carrying raw meat through it, this is due to the fear of blood dripping from it, just as the menstruating woman was forbidden to pass through it if she feared soiling it.

As for its being said that "no legal punishment is to be carried out in it, nor retaliation exacted," this is due to the fear of causing impurity within it from the one struck or the one whose limb is severed.

As for its not being "turned into a marketplace," this follows from the aforementioned prohibition of buying and selling within it, for it was built only for the remembrance of Allah and for prayer, as the Prophet, upon him be peace and blessings, said to that Bedouin who urinated in a corner of the mosque: "Mosques were not built for this; they were built only for the remembrance of Allah and for prayer within them." He then commanded that a bucket of water be brought, and it was poured over his urine.

In the second hadith: "Keep your children away from your mosques," because they play within them and it is not fitting for them to be there. Umar ibn al-Khattab, may Allah be pleased with him, when he saw children playing in the mosque, would strike them with the mikhfaqah, which is a whip, and he used to patrol the mosque after the night prayer, leaving no one inside it.

"And your insane ones," meaning because of the weakness of their reasoning and because people mock them, which leads to disorder and play within it, and because of the fear that they might soil the mosque, and the like.

"Your buying and selling," as mentioned before.

"Your disputes," meaning litigation and rendering judgment within it. For this reason many scholars have explicitly stated that a judge should not set himself up to settle cases within the mosque, but should be in another place, because of the great amount of contention, quarreling, and shouting involved, which is unbefitting it. For this reason he said next: "and the raising of your voices."

Al-Bukhari said: Ali ibn Abd Allah related to us, Yahya ibn Sa'id related to us, al-Ju'ayd ibn Abd al-Rahman related to us, saying: Yazid ibn Khusayfah related to me, from al-Sa'ib ibn Yazid al-Kindi, who said: I was standing in the mosque, and a man threw a pebble at me. I looked, and it was Umar ibn al-Khattab, who said: Go and bring me these two. So I brought them to him, and he said: Who are you two? Or: Where are you from? They said: We are from the people of Ta'if. He said: Had you been from the people of this town, I would have dealt you a painful blow, raising your voices in the mosque of the Messenger of Allah ﷺ!

Al-Nasa'i said: Suwayd ibn Nasr related to us, from Abd Allah ibn al-Mubarak, from Shu'bah, from Sa'd ibn Ibrahim, from his father Ibrahim ibn Abd al-Rahman ibn Awf, who said: Umar heard the voice of a man in the mosque, and said: Do you know where you are? This too is sound.

His saying: "and the carrying out of your legal punishments, and the drawing of your swords," has already been discussed.

His saying: "and set up places of ablution at their doors," meaning the facilities used for ablution and relieving oneself. Near the mosque of the Messenger of Allah ﷺ there were wells from which people drew water, and drank, purified themselves, performed ablution, and did other such things.

His saying: "and fumigate them with incense on Fridays," meaning: perfume them with incense on the days of Friday because of the great gathering of people on that day.

The hafiz Abu Ya'la al-Mawsili said: Ubayd Allah related to us, Abd al-Rahman ibn Mahdi related to us, from Abd Allah ibn Umar, from Nafi, from Ibn Umar, that Umar used to fumigate the mosque of the Messenger of Allah ﷺ with incense every Friday. Its chain is hasan (sound), there is no harm in it, and Allah knows best.

It has been established in the two Sahihs (Bukhari and Muslim) from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ that he said: "The prayer of a man in congregation is multiplied over his prayer in his house and in his marketplace by twenty-five times. That is because when he performs ablution and does it well, then goes out to the mosque, going out for nothing but the prayer, he does not take a step but that a degree is raised for him by it, and a sin is removed from him by it. Then when he prays, the angels continue praying for him as long as he remains in his place of prayer: 'O Allah, send blessings upon him, O Allah, have mercy on him.' And he remains in a state of prayer as long as he waits for the prayer."

Al-Daraqutni has it as a raised report: "There is no prayer for the neighbor of the mosque except in the mosque."

And in the Sunan: "Give glad tidings to those who walk to the mosques in the darkness, of complete light on the Day of Resurrection."

It is recommended for one who enters the mosque to begin with his right foot, and to say, as is established in Sahih al-Bukhari from Abdullah ibn Amr, may Allah be pleased with him, from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, that when he entered the mosque he would say: "I seek refuge in Allah the Magnificent, and in His noble Face, and His eternal sovereignty, from the accursed Satan." [He said: Was that all? He said: Yes.] He said: When he says that, Satan says: "He has been protected from me for the rest of the day."

Muslim narrated with his chain from Abu Humayd, or Abu Usayd, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "When one of you enters the mosque, let him say: O Allah, open for me the doors of Your mercy. And when he leaves, let him say: O Allah, I ask You from Your bounty."

Al-Nasa'i narrated it from both of them, from the Prophet ﷺ, [similarly].

And from Abu Hurayrah, may Allah be pleased with him, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "When one of you enters the mosque, let him send salutations upon the Prophet ﷺ and say: O Allah, open for me the doors of Your mercy. And when he leaves, let him send salutations upon the Prophet ﷺ and say: O Allah, protect me from the accursed Satan."

Ibn Majah, Ibn Khuzaymah, and Ibn Hibban narrated it in their two Sahihs.

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Isma'il ibn Ibrahim told us, Layth ibn Abi Sulaym told us, from Abdullah ibn Hasan, from his mother Fatimah bint Husayn, from her grandmother Fatimah, daughter of the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, who said: When the Messenger of Allah ﷺ entered the mosque he would send blessings and salutations upon Muhammad, then say: "O Allah, forgive me my sins, and open for me the doors of Your mercy." And when he left he would send blessings and salutations upon Muhammad, then say: "O Allah, forgive me my sins, and open for me the doors of Your bounty."

Al-Tirmidhi and Ibn Majah narrated it, and al-Tirmidhi said: This is a hasan (sound) hadith, but its chain is not connected, because Fatimah bint al-Husayn the younger did not meet Fatimah the elder.

All that we have mentioned, together with what we have left out of the hadiths reported on this subject due to length, all of it falls under His statement: {In houses which Allah has permitted to be raised}.

His statement, {and His name be mentioned therein}, means: the name of Allah, as in His statement: {O children of Adam, take your adornment at every mosque} [al-A'raf: 31], and His statement: {And turn your faces at every place of worship and call upon Him, sincere in religion for Him} [al-A'raf: 29], and His statement: {And the mosques are for Allah, so do not call upon anyone besides Allah} [al-Jinn: 18].

Ibn Abbas said: {and His name be mentioned therein} means: His Book is recited therein.

His statement: {He is glorified therein in the mornings and the evenings}, means: in the early mornings and the late afternoons. Al-asal (evenings) is the plural of asil, which is the end of the day.

Sa'id ibn Jubayr said, from Ibn Abbas: Every mention of tasbih (glorification) in the Qur'an refers to prayer.

Ali ibn Abi Talhah said, from Ibn Abbas: By al-ghuduww (mornings) he means the dawn prayer, and by al-asal (evenings) he means the afternoon prayer, and these two were the first prayers Allah made obligatory, so He loved to mention them and to remind His servants by them.

Likewise al-Hasan and al-Dahhak said: {He is glorified therein in the mornings and the evenings} means: the prayer.

Those among the reciters who read it as "yusabbahu lahu fiha bi'l-ghuduwwi wa'l-asal" (with fatha on the ba of yusabbah, making it passive, with the doer of the action unnamed) would make a full stop at {wa'l-asal}, and begin anew with {Men whom neither commerce nor sale distracts from the remembrance of Allah}, as though this were an explanation of the omitted doer, similar to what the poet said:

"Let Yazid be wept for, one humbled by dispute, and one afflicted by what misfortunes cast down..."

as though he said: Who weeps for him? He said: This one weeps for him. And it is as though it were said: Who glorifies Him therein? He said: Men.

As for the reading of those who read it as "yusabbihu" (with kasra on the ba), making it an active verb with {rijal} (men) as its subject, then the pause is best made only after the subject, since that completes the sentence.

His statement {rijal} (men) indicates their lofty aspirations, their intentions, and their exalted resolves, by which they became those who populate the mosques, which are the houses of Allah on His earth, and places of His worship, of gratitude to Him, of His oneness and glorification, as He said: {Among the believers are men who have been true to what they pledged to Allah} [al-Ahzab: 23].

As for women, their prayer in their houses is better for them, due to what Abu Dawud narrated from Abdullah ibn Mas'ud, may Allah be pleased with him, from the Prophet ﷺ, who said: "A woman's prayer in her house is better than her prayer in her chamber, and her prayer in her innermost private room is better than her prayer in her house."

Imam Ahmad also said: [chain] Yahya ibn Ghaylan told us, Rishdin told us, Amr told me, from Abu al-Samh, from al-Sa'ib, the freedman of Umm Salamah, from Umm Salamah, may Allah be pleased with her, from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, that he said: "The best places of prayer for women are the innermost parts of their houses."

Imam Ahmad also said: [chain] Harun told us, Abdullah ibn Wahb informed me, Dawud ibn Qays told us, from Abdullah ibn Suwayd al-Ansari, from his aunt Umm Humayd, the wife of Abu Humayd al-Sa'idi, that she came to the Prophet ﷺ and said: O Messenger of Allah, I love to pray with you. He said: "I know that you love to pray with me, but your prayer in your inner room is better than your prayer in your chamber, and your prayer in your chamber is better than your prayer in your house, and your prayer in your house is better than your prayer in the mosque of your people, and your prayer in the mosque of your people is better than your prayer in my mosque." He said: So she ordered that a place of prayer be built for her in the furthest and darkest part of her house, and she used to pray there until she met Allah, Mighty and Majestic. The two main compilers (Bukhari and Muslim) did not include this. That said, it is permissible for her to attend congregational prayer with the men, on condition that she not cause harm to any of the men by displaying adornment or the scent of perfume, as is established in the two Sahihs from Abdullah ibn Umar, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Do not prevent the female servants of Allah from the mosques of Allah."

Narrated by Bukhari and Muslim, and Ahmad and Abu Dawud add: "and their houses are better for them," and in another version: "and let them go out unscented," meaning: without any perfume on them.

It is established in Sahih Muslim, from Zaynab, wife of Ibn Mas'ud, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said to us: "When any one of you attends the mosque, let her not touch any perfume."

And in the two Sahihs from Aisha, may Allah be pleased with her, that she said: The believing women used to attend the dawn prayer with the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, then return wrapped in their outer garments, unrecognized on account of the darkness.

Also in the two Sahihs from her, she said: If the Messenger of Allah ﷺ had seen what women have introduced, he would have prevented them from the mosques, just as the women of the Children of Israel were prevented.

His statement: {Men whom neither commerce nor sale distracts from the remembrance of Allah}, is like His statement: {O you who believe, let not your wealth and your children distract you from the remembrance of Allah, and whoever does that, then those are the losers} [al-Munafiqun: 9], and He said: {O you who believe, when the call is made for prayer on the day of Friday, hasten to the remembrance of Allah and leave off trading, that is better for you if you only knew} [al-Jumu'ah: 9].

He, exalted is He, says: The worldly life and its ornaments and adornments, and the pleasures of its trade and its scent, do not occupy them away from the remembrance of their Lord, who is their Creator and their Provider, and those who know that what is with Him is better for them and more beneficial than what is in their own hands, because what they possess runs out while what is with Allah remains. For this reason He said: {neither commerce nor sale distracts them from the remembrance of Allah, the establishment of prayer, and the giving of zakat}, meaning: they give precedence to obedience to Him, His will, and love of Him, over their own desires and their own love.

Hushaym said, from Sayyar: [he said] I was told, from Ibn Mas'ud, that he saw a group of the people of the marketplace who, when the call for prayer was made, left their trading and rose up for prayer. Abdullah said: These are among those whom Allah mentioned in His Book: {Men whom neither commerce nor sale distracts from the remembrance of Allah}.

Similarly, Amr ibn Dinar al-Qahramani narrated, from Salim, from Abdullah ibn Umar, may Allah be pleased with them both, that he was in the market when the prayer was established, so they closed their shops and entered the mosque. Ibn Umar said, "It was concerning them that this was revealed: {Men whom neither commerce nor sale distracts from the remembrance of Allah}." Narrated by Ibn Abi Hatim and Ibn Jarir.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: Muhammad ibn Abdullah ibn Bakr al-San'ani narrated to us, Abu Sa'id, the freedman of Banu Hashim, narrated to us, Abdullah ibn Bujayr narrated to us, Abu Abd Rabb narrated to us, saying: Abu al-Darda, may Allah be pleased with him, said: "I stand upon these steps conducting trade, earning three hundred dinars every day, yet I attend the prayer every day in the mosque. Now, I do not say that this is not lawful, but I love to be among those about whom Allah said: {Men whom neither commerce nor sale distracts from the remembrance of Allah}."

Amr ibn Dinar al-A'war said: "I was with Salim ibn Abdullah, and we were heading to the mosque. We passed by the market of Medina, and they had risen for the prayer and covered their goods. Salim looked at their goods, with no one attending them, and recited this verse: {Men whom neither commerce nor sale distracts from the remembrance of Allah}, then said: 'These are they.'"

Sa'id ibn Abi al-Hasan and al-Dahhak said likewise: "Commerce and sale do not distract them from coming to the prayer at its proper time."

Matar al-Warraq said: "They used to buy and sell, but when one of them heard the call while his scale was in his hand, he would lower it and go forward to the prayer."

Ali ibn Abi Talha said, from Ibn Abbas, regarding {neither commerce nor sale distracts them from the remembrance of Allah}: "He means from the obligatory prayer." Al-Rabi' ibn Anas and Muqatil ibn Hayyan said likewise.

Al-Suddi said: "From the prayer in congregation."

And from Muqatil ibn Hayyan: "That does not distract them from attending the prayer, from establishing it as Allah commanded them, from maintaining its appointed times, and from what Allah entrusted them to preserve regarding it."

Concerning His saying, {They fear a day in which the hearts and the sights will be overturned}: that is, the Day of Resurrection, in which the hearts and the sights will be overturned, meaning from the intensity of terror and the magnitude of the horrors, as the Most High said: {And warn them of the approaching day, when the hearts will be at the throats, choking them} [Ghafir: 18], and the Most High said: {He only delays them for a day when the eyes will stare in horror} [Ibrahim: 42], and the Most High said: {And they feed food, despite love for it, to the needy, the orphan, and the captive, saying: We feed you only for the sake of Allah's countenance; we desire no reward nor thanks from you. Indeed, we fear from our Lord a Day, austere and distressful. So Allah will protect them from the evil of that Day and give them radiance and joy, and reward them for their patience with Paradise and silk} [al-Insan: 8-12].

And He said here, {That Allah may reward them the best of what they used to do}, meaning: these are among those from whom Allah accepts the best of their deeds and overlooks their bad deeds.

Concerning His saying, {And increase them from His bounty}: that is, He accepts from them the good and multiplies it for them, as the Most High said: {Indeed, Allah does not wrong anyone by an atom's weight, and if there is a good deed, He multiplies it and gives from Himself a great reward} [al-Nisa: 40], and the Most High said: {Whoever comes with a good deed will have ten times its like} [al-An'am: 160], and He said: {Who is it that will lend Allah a goodly loan, that He may multiply it for him many times over} [al-Baqarah: 245], and He said: {And Allah multiplies for whom He wills} [al-Baqarah: 261], just as He said here: {And Allah provides for whom He wills without account}.

And from Ibn Mas'ud: that milk was brought to him, and he offered it to his companions one by one, but none of them drank it because he was fasting. Ibn Mas'ud took it, and he was not fasting, and drank it, then recited the saying of the Most High: {They fear a day in which the hearts and the sights will be overturned}. Narrated by al-Nasa'i and Ibn Abi Hatim, from the hadith of al-A'mash, from Ibrahim, from Alqamah, from him.

[Ibn Abi Hatim] also said: My father narrated to us, Suwayd ibn Sa'id narrated to us, Ali ibn Mushir narrated to us, from Abd al-Rahman ibn Ishaq, from Shahr ibn Hawshab, from Asma bint Yazid, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "When Allah gathers the first and the last on the Day of Resurrection, a caller will come and call out with a voice that will make the creation hear: 'The people of the gathering will know who is most deserving of honor. Let those stand up whom neither commerce nor sale distracted from the remembrance of Allah.' So they will stand up, and they are few. Then He will call the rest of the creation to account."

Al-Tabarani narrated, from the hadith of Baqiyyah, from Isma'il ibn Abdullah al-Kindi, from al-A'mash, from Abu Wa'il, from Ibn Mas'ud, from the Prophet ﷺ, concerning His saying, {That He may give them their rewards in full and increase them from His bounty} [Fatir: 30]: he said: "{Their rewards}: He will admit them into Paradise. {And increase them from His bounty}: the intercession for whoever intercession is due to him, for whoever did good for them in the world."

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

لَمَّا ضَرَبَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى [مَثَلَ] قَلْبِ الْمُؤْمِنِ، وَمَا فِيهِ مِنَ الْهُدَى وَالْعِلْمِ، بِالْمِصْبَاحِ فِي الزُّجَاجَةِ الصَّافِيَةِ الْمُتَوَقِّدِ مِنْ زَيْتٍ طَيِّبٍ، وَذَلِكَ كَالْقِنْدِيلِ، ذَكَرَ مَحِلَّهَا وَهِيَ الْمَسَاجِدُ، الَّتِي هِيَ أَحَبُّ الْبِقَاعِ إِلَى اللَّهِ تَعَالَى مِنَ الْأَرْضِ، وَهِيَ بُيُوتُهُ الَّتِي يُعْبَدُ فِيهَا ويُوَحّد، فَقَالَ: ﴿فِي بُيُوتٍ أَذِنَ اللَّهُ أَنْ تُرْفَعَ﴾ أَيْ: أَمَرَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى بِرَفْعِهَا، أَيْ: بِتَطْهِيرِهَا مِنَ الدَّنَسِ وَاللَّغْوِ، وَالْأَفْعَالِ وَالْأَقْوَالِ الَّتِي لَا تَلِيقُ فِيهَا، كَمَا قَالَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ فِي هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ الْكَرِيمَةِ: ﴿فِي بُيُوتٍ أَذِنَ اللَّهُ أَنْ تُرْفَعَ﴾ قَالَ: نَهَى اللَّهُ سُبْحَانَهُ عَنِ اللَّغْوِ فِيهَا. وَكَذَا قَالَ عِكْرِمَةُ، وَأَبُو صَالِحٍ، وَالضَّحَّاكُ، وَنَافِعُ بْنُ جُبَيْرٍ، وَأَبُو بَكْرِ بْنُ سُلَيْمَانَ بْنِ أَبِي حَثْمة وَسُفْيَانُ بْنُ حُسَيْنٍ، وَغَيْرُهُمْ مِنْ عُلَمَاءِ الْمُفَسِّرِينَ. 

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: هِيَ هَذِهِ الْمَسَاجِدُ، أَمَرَ اللَّهُ، سُبْحَانَهُ، بِبِنَائِهَا وَرَفْعِهَا، وَأَمَرَ بِعِمَارَتِهَا وَتَطْهِيرِهَا. وَقَدْ ذُكِرَ لَنَا أَنَّ كَعْبًا كَانَ يَقُولُ: إِنَّ فِي التَّوْرَاةِ مَكْتُوبًا: " أَلَا إِنَّ بُيُوتِي فِي الْأَرْضِ الْمَسَاجِدُ، وَإِنَّهُ مَنْ تَوَضَّأَ فَأَحْسَنَ وَضَوْءَهُ، ثُمَّ زَارَنِي فِي بَيْتِي أَكْرَمْتُهُ، وحَقّ عَلَى المَزُور كرامةُ الزَّائِرِ". رَوَاهُ عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ فِي تَفْسِيرِهِ.

وَقَدْ وَرَدَتْ أَحَادِيثُ كَثِيرَةٌ فِي بِنَاءِ الْمَسَاجِدِ، وَاحْتِرَامِهَا وَتَوْقِيرِهَا، وَتَطْيِيبِهَا وَتَبْخِيرِهَا. وَذَلِكَ لَهُ مَحَلٌّ مُفْرَدٌ يُذْكَرُ فِيهِ، وَقَدْ كَتَبْتُ فِي ذَلِكَ جُزْءًا عَلَى حدَة، وَلِلَّهِ الْحَمْدُ وَالْمِنَّةُ. وَنَحْنُ بِعَوْنِ اللَّهِ تَعَالَى نَذْكُرُ هَاهُنَا طَرَفًا مِنْ ذَلِكَ، إِنْ شَاءَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى، وَبِهِ الثِّقَةُ وَعَلَيْهِ التُّكْلَانُ:

فَعَنْ أَمِيرِ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ عُثْمَانَ بْنِ عَفَّانَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: سمعتُ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَقُولُ: "مَنْ بَنَى مَسْجِدًا يَبْتَغِي بِهِ وَجْهَ اللَّهِ، بَنَى اللَّهُ لَهُ مَثْلَهُ فِي الْجَنَّةِ". أَخْرَجَاهُ فِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ .

وَرَوَى ابْنُ مَاجَهْ، عَنْ عُمَرَ بْنِ الْخَطَّابِ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "مَنْ بَنَى مَسْجِدًا يُذْكَرُ فِيهِ اسْمُ اللَّهِ، بَنَى اللَّهُ لَهُ بَيْتًا فِي الْجَنَّةِ" .

وَلِلنَّسَائِيِّ عَنْ عَمْرِو بْنِ عَبَسَة مَثْلُهُ . وَالْأَحَادِيثُ فِي هَذَا كَثِيرَةٌ جِدًّا.

وَعَنْ عَائِشَةَ رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهَا، قَالَتْ: أَمْرَ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ بِبِنَاءِ الْمَسَاجِدِ فِي الدور، وأن تنظف وَتُطَيَّبَ . رَوَاهُ أَحْمَدُ وَأَهْلُ السُّنَنِ إِلَّا النَّسَائِيُّ. وَلِأَحْمَدَ وَأَبِي دَاوُدَ، عَنْ سَمُرة بْنِ جُنْدب نَحْوُهُ. 

وَقَالَ الْبُخَارِيُّ: قَالَ عُمَرُ: ابْنِ لِلنَّاسِ مَا يُكِنُّهُمْ، وَإِيَّاكَ أَنْ تُحَمِّرَ أَوْ تُصَفِّرَ فَتَفْتِنَ النَّاسَ .

وَرَوَى ابْنُ مَاجَهْ عَنْهُ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ صَلَّى اللَّهُ عليه وسلم: "مَا سَاءَ عملُ قَوْمٍ قَطُّ إِلَّا زَخْرَفُوا مَسَاجِدَهُمْ". وَفِي إِسْنَادِهِ ضَعْفٌ.

وَرَوَى أَبُو دَاوُدَ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمَا، قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "مَا أمِرْتُ بِتَشْيِيدِ الْمَسَاجِدِ". قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: لَتُزَخرفُنّها كَمَا زَخْرَفت الْيَهُودُ وَالنَّصَارَى 

وَعَنْ أَنَسٍ رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "لَا تَقُومُ السَّاعَةُ حَتَّى يَتَبَاهَى النَّاسُ فِي الْمَسَاجِدِ". رَوَاهُ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ وَأَهْلُ السُّنَنِ إِلَّا التِّرْمِذِيُّ 

وَعَنْ بُرَيْدَةَ أَنَّ رَجُلا أنشدَ فِي الْمَسْجِدِ، فَقَالَ: مَنْ دَعَا إِلَى الْجَمْلِ الْأَحْمَرِ؟ فَقَالَ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ: "لَا وَجَدْتَ، إِنَّمَا بُنِيت الْمَسَاجِدُ لِمَا بُنِيَتْ لَهُ". رَوَاهُ مُسْلِمٌ. 

وَعَنْ عَمْرِو بْنِ شُعَيْبٍ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنْ جَدِّهِ قَالَ: نَهَى رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ، عَنِ الْبَيْعِ وَالِابْتِيَاعِ، وَعَنْ تَنَاشُدِ الْأَشْعَارِ فِي الْمَسَاجِدِ. رَوَاهُ أَحْمَدُ وَأَهْلُ السُّنَنِ ، وَقَالَ التِّرْمِذِيُّ: حَسَنٌ.

وَعَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ صَلَّى اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ سَلَّمَ: قَالَ: "إِذَا رَأَيْتُمْ مَنْ يَبِيعُ أَوْ يَبْتَاعُ فِي الْمَسْجِدِ، فَقُولُوا: لَا أَرْبَحَ اللَّهُ تِجَارَتَكَ. وَإِذَا رَأَيْتُمْ مَنْ يَنشُد ضَالَّةً فِي الْمَسْجِدِ، فَقُولُوا: لَا رَدَّ اللَّهُ عَلَيْكَ". رَوَاهُ التِّرْمِذِيُّ، وَقَالَ: حَسَنٌ غَرِيبٌ. 

وَقَدْ رَوَى ابْنُ مَاجَهْ وَغَيْرُهُ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ ابْنِ عُمَرَ مَرْفُوعًا، قَالَ: "خِصَالٌ لَا تَنْبَغِي فِي الْمَسْجِدِ: لَا يُتَّخذُ طَرِيقًا، وَلَا يُشْهَرُ فِيهِ سِلَاحٌ، وَلَا يُنبَض فِيهِ بِقَوْسٍ، وَلَا يُنْثَرُ فِيهِ نَبْلٌ، وَلَا يُمرّ فِيهِ بِلَحْمٍ نِيء: وَلَا يُضرَبُ فِيهِ حَدٌّ، وَلَا يُقْتَص فِيهِ مِنْ أَحَدٍ، وَلَا يُتَّخذ سُوقًا" .

وَعَنْ وَاثِلَةَ بْنِ الْأَسْقَعِ، عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَ: "جَنِّبوا الْمَسَاجِدَ صِبْيَانَكُمْ وَمَجَانِينَكُمْ، وَشِرَاءَكُمْ وَبَيْعَكُمْ، وَخُصُومَاتِكُمْ وَرَفْعَ أَصْوَاتِكُمْ، وَإِقَامَةَ حُدُودِكُمْ وَسَلَّ سُيُوفِكُمْ، وَاتَّخِذُوا عَلَى أَبْوَابِهَا الْمَطَاهِرَ، وجَمّروها فِي الجُمَع".

وَرَوَاهُ ابْنُ مَاجَهْ أَيْضًا وَفِي إِسْنَادِهِمَا ضَعُفٌ.

أَمَّا أَنَّهُ "لَا يُتَّخَذُ طَرِيقًا" فَقَدْ كَرِهَ بَعْضُ الْعُلَمَاءِ الْمُرُورَ فِيهِ إِلَّا لِحَاجَةٍ إِذَا وَجَد مَنْدُوحَةً عَنْهُ. وَفِي الْأَثَرِ: "إِنَّ الْمَلَائِكَةَ لَتَتَعَجَّبُ مِنَ الرَّجُلِ يَمُرُّ بِالْمَسْجِدِ لَا يُصَلِّي فِيهِ".

وَأَمَّا أَنَّهُ "لَا يُشْهَرُ فِيهِ بِسِلَاحٍ . وَلَا يُنْبَضُ فِيهِ بِقَوْسٍ، وَلَا يُنْثَرُ فِيهِ نَبْلٌ . فَلِمَا يُخْشَى مِنْ إِصَابَةِ بَعْضِ النَّاسِ بِهِ، لِكَثْرَةِ الْمُصَلِّينَ فِيهِ؛ وَلِهَذَا أَمْرَ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ إِذَا مَرَّ أَحَدٌ بِسِهَامٍ أَنْ يَقْبِضَ عَلَى نِصَالِهَا؛ لِئَلَّا يُؤْذِيَ أَحَدًا، كَمَا ثَبَتَ فِي الصَّحِيحِ .

وَأَمَا النَّهْيُ عَنِ الْمُرُورِ بِاللَّحْمِ النَّيِّءِ فِيهِ، فَلِما يُخْشَى مِنْ تَقَاطُرِ الدَّمِ مِنْهُ، كَمَا نُهِيَتِ الْحَائِضُ عَنِ الْمُرُورِ فِيهِ إِذَا خَافَتِ التَّلْوِيثَ.

وَأَمَّا أَنَّهُ "لَا يُضْرَبُ فِيهِ حَدٌّ وَلَا يُقْتَصُّ"، فَلِمَا يُخْشَى مِنْ إِيجَادِ نَجَاسَةٍ فِيهِ مِنَ الْمَضْرُوبِ أَوِ الْمَقْطُوعِ.

وَأَمَّا أَنَّهُ "لَا يُتَّخَذُ سُوقًا"، فَلِمَا تَقَدَّمَ مِنَ النَّهْيِ عَنِ الْبَيْعِ وَالشِّرَاءِ فِيهِ، فَإِنَّهُ إِنَّمَا بُنِيَ لِذِكْرِ اللَّهِ وَالصَّلَاةِ كَمَا قَالَ النَّبِيُّ عَلَيْهِ الصَّلَاةُ وَالسَّلَامُ، لِذَلِكَ الْأَعْرَابِيِّ الَّذِي بَالَ فِي طَائِفَةِ الْمَسْجِدِ: "إِنَّ الْمَسَاجِدَ لَمْ تُبْنَ لِهَذَا، إِنَّمَا بُنِيَتْ لِذِكْرِ اللَّهِ وَالصَّلَاةِ فِيهَا". ثُمَّ أَمَرَ بسَجْل مِنْ مَاءٍ، فَأُهْرِيقَ عَلَى بَوْلِهِ .

وَفِي الْحَدِيثِ الثَّانِي: "جَنِّبوا مَسَاجِدَكُمْ صِبْيَانَكُمْ"، وَذَلِكَ لِأَنَّهُمْ يَلْعَبُونَ فِيهِ وَلَا يُنَاسِبُهُمْ، وَقَدْ كَانَ عُمَرُ بْنُ الْخَطَّابِ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، إِذَا رَأَى صِبْيَانًا يَلْعَبُونَ فِي الْمَسْجِدِ ، ضَرَبَهُمْ بالمِخْفَقَة -وَهِيَ الدِّرَّة -وَكَانَ يَعُسّ الْمَسْجِدِ بَعْدَ الْعَشَاءِ، فَلَا يَتْرُكُ فِيهِ أَحَدًا.

"وَمَجَانِينَكُمْ" يَعْنِي: لِأَجْلِ ضَعْفِ عُقُولِهِمْ، وسَخْر النَّاسِ بِهِمْ، فَيُؤَدِّي إِلَى اللَّعِبِ فِيهَا، وَلِمَا يَخْشَى مِنْ تَقْذِيرِهِمُ الْمَسْجِدَ، وَنَحْوِ ذَلِكَ.

"وَبَيْعَكُمْ وَشِرَاءَكُمْ" كَمَا تَقَدَّمَ.

"وَخُصُومَاتِكُمْ" يَعْنِي: التَّحَاكُمَ وَالْحُكْمَ فِيهِ؛ وَلِهَذَا نَصَّ كَثِيرٌ مِنَ الْعُلَمَاءِ عَلَى أَنَّ الْحَاكِمَ لَا يَنْتَصِبُ لِفَصْلِ الْأَقْضِيَةِ فِي الْمَسْجِدِ، بَلْ يَكُونُ فِي مَوْضِعٍ غَيْرِهِ؛ لِمَا فِيهِ مِنْ كَثْرَةِ الْحُكُومَاتِ وَالتَّشَاجُرِ وَالْعِيَاطِ الَّذِي لَا يُنَاسِبُهُ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ بَعْدَهُ: "وَرَفْعَ أَصْوَاتِكُمْ".

وَقَالَ الْبُخَارِيُّ: حَدَّثَنَا عَلِيُّ بْنُ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ، حَدَّثَنَا يَحْيَى بْنُ سَعِيدٍ، حَدَّثَنَا الجُعَيْد بْنُ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ قَالَ: حَدَّثَنِي يَزِيدُ بْنُ خُصَيفَة ، عَنِ السَّائِبِ بْنِ يَزيدَ الكنْديِّ قَالَ: كُنْتُ قَائِمًا فِي الْمَسْجِدِ، فَحَصَبَنِي رَجُلٌ، فَنَظَرْتُ فَإِذَا عُمَرُ بْنُ الْخَطَّابِ، فَقَالَ: اذْهَبْ فَأْتِنِي بِهَذَيْنَ. فَجِئْتُهُ بِهِمَا، فَقَالَ: مَنْ أَنْتُمَا؟ أَوْ: مِنْ أَيْنَ أَنْتُمَا؟ قَالَا مِنْ أَهْلِ الطَّائِفِ. قال: لو كنتما من أهل الْبَلَدِ لَأَوْجَعْتُكُمَا: تَرْفَعَانِ أَصْوَاتَكُمَا فِي مَسْجِدِ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ .

وَقَالَ النَّسَائِيُّ: حَدَّثَنَا سُوَيْد بْنُ نَصْرٍ، عَنْ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ الْمُبَارَكِ، عَنْ شُعْبَةَ، عَنْ سَعْدِ بْنِ إِبْرَاهِيمَ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ إِبْرَاهِيمَ بْنِ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنِ عَوْفٍ قَالَ: سَمِعَ عُمَرُ صَوْتَ رَجُلٍ فِي الْمَسْجِدِ فَقَالَ: أَتَدْرِي أَيْنَ أَنْتَ؟ وَهَذَا أَيْضًا صَحِيحٌ. 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: "وَإِقَامَةَ حُدُودِكُمْ، وَسَلَّ سُيُوفِكُمْ": تَقَدَّمَا. 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: "وَاتَّخِذُوا عَلَى أَبْوَابِهَا الْمَطَاهِرَ" يَعْنِي: الْمَرَاحِيضَ الَّتِي يُسْتَعَانُ بِهَا عَلَى الْوُضُوءِ وَقَضَاءِ الْحَاجَةِ. وَقَدْ كَانَتْ قَرِيبًا مِنْ مَسْجِدِ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ آبَارٌ يَسْتَقُونَ منها، فيشربون ويتطهرون، ويتوضؤون وَغَيْرَ ذَلِكَ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: "وجمِّروها فِي الجُمَع" يَعْنِي: بَخِّرُوهَا فِي أَيَّامِ الجُمَع لِكَثْرَةِ اجْتِمَاعِ النَّاسِ يَوْمَئِذٍ.

وَقَدْ قَالَ الْحَافِظُ أَبُو يَعْلَى الْمَوْصِلِيُّ: حَدَّثَنَا عُبَيْدُ اللَّهِ، حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ مَهْدِيٍّ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عُمَرَ، عَنْ نَافِعٍ عَنِ ابْنِ عُمَرَ؛ أَنَّ عُمَرَ كَانَ يُجَمِّر مَسْجِدِ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ كُلَّ جُمُعَةٍ. إِسْنَادُهُ حَسَنٌ لَا بَأْسَ بِهِ وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

وَقَدْ ثَبَتَ فِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: "صَلَاةُ الرَّجُلِ فِي الْجَمَاعَةِ تُضَعَّف عَلَى صِلَاتِهِ فِي بَيْتِهِ وَفِي سُوقِهِ، خَمْسًا وَعِشْرِينَ ضِعْفًا. وَذَلِكَ أَنَّهُ إِذَا تَوَضَّأَ فَأَحْسَنَ وَضَوْءَهُ ثُمَّ خَرَجَ إِلَى الْمَسْجِدِ، لَا يُخْرِجُهُ إِلَّا الصَّلَاةُ، لَمْ يَخطُ خَطوة إِلَّا رُفع لَهُ بِهَا دَرَجَةٌ، وَحُطَّ عَنْهُ بِهَا خَطِيئَةٌ، فَإِذَا صَلَّى لَمْ تَزَلِ الْمَلَائِكَةُ تُصَلِّي عَلَيْهِ مَا دَامَ فِي مُصَلاه: اللَّهُمَّ صَلِّ عَلَيْهِ، اللَّهُمَّ ارْحَمْهُ، وَلَا يَزَالُ فِي صَلَاةٍ مَا انْتَظَرَ الصَّلَاةَ" 

وَعِنْدَ الدَّارَقُطْنِيِّ مَرْفُوعًا: "لَا صَلَاةَ لِجَارِ الْمَسْجِدِ إِلَّا فِي الْمَسْجِدِ" .

وَفِي السُّنَنِ: "بشِّر الْمَشَّائِينَ إِلَى الْمَسَاجِدِ فِي الظُّلَمِ بِالنُّورِ التَّامِّ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ" .

وَالْمُسْتَحَبُّ لِمَنْ دَخَلَ الْمَسْجِدَ أَنْ يَبْدَأَ بِرِجْلِهِ الْيُمْنَى، وَأَنْ يَقُولَ كَمَا ثَبَتَ فِي صَحِيحِ الْبُخَارِيُّ عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عَمرو رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ أَنَّهُ كَانَ إذا دخل المسجد قال: أَعُوذُ بِاللَّهِ الْعَظِيمِ، وَبِوَجْهِهِ الْكَرِيمِ، وَسُلْطَانِهِ الْقَدِيمِ، مِنَ الشَّيْطَانِ الرَّجِيمِ" [قَالَ: أَقَطُّ؟ قَالَ: نَعَمْ] . قَالَ: فَإِذَا قَالَ ذَلِكَ قَالَ الشَّيْطَانُ: حُفظ مِنِّي سَائِرَ الْيَوْمِ .

وَرَوَى مُسْلِمٌ بِسَنَدِهِ عَنْ أَبِي حُمَيْدٍ -أَوْ: أَبِي أسَيْد -قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "إِذَا دخل أحدكم المسجد فليقل: اللهم افتح لي أبواب رحمتك، وإذا خرج فليقل: اللهم إني أَسْأَلُكَ مِنْ فَضْلِكَ".

وَرَوَاهُ النَّسَائِيُّ عَنْهُمَا، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ [مِثْلَهُ] .

وَعَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "إِذَا دَخَلَ أَحَدُكُمُ الْمَسْجِدَ، فَلْيُسَلِّمْ عَلَى النَّبِيِّ ﷺ وَلِيَقُلِ: اللَّهُمَّ افْتَحْ لِي أَبْوَابَ رَحْمَتِكَ. وَإِذَا خَرَجَ فَلْيُسَلِّمْ عَلَى النَّبِيِّ ﷺ وَلِيَقِلِ: اللَّهُمَّ اعْصِمْنِي مِنَ الشَّيْطَانِ الرَّجِيمِ".

وَرَوَاهُ ابْنُ مَاجَهْ، وَابْنُ خُزَيْمَةَ وَابْنُ حِبَّان فِي صَحِيحَيْهِمَا .

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا إِسْمَاعِيلُ بْنُ إِبْرَاهِيمَ، حَدَّثَنَا لَيْث بْنُ أَبِي سُلَيْمٍ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ حَسَنٍ . عَنْ أُمِّهِ فَاطِمَةَ بِنْتِ حُسَيْنٍ، عَنْ جَدَّتِهَا فَاطِمَةُ بِنْتُ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَتْ: كَانَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ إِذَا دَخَلَ الْمَسْجِدَ صَلَّى عَلَى مُحَمَّدٍ وَسَلَّمَ، ثُمَّ قَالَ:"اللَّهُمَّ، اغْفِرْ لِي ذُنُوبِي، وَافْتَحْ لِي أَبْوَابَ رَحْمَتِكَ". وَإِذَا خَرَجَ صَلَّى عَلَى مُحَمَّدٍ وَسَلَّمَ ثُمَّ قَالَ: "اللَّهُمَّ، اغْفِرْ لِي ذُنُوبِي، وَافْتَحْ لِي أَبْوَابَ فَضْلِكَ".

وَرَوَاهُ التِّرْمِذِيُّ وَابْنُ مَاجَهْ ، وَقَالَ التِّرْمِذِيُّ: هَذَا حَدِيثٌ حَسَنٌ وَإِسْنَادُهُ لَيْسَ بِمُتَّصِلٍ؛ لِأَنَّ فَاطِمَةَ بِنْتَ الْحُسَيْنِ الصُّغْرَى لَمْ تُدْرِكْ فَاطِمَةَ الْكُبْرَى.

فَهَذَا الَّذِي ذَكَرْنَاهُ، مَعَ مَا تَرَكْنَاهُ مِنَ الْأَحَادِيثِ الْوَارِدَةِ فِي ذَلِكَ لِحَالِ الطُّولِ . كُلُّهُ دَاخِلٌ فِي قَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿فِي بُيُوتٍ أَذِنَ اللَّهُ أَنْ تُرْفَعَ﴾ .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَيُذْكَرَ فِيهَا اسْمُهُ﴾ أي: اسم الله، كقوله: ﴿يَا بَنِي آدَمَ خُذُوا زِينَتَكُمْ عِنْدَ كُلِّ مَسْجِدٍ﴾ [الْأَعْرَافِ: ٣١] ، وَقَوْلُهُ ﴿وَأَقِيمُوا وُجُوهَكُمْ عِنْدَ كُلِّ مَسْجِدٍ وَادْعُوهُ مُخْلِصِينَ لَهُ الدِّينَ﴾ [الْأَعْرَافِ: ٢٩] ، وَقَوْلُهُ ﴿وَأَنَّ الْمَسَاجِدَ لِلَّهِ فَلا تَدْعُوا مَعَ اللَّهِ أَحَدًا﴾ [الْجِنِّ: ١٨] .

قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: ﴿وَيُذْكَرَ فِيهَا اسْمُهُ﴾ يَعْنِي: يُتْلَى فِيهَا كِتَابُهُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿يُسَبِّحُ لَهُ فِيهَا بِالْغُدُوِّ وَالآصَالِ﴾ أَيْ: فِي البُكَرات والعَشِيَّات. وَالْآصَالُ: جمع أصيل، وَهُوَ آخِرُ النَّهَارِ.

وَقَالَ سَعِيدُ بْنُ جُبَير، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: كُلُّ تَسْبِيحٍ فِي الْقُرْآنِ هُوَ الصَّلَاةُ.

وَقَالَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: يَعْنِي بِالْغُدُوِّ: صَلَاةَ الْغَدَاةِ، وَيَعْنِي بِالْآصَالِ: صَلَاةَ الْعَصْرِ، وَهُمَا أَوَّلُ مَا افْتَرَضَ اللَّهُ مِنَ الصَّلَاةِ، فَأَحَبَّ أَنْ يَذْكُرهما وَأَنْ يُذَكِّر بِهِمَا عِبَادَهُ.

وَكَذَا قَالَ الْحَسَنُ، وَالضَّحَّاكُ: ﴿يُسَبِّحُ لَهُ فِيهَا بِالْغُدُوِّ وَالآصَالِ﴾ يَعْنِي: الصَّلَاةَ.

وَمَنْ قَرَأَ مِنَ القَرَأَة " يُسَبَّحُ لَهُ فِيهَا بِالْغُدُوِّ وَالآصَالِ" -بِفَتْحِ الْبَاءِ مِنْ "يُسبح" عَلَى أَنَّهُ مَبْنِيٌّ لِمَا لَمْ يُسَمَّ فَاعِلُهُ -وَقَفَ عَلَى قَوْلِهِ: ﴿والآصَال﴾ وَقَفًا تامًا، وَابْتَدَأَ بِقَوْلِهِ: ﴿رِجَالٌ لَا تُلْهِيهِمْ تِجَارَةٌ وَلا بَيْعٌ عَنْ ذِكْرِ اللَّهِ﴾ وَكَأَنَّهُ مُفَسِّرٌ لِلْفَاعِلِ الْمَحْذُوفِ، كَمَا قَالَ الشَّاعِرُ .

لِيُبْكَ يزيدُ، ضارعٌ لخُصُومة ... ومُخْتَبطٌ مِمَّا تُطيح الطّوَائحُ ...

كَأَنَّهُ قَالَ: مَنْ يَبْكِيهِ؟ قَالَ: هَذَا يَبْكِيهِ. وَكَأَنَّهُ قِيلَ: مَنْ يُسَبِّحُ لَهُ فِيهَا؟ قَالَ: رِجَالٌ.

وَأَمَّا عَلَى قِرَاءَةِ مَنْ قَرَأَ: ﴿يسبِّح﴾ -بِكَسْرِ الْبَاءِ -فَجَعَلَهُ فِعْلًا وَفَاعِلَهُ: ﴿رِجَال﴾ فَلَا يَحْسُنُ الْوَقْفُ إِلَّا عَلَى الْفَاعِلِ؛ لِأَنَّهُ تَمَامُ الْكَلَامِ.

فَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿رِجَال﴾ فِيهِ إِشْعَارٌ بِهِمَمِهِمُ السَّامِيَةِ، وَنِيَّاتِهِمْ وَعَزَائِمِهِمُ الْعَالِيَةِ، الَّتِي بِهَا صَارُوا عُمَّارا لِلْمَسَاجِدِ، الَّتِي هِيَ بُيُوتُ اللَّهِ فِي أَرْضِهِ، وَمَوَاطِنُ عِبَادَتِهِ وَشُكْرِهِ، وَتَوْحِيدِهِ وَتَنْزِيهِهِ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿مِنَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ رِجَالٌ صَدَقُوا مَا عَاهَدُوا اللَّهَ عَلَيْهِ﴾ [الْأَحْزَابِ: ٢٣] .

فَأَمَّا النِّسَاءُ فَصَلاتهن فِي بُيُوتِهِنَّ أَفْضَلُ لَهُنَّ؛ لِمَا رَوَاهُ أَبُو دَاوُدَ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ مَسْعُودٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ قَالَ: "صَلَاةُ الْمَرْأَةِ فِي بَيْتِهَا أَفْضَلُ مِنْ صَلَاتِهَا فِي حُجْرَتِهَا، وَصَلَاتُهَا فِي مَخْدَعِهَا أَفْضَلُ مِنْ صَلَاتِهَا فِي بَيْتِهَا" .

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا يَحْيَى بْنُ غَيْلان، حَدَّثَنَا رِشْدِين، حَدَّثَنِي عَمْرٌو، عَنْ أَبِي السَّمْحِ، عَنِ السَّائِبِ مَوْلَى أُمِّ سَلَمَةَ عَنْ أُمِّ سَلَمَةَ -رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهَا، -عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: "خَيْرُ مَسَاجِدِ النِّسَاءِ [قَعْرُ] بُيُوتِهِنَّ" .

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ أَيْضًا: حَدَّثَنَا هَارُونُ، أَخْبَرَنِي عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ وَهْبٍ، حَدَّثَنَا دَاوُدُ بْنُ قَيْسٍ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ سُوَيد الْأَنْصَارِيِّ، عَنْ عَمَّتِهِ أُمِّ حُمَيْدٍ -امْرَأَةِ أَبِي حُمَيْدٍ السَّاعِدِيِّ -أَنَّهَا جَاءَتِ النَّبِيَّ ﷺ فَقَالَتْ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، إِنِّي أُحِبُّ الصَّلَاةَ مَعَكَ قَالَ: "قَدْ عَلِمْتُ أَنَّكِ تُحِبِّينَ الصَّلَاةَ مَعِي، وَصَلَاتُكِ فِي بَيْتِكِ خَيْرٌ مِنْ صَلَاتِكِ فِي حُجْرَتِكِ، وَصَلَاتُكِ فِي حُجْرَتك خَيْرٌ مِنْ صَلَاتِكِ فِي دَارِكِ، وَصَلَاتُكِ فِي دَارِكِ خَيْرٌ مِنْ صَلَاتِكِ فِي مَسْجِدِ قَوْمِكِ، وَصَلَاتُكِ فِي مَسْجِدِ قَوْمِكِ خَيْرٌ مِنْ صَلَاتِكِ فِي مَسْجِدِي". قَالَ: فأمَرَت فبُني لَهَا مَسْجِدٌ فِي أَقْصَى بَيْتٍ مِنْ بُيُوتِهَا وَأَظْلَمِهِ ، فَكَانَتْ تُصْلِي فِيهِ حَتَّى لقيت الله، عز وجل. لم يخرجوه. هَذَا وَيَجُوزُ لَهَا شُهُودُ جَمَاعَةِ الرِّجَالِ، بِشَرْطِ أَنْ لَا تُؤْذِيَ أَحَدًا مِنَ الرِّجَالِ بِظُهُورِ زِينَةٍ وَلَا رِيحِ طِيبٍ كَمَا ثَبَتَ فِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عُمَر أَنَّهُ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "لَا تَمْنَعُوا إِمَاءَ اللَّهِ مَسَاجِدَ اللَّهِ" .

رَوَاهُ الْبُخَارِيُّ وَمُسْلِمٌ، وَلِأَحْمَدَ وَأَبِي دَاوُدَ: "وَبُيُوتُهُنَّ خَيْرٌ لَهُنَّ" وَفِي رِوَايَةٍ: "وَلِيَخْرُجْنَ وَهُنَّ تَفِلات" أَيْ: لَا رِيحَ لَهُنَّ.

وَقَدْ ثَبَتَ فِي صَحِيحِ مُسْلِمٍ، عَنْ زَيْنَبَ -امْرَأَةِ ابْنِ مَسْعُودٍ -قَالَتْ: قَالَ لَنَا رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "إِذَا شَهِدَتْ إِحْدَاكُنَّ الْمَسْجِدَ فَلَا تَمَسَّ طِيبًا" .

وَفِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ عَنْ عَائِشَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهَا، أَنَّهَا قَالَتْ: كَانَ نِسَاءُ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ يَشْهَدْنَ الْفَجْرَ مَعَ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ، ثُمَّ يَرْجِعْنَ مُتَلَفِّعَاتٍ بمُرُوطهن، مَا يُعْرَفْن مِنَ الغَلَس .

وَفِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ أَيْضًا عَنْهَا أَنَّهَا قَالَتْ: لَوْ أَدْرَكَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ مَا أَحْدَثَ النِّسَاءُ لمنعهُنّ الْمَسَاجِدَ، كَمَا مُنعت نِسَاءُ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿رِجَالٌ لَا تُلْهِيهِمْ تِجَارَةٌ وَلا بَيْعٌ عَنْ ذِكْرِ اللَّهِ﴾ ، كَقَوْلِهِ ﴿يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا لَا تُلْهِكُمْ أَمْوَالُكُمْ وَلا أَوْلادُكُمْ عَنْ ذِكْرِ اللَّهِ وَمَنْ يَفْعَلْ ذَلِكَ فَأُولَئِكَ هُمُ الْخَاسِرُونَ﴾ [الْمُنَافِقُونَ: ٩] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى ﴿يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا إِذَا نُودِيَ لِلصَّلاةِ مِنْ يَوْمِ الْجُمُعَةِ فَاسْعَوْا إِلَى ذِكْرِ اللَّهِ وَذَرُوا الْبَيْعَ ذَلِكُمْ خَيْرٌ لَكُمْ إِنْ كُنْتُمْ تَعْلَمُونَ﴾ [الْجُمُعَةِ: ٩]

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى: لَا تَشْغَلُهُمُ الدُّنْيَا وَزُخْرُفُهَا وَزِينَتُهَا ومَلاذ بَيعها وَرِيحُهَا، عَنْ ذِكْرِ رَبِّهِمُ الَّذِي هُوَ خَالِقُهُمْ وَرَازِقُهُمْ، وَالَّذِينَ يَعْلَمُونَ أَنَّ الَّذِي عِنْدَهُ هُوَ خَيْرٌ لَهُمْ وَأَنْفَعُ مِمَّا بِأَيْدِيهِمْ؛ لِأَنَّ مَا عِنْدَهُمْ يَنْفَدُ وَمَا عِنْدَ اللَّهِ بَاقٍ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿لَا تُلْهِيهِمْ تِجَارَةٌ وَلا بَيْعٌ عَنْ ذِكْرِ اللَّهِ وَإِقَامِ الصَّلاةِ وَإِيتَاءِ الزَّكَاةِ﴾ أَيْ: يُقَدِّمُونَ طَاعَتَهُ ومُرَاده وَمَحَبَّتَهُ عَلَى مُرَادِهِمْ وَمَحَبَّتِهِمْ.

قَالَ هُشَيْم: عَنْ سَيَّار : [قَالَ] حُدِّثت عَنِ ابْنِ مَسْعُودٍ أَنَّهُ رَأَى قَوْمًا مِنْ أَهْلِ السُّوقِ، حَيْثُ نُودِيَ بِالصَّلَاةِ، تَرَكُوا بِيَاعَاتِهِمْ وَنَهَضُوا إِلَى الصَّلَاةِ، فَقَالَ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ: هَؤُلَاءِ مِنَ الَّذِينَ ذَكَرَ اللَّهُ فِي كِتَابِهِ: ﴿رِجَالٌ لَا تُلْهِيهِمْ تِجَارَةٌ وَلا بَيْعٌ عَنْ ذِكْرِ اللَّهِ﴾ .

وَهَكَذَا رَوَى عَمْرو بْنُ دِينَارٍ القَهْرَمَانيّ، عَنْ سَالِمٍ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عُمَرَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمَا، أَنَّهُ كَانَ فِي السُّوقِ فَأُقِيمَتِ الصَّلَاةُ، فَأَغْلَقُوا حَوَانِيتَهُمْ وَدَخَلُوا الْمَسْجِدَ، فَقَالَ ابْنُ عمر: فيهم نَزَلَتْ: ﴿رِجَالٌ لَا تُلْهِيهِمْ تِجَارَةٌ وَلا بَيْعٌ عَنْ ذِكْرِ اللَّهِ﴾ . رَوَاهُ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ، وَابْنُ جَرِيرٍ .

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ بَكْرٍ الصَّنْعَانِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو سَعِيدٍ مَوْلَى بَنِي هَاشِمٍ حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ بُجَيْر، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو عَبْدِ رَبٍّ قَالَ: قَالَ أَبُو الدَّرْدَاءِ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ: إِنِّي قُمْتُ عَلَى هَذَا الدَّرَجِ أُبَايِعُ عَلَيْهِ، أَرْبَحُ كُلَّ يَوْمٍ ثَلَاثَمِائَةِ دِينَارٍ، أَشْهَدُ الصَّلَاةَ فِي كُلِّ يَوْمٍ فِي الْمَسْجِدِ، أَمَا إِنِّي لَا أَقُولُ: "إِنَّ ذَلِكَ لَيْسَ بِحَلَالٍ" وَلَكِنِّي أُحِبُّ أَنْ أَكُونَ مِنَ الَّذِينَ قَالَ اللَّهُ: ﴿رِجَالٌ لَا تُلْهِيهِمْ تِجَارَةٌ وَلا بَيْعٌ عَنْ ذِكْرِ اللَّهِ﴾ .

وَقَالَ عَمْرُو بْنُ دِينَارٍ الْأَعْوَرُ: كُنْتُ مَعَ سَالِمِ بْنِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ وَنَحْنُ نُرِيدُ الْمَسْجِدَ، فَمَرَرْنَا بِسُوقِ الْمَدِينَةِ وَقَدْ قَامُوا إِلَى الصَّلَاةِ وخَمَّروُا مَتَاعَهُمْ، فَنَظَرَ سَالِمٌ إِلَى أَمْتِعَتِهِمْ لَيْسَ مَعَهَا أَحَدٌ، فَتَلَا سَالِمٌ هَذِهِ الْآيَةَ: ﴿رِجَالٌ لَا تُلْهِيهِمْ تِجَارَةٌ وَلا بَيْعٌ عَنْ ذِكْرِ اللَّهِ﴾ ثُمَّ قَالَ: هُمْ هَؤُلَاءِ.
